śrī gaṇādhipataye namaḥ atha śrī garuḍa mahā purāṇam prārabhyate tatra ādau karmakāṇḍa ākhyaḥ pūrva khaṇḍaḥ prārabhyate om nārāyaṇam namaskṛtya naram ca eva narottamam om ajam ajaram anantam jñāna rūpam mahāntam śivam amalam anādim bhūta deha ādi hīnam namasyāmi harim rudram brahmāṇam ca gaṇādhipam devīm sarasvatīm ca eva manaḥ vāc karmabhiḥ sadā sūtam paurāṇikam śāntam sarva śāstra viśāradam viṣṇu bhaktam mahātmānam naimiśa araṇyam āgatam tīrtha yātrā prasaṅgena upaviṣṭam śubha āsane śaunaka ādyāḥ mahābhāgāḥ naimiṣīyāḥ tapodhanāḥ munayaḥ ravi saṅkāśāḥ śāntāḥ yajña parāyaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ sūta jānāsi sarvam tvam pṛcchāmaḥ tvām atas vayam devatānām hi kaḥ devaḥ īśvaraḥ pūjyaḥ eva kaḥ kasmāt pravartate dharmaḥ duṣṭa hantā ca kaḥ smṛtaḥ avatārāḥ ca ke tasya katham vaṃśa ādi sambhavaḥ varṇa āśrama ādi dharmāṇām kaḥ pātā kaḥ pravartakaḥ nārāyaṇa kathāḥ sarvāḥ kathaya asmākam uttamāḥ sūtaḥ uvāca purāṇam gāruḍam vakṣye sāram viṣṇu kathā śrayam garuḍa uktam kaśyapāya purā vyāsāt śrutam mayā ekaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ devānām īśvara īśvaraḥ jagataḥ rakṣaṇa arthāya vāsudevaḥ ajaraḥ amaraḥ sa kumāra ādi rūpeṇa avatārān karoti ajaḥ hariḥ sa prathamam devaḥ kaumāram sargam āsthitaḥ dvitīyam tu bhavāya asya rasātala gatām mahīm uddhariṣyan upādatte yajñeśaḥ saukaram vapuḥ tṛtīyam ṛṣi sargam tu devarṣi tvam upetya saḥ tantram sātvatam ācaṣṭe naiṣkarmyam karmaṇām yatas naranārāyaṇaḥ bhūtvā turye tepe tapaḥ hariḥ dharmasam rakṣaṇa arthāya pūjitaḥ sa sura asuraiḥ pañcamaḥ kapilaḥ nāma siddha īśaḥ kāla viplutam provāca sūraye sāṅkhyam nirṇayam ṣaṣṭham atreḥ apatya tvam dattaḥ prāptaḥ anasūyayā ānvīkṣikīm alarkāya prahlāda ādibhyaḥ ūcivān tatas sapta ākūtyām ruceḥ yajñaḥ abhyajāyata sutrāma ādyaiḥ sura gaṇaiḥ yaṣṭvā svāyambhuva antare aṣṭame merudevyām tu nābheḥ jātaḥ uru kramaḥ darśayan vartma nārīṇām sarva āśrama namaskṛtam ṛṣibhiḥ yācitaḥ bheje navamam pārthivam vapuḥ dugdhaiḥ mahauṣadhaiḥ viprāḥ tena saṃjīvitāḥ prajāḥ rūpam sa jagṛhe mātsyam cākṣuṣa antara saṃplave naau āropya mahīmayyām apāt vaivasvatam manum sura asurāṇām udadhim mathnatām mandara acalam dadhre kamaṭha rūpeṇa pṛṣṭhe ekādaśe vibhuḥ dhānvantaram dvādaśamam trayodaśamam eva ca āpyāyat surān anyān mohinyā mohayan striyā pañcadaśam vāmanakaḥ bhūtvā agāt adhvaram baleḥ pāda trayam yācamānaḥ pratyāditsuḥ triviṣṭapam avatāre ṣoḍaśame paśyan brahma druhaḥ nṛpān tris sapta kṛtvas kupitaḥ niḥ kṣattrām akarot mahīm tatas saptadaśe jātaḥ satyavatyām parāśarāt cakre veda taroḥ śākhām dṛṣṭvā puṃsaḥ alpamedhasaḥ naradeva tvam āpannaḥ sura kārya cikīrṣayā samudra nigraha ādīni cakre kāryāṇi atas param ekonaviṃśe viṃśatime vṛṣṇiṣu prāpya janmanī rāma kṛṣṇau iti bhuvaḥ bhagavān aharat bharam buddhaḥ nāmrā jinasutaḥ kīkaṭeṣu bhaviṣyati atha saḥ aṣṭama sandhyāyām naṣṭa prāyeṣu bhavitā viṣṇuyaśasaḥ nāmnā kalkī jagatpatiḥ avatārāḥ hi asaṃkhyeyāḥ hareḥ sattva nidheḥ dvijāḥ manu veda vidaḥ hi ādyāḥ sarve viṣṇu kalāḥ smṛtāḥ tasmāt sarga ādayaḥ jātāḥ saṃpūjyāḥ ca vrata ādinā purāṇam gāruḍam vyāsaḥ purā asau me abravīt idam iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye karmakāṇḍe etatpurāṇapravṛttihetunirūpaṇam nāma prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ katham vyāsena kathitam purāṇam gāruḍam tava etat sarvam samākhyāhi param viṣṇu kathā āśrayam sūtaḥ uvāca aham hi munibhiḥ sārdham gataḥ badarikāśramam tatra dṛṣṭaḥ mayā vyāsaḥ dhyāyamānaḥ para īśvaram tam praṇamya upaviṣṭaḥ aham pṛṣṭavān hi muni īśvaram sūtaḥ uvāca vyāsa brūhi hareḥ rūpam jagat sarga ādikam tatas manye dhyāyasi tam yasmāt tasmāt jānāsi tam vibhum evam pṛṣṭaḥ yathā prāha tathā viprāḥ nibodhata vyāsaḥ uvāca śṛṇu sūta pravakṣyāmi purāṇam gāruḍam tava saha nārada dakṣa ādyaiḥ brahmā mām uktavān yathā sūtaḥ uvāca brahmā śrī gāruḍam puṇyam purāṇam sāra vācakam vyāsaḥ uvāca aham hi nāradaḥ dakṣaḥ bhṛgu ādyāḥ praṇipatya tam sāram brūhi iti papracchuḥ brahmāṇam brahma loka gam purāṇam gāruḍam sāram rudram ca mām yathā suraiḥ saha abravīt viṣṇuḥ tathā aham vyāsa vacmi te vyāsaḥ uvāca katham rudram suraiḥ sārdham abravīt vai hariḥ purā purāṇam gāruḍam sāram brūhi brahman mahā arthakam tatra dṛṣṭaḥ mayā rudraḥ dhyāyamānaḥ param padam pṛṣṭaḥ namaskṛtaḥ kim tvam devam dhyāyasi śaṅkara tvattaḥ nā anyam param devam jānāmi brūhi mām tatas sārāt sārataram tattvam śrotu kāmaḥ suraiḥ saha aham dhyāyāmi tam viṣṇum paramātmānam īśvaram bhasma uddhūlita dehaḥ tu jaṭā maṇḍala maṇḍitaḥ viṣṇoḥ ārādhana artham me vrata caryā pitāmaha tam eva gatvā pṛcchāmaḥ sāram yam cintayāmi aham viṣṇum jiṣṇum padmanābham harim deha vivarjitam śucim śuciṣadam haṃsam tad padam parameśvaram yuktā sarva ātmanā ātmānam tam devam cintayāmi aham yasmin viśvāni bhūtāni tiṣṭhanti ca viśanti ca guṇa bhūtāni bhūteśe sūtre maṇi gaṇāḥ iva sahasra akṣam sahasra aṅghrim sahasra ūrum vara ānanam aṇīyasām aṇīyāṃsam sthaviṣṭham ca sthavīyasām garīyasām gariṣṭham ca śreṣṭham ca śreyasām api yam vākyeṣu anuvākyeṣu ca gṛṇanti satya karmāṇam satyam satyeṣu sāmasu purāṇa puruṣaḥ proktaḥ brahmā proktaḥ dvijātiṣu kṣaye saṅkarṣaṇaḥ proktaḥ tam upāsyam upāsmahe yasmin lokāḥ sphuranti ime jale śakunayaḥ yathā arcayanti ca yam devāḥ yakṣa rākṣasa pannagāḥ yasya agniḥ āsyam dyauḥ mūrdhā kham nābhiḥ caraṇau kṣitiḥ yasya trilokī jaṭhare kāṣṭhāḥ ca bāhavaḥ yasya keśeṣu jīmūtāḥ nadyaḥ sarva aṅga sandhiṣu kukṣau samudrāḥ catvāraḥ tam devam cintayāmi aham paraḥ kālāt paraḥ yajñāt paraḥ sat asataḥ cayaḥ anādiḥ ādiḥ viśvasya tam devam cintayāmi aham manasaḥ candramāḥ yasya cakṣuṣoḥ ca divākaraḥ mukhāt agniḥ ca saṃjajñe tam devam cintayāmi aham padībhām yasya kṣitiḥ jātā śrotrābhyām ca tathā diśaḥ mūrdha bhāgāt divam yasya tam devam cintayāmi aham sargaḥ ca pratisargaḥ ca vaṃśaḥ manvantarāṇi ca vaṃśānucaritam yasmāt tam devam cintayāmi aham yam dhyāyāmi aham etasmāt ūjāmaḥ sāram īkṣitum iti uktaḥ aham purā rudraḥ śvetadvīpa nivāsinam stutvā praṇamya tam viṣṇum śrotu kāma sthitaḥ suraiḥ sārān sārataram viṣṇum pṛṣṭavān tam praṇamya vai yathā papraccha mām vyāsaḥ stathā asau bhagavān bhavaḥ papraccha viṣṇum deva ādyaiḥ śṛṇvatām amaraiḥ saha kaiḥ dharmaiḥ kaiḥ ca niyamaiḥ kayā vā dharma pūjayā kena ācāreṇa tuṣṭaḥ syāt kim tad rūpam ca tasya vai kasmāt devāt jagat jātam jagat pālayate cakaḥ kīdṛśaiḥ avatāraiḥ ca kasmin yāti layam jagat sargaḥ ca pratisargaḥ ca vaṃśaḥ manvantarāṇi ca parameśvara māhātmyam yukta yoga ādikam tathā tathā aṣṭādaśa vidyāḥ ca hariḥ rudram tatas abravīt śṛṇu rudra pravakṣyāmi brahmaṇā ca suraiḥ saha aham hi devaḥ devānām sarva loka īśvara īśvaraḥ aham dhyeyaḥ ca pūjyaḥ ca stutyaḥ uham statibhiḥ suraiḥ niyamaiḥ ca vrataiḥ tuṣṭaḥ ācāreṇa ca mānavaiḥ avatāraiḥ ca matsya ādyaiḥ pālayāmi akhilam jagat aham mantrāḥ ca mantra arthaḥ pūjā dhyāna paraḥ hi aham svarga ādīnām ca kartāham svarga ādīni aham eva ca yogī yogaḥ uham eva ādyaḥ purāṇāni aham eva ca jñātā śrotā tathā mantā vaktā vaktavyam eva ca dhyānam pūjā upahāraḥ aham maṇḍalāni aham eva ca itihāsāni aham rudra sarva vedāḥ hi aham śiva sarva jñānāni aham śambho brahma ātmā aham aham śiva aham sākṣāt sat ācāraḥ dharmaḥ aham vaiṣṇavaḥ hi aham varṇa āśramāḥ tathā ca aham tad dharmaḥ aham purātanaḥ aham sūryaḥ tathā candraḥ maṅgala ādīni aham tathā purā mām garuḍaḥ pakṣī tapasā ārādhayat bhuvi tuṣṭaḥ ūce varam brūhi mattaḥ vavre varam sa tu garuḍaḥ uvāca mama mātā ca vinatā nāgaiḥ dāsīkṛtā hare yathā aham deva tān jitvā ca amṛtam hi ānayāmi tat dāsyāt vimokṣayiṣyāmi yathā aham vāhanaḥ tava mahā balaḥ mahā vīryaḥ sarvajñaḥ nāga dāraṇaḥ purāṇa saṃhitā kartā yathā aham syām tathā kurum viṣṇuḥ uvāca nāga dāsyāt mātaram tvam vinatām mokṣayiṣyasi deva ādīn sakalān jitvā ca amṛtam hi ānayiṣyasi mahā balaḥ vāhanaḥ tvam bhaviṣyasi viṣa ardanaḥ purāṇam mad prasādāt ca mama māhātmya vācakam gāruḍam tava nāmnā tat loke khyātim gamiṣyati yathā aham deva devānām śrīḥ khyātaḥ vinatā suta tathā khyātim purāṇeṣu gāruḍam gāruḍa eṣyati yathā aham kīrtanīyaḥ atha tathā tvam garuḍa ātmanā mām dhyātvā pakṣi mukhya idam purāṇam gada gāruḍam kaśyapaḥ gāruḍam śrutvā vṛkṣam dagdham ajīvayat svayam ca anya manāḥ bhūtvā jīvayat yakṣi om uṃ svāhā jāpī gāruḍī parā garuḍa uktam gāruḍam hi śṛṇu rudra mad ātmakam iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇotpattinirūpaṇam nāma dvitīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca iti rudra abjajaḥ viṣṇoḥ śuśrāva brahmaṇaḥ muniḥ vyāsaḥ vyāsāt aham vakṣyā iham te śaunaka naimiṣe munīnām śṛṇvatām madhye sarga ādyam deva pūjanam varṇa āśrama ādi dharmāḥ ca dāna rāja ādi dharmakāḥ vyavahāraḥ vratam vaṃśāḥ vaidyakam sa nidānakam aṅgāni pralayaḥ dharma kāma artha jñānam uttamam sa prapañcam niṣprapañcam kṛtam viṣṇoḥ nigadyate purāṇe gāruḍe sarvam garuḍaḥ bhagavān atha vāsudeva prasādena sāmarthya atiśayaiḥ yutaḥ bhutvā hareḥ vāhanam ca sarga ādīnām ca kāraṇam devān vijitya garuḍaḥ hi amṛtā haraṇam tathā cakre kṣudhā hṛtam yasya brahmāṇḍam udare hareḥ yam dṛṣṭvā smṛta mātreṇa nāgāndīnām ca saṃkṣayaḥ kaśyapaḥ gāruḍāt vṛkṣam dagdham ca ajīvayat yatas garuḍaḥ sa hariḥ tena proktam śrī kaśyapāya ca tat śrīmat rāruḍam puṇyam sarva dam paṭhataḥ tava vakṣye vyāsam namaskṛtya śṛṇu śaunaka tat yathā iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe viṣayanirūpaṇam nāma tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sargaḥ ca pratisargaḥ ca vaṃśaḥ manvantarāṇi ca vaṃśānucaritam ca eva etat brūhi janārdana śṛṇu rudra pravakṣyāmi sarga ādīn pāpa nāśanām sarga sthiti laya antām tām viṣṇoḥ krīḍām purātanīm naranārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ vāsudevaḥ nirañjanaḥ tathā puruṣa rūpeṇa kāla rūpeṇa ca sthitam vyaktam viṣṇuḥ tathā avyaktam puruṣaḥ kālaḥ eva ca krīḍataḥ bālakasya iva ceṣṭāḥ tasya niśāmaya an ādi nidhanaḥ dhātā tu anantaḥ puruṣottamaḥ tasmāt bhavati ca avyaktam tasmāt ātmā api jāyate śarīra grahaṇam pūrvam sṛṣṭi artham kurute prabhuḥ brahmā catur mukhaḥ bhūtvā rajaḥ mātra adhikaḥ sadā śarīra grahaṇam kṛtvā sṛjat etat carācaram aṇḍasya antar jagat sarvam sa deva asura mānuṣam sraṣṭā sṛjati ca ātmānam viṣṇuḥ pālyam ca pāti ca brahmā bhūtvā sṛjat viṣṇuḥ jagat pāti hariḥ svayam brahmā tu sṛṣṭi kāle asmin ja madhya gatām mahīm daṃṣṭūya uddharati jñātvā vāra hīm āsthitaḥ tanūm deva ādi sargān vakṣye aham saṃkṣepāt śṛṇu śaṅkara nanmātrāṇām dvitīyaḥ tu bhūta sargaḥ hi sa smṛtaḥ iti eṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ sambhūtaḥ buddhi pūrvakaḥ mukhya sargaḥ caturthaḥ tu mukhyāḥ vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ tat ūrdhvastotasām ṣaṣṭhaḥ deva sargaḥ tu sa smṛtaḥ tatas avāksrotasām sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mā aṣṭamaḥ anugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttvikaḥ tāmasaḥ tu saḥ pañca ete vaikṛtāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtāḥ tu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ prākṛtaḥ vaikṛtaḥ ca api kaumāraḥ navamaḥ smṛtaḥ sthāvara antāḥ sura ādyāḥ tu prajāḥ rudra caturvidhāḥ brahmaṇaḥ kurvataḥ sṛṣṭim jajñire mānasāḥ sutāḥ tatas deva asura pitṝn mānuṣān ca catuṣṭayam sisṛkṣuḥ ambhāṃsi etāni svam ātmānam ayūyujat sisṛkṣeḥ jaghanāt pūrvam asurāḥ jajñire tatas utsasarja tatas tām tu tamaḥ mātra ātmikām tanūm tamaḥ mātrā tanuḥ tyaktā śaṅkara abhūt vibhāvarī yakṣa upakṣāṃsi tad dehe prītim āpuḥ tatas surāḥ tatas hi balinaḥ rātrau asurāḥ devatāḥ divā sā ca utsṛṣṭā abhavat sandhyā dina nakta antara sthitiḥ rajaḥ mātrām tanum gṛhya manuṣyāḥ tu abhavan tatas sā tyaktā ca abhavat jyotsnā prāc sandhyā yā abhidhīyate jyotsnā rātri ahanī sandhyā śarīrāṇi tu tasya vai rajaḥ mātrām tanu gṛhya kṣudh abhūt kopaḥ eva ca kṣudh tṛṣ kṣāmāḥ a mṛgbhakṣāḥ rākṣasāḥ rakṣaṇāt ca ye yakṣa ākhyāḥ jakṣaṇāt jñeyāḥ sarpāḥ vai keśa sarpaṇāt jātāḥ kopena bhūtāḥ te gandharvāḥ jajñire tatas gāyantaḥ jajñire vācam gandharva apsarasaḥ ca ye svargam dyauḥ vakṣasaḥ cakre sukhataḥ sa sṛṣṭavān udarāt rāj ca pārśvābhyām ca prajāpatiḥ ca eva antya mātaṅgān mahiṣa uṣṭra avikān tathā gauḥ ajaḥ puruṣaḥ medhyaḥ hi aśva aśvatara gardabhāḥ etān grāmyān paśūn prāhuḥ āraṇyān ca nibodha me śvāpadam dvi khuram hasti vānarāḥ pakṣi pañcamāḥ audakāḥ paśavaḥ ṣaṣṭhāḥ saptamāḥ ca sarīsṛpāḥ pūrva ādibhyaḥ mukhebhyaḥ tu ṛgveda ādyāḥ prajajñire āsyāt vai brāhmaṇāḥ jātāḥ bāhubhyām kṣattriyāḥ smṛtāḥ ūrubhyām tu viśaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ śūdraḥ padibhāma jāyata brahma lokaḥ brāhmaṇānām śākraḥ kṣattriya janmanām mārutam ca viśām sthānam gāndharvam śūdra janmanām prājāpatyam gṛhasthānām yathā vihita kāriṇām sthānam sapta ṛṣīṇām ca tathā eva vanavāsinām yatīnām akṣayam sthānam yadṛcchā gāminām sadā iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe sṛṣṭivarṇanam nāma caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam kṛtvā iha amutra saṃsthānam prajā sargam tu mānasam atha amṛjat prajā kartṝn bhānasān tanayān prabhuḥ bhṛgum sanatkumāram ca rucim śraddhām tathā eva ca vasiṣṭham nāradam ca eva pitṝn barhiṣadaḥ tathā agniṣvāttān ca kavya ādān ājyapān ca sukālinaḥ upahūtān tathā dīpyān strīn ca mūrti vivarjitān caturaḥ mūrti yuktān ca aṅguṣṭhāt dakṣam īśvaram vāmām guṣṭhāt tasya bhāryām asṛjat padmasambhavaḥ tasyām tu janayāmāsa dakṣaḥ duhitaraḥ śubhāḥ rudra putrāḥ babhūvurhi asaṃkhyātāḥ mahā balāḥ bhṛgave ca dadau khyātim rūpeṇa apratimām śubhām bhṛgoḥ dhātāvidhātārau janayāmāsa sā śubhā śriyam ca janayāmāsa patnī nārāyaṇasya yā tasyām vai janayāmāsa bala unmādau hariḥ svayam prāṇaḥ ca eva mṛkaṇḍuḥ ca mārkaṇḍeyaḥ mṛkaṇḍutaḥ patni marīceḥ sambhūtiḥ paurṇamāsam asūyata smṛteḥ ca aṃṅgirasaḥ putrāḥ prasūtāḥ kanyakāḥ tathā sinīvālī kuhūḥ ca eva rākā ca anumatiḥ tathā anasūyā tathā eva atreḥ jajñe putrān akalmaṣān prītyām pulastya bhāryāyām dattoliḥ tad sutaḥ abhavat karṃmaśaḥ ca arthavīraḥ ca sahiṣṇuḥ ca suta trayam kṣamā tu suṣuve bhāryā pulahasya prijāpateḥ kratoḥ ca sumatiḥ bhāryā bālakhilyā anasūyata ṣaṣṭiḥ yāni sahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇām ūrdharetasām aṅguṣṭha parva mātrāṇām jvalat bhāskara varcasām ūrjāyām tu vasiṣṭasya sapta ajāyanta vai sutāḥ rajogātra ūrdhabāhuḥ ca śaraṇaḥ ca anaghaḥ tathā sutapāḥ śukraḥ iti ete sarve saptarṣayaḥ amalāḥ svāhām prādāt sa dakṣaḥ api śaśarīrāya vahnaye tasmāt svāhā sutān lebhe trīn udāra ojasaḥ hara phāvakam pavamānam ca śucim ca api jala āśinaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ ca svadhā jajñe menām vaitaraṇīm tathā te ubhe brahma vādinyau menāyām tu himācalaḥ mainākam janayāmāsa gaurīm pūrvam tu yā satī tatas brahma ātma sambhūtam pūrvam svāyaṃbhuvam prabhuḥ ātmānam eva kṛtavān prajāpālyam manum hara śatarūpām ca tām nārīm tapaḥ nihata kalmaṣām tasmāt ca puruṣāt devī śatarūpā vyajāyata priyavrata uttānapādau prasūti ākūti saṃjñā ite devahūtim manuḥ tāsu ākūtim rucaye dadau prasūtim ca eva dakṣāya davahūtim ca kardame ruceḥ yajñaḥ dakṣiṇā abhūt dakṣiṇāyām ca yajñataḥ abhavan dvādaśa sutāḥ yāmāḥ nāma mahā balāḥ sṛṣṭavān dakṣaḥ uttamāḥ śraddhā calā dhṛtiḥ tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ medhā kriyā tathā buddhiḥ lajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ ṛddhiḥ kīrtiḥ tnayodaśī patnī artham pratijagrāha dharmaḥ dākṣāyaṇī prabhuḥ khyatiḥ satī atha sambhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamā tathā sannatiḥ ca anasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā marīciḥ ca tathā ca eva aṅgirāḥ muniḥ khyāti ādyāḥ jagṛhuḥ kanyāḥ munayaḥ muni sattamāḥ śraddhā kāmam calā darpam niyamam dhṛtiḥ ātmajam santoṣam ca tathā tuṣṭiḥ lobham puṣṭiḥ asūyata medhā śrutam kriyā daṇḍam layam vinayam eva ca vyavasāyam prajajñe vai kṣemam śāntiḥ asūyata tasya jāmātaraḥ sarve yajñam jagmuḥ nimantritāḥ bhāryabhiḥ sahitāḥ sarve rudram devīm satīm vinā anāhūtā satī prāptā dakṣeṇa eva avamānitā tyaktā deham punar jātā menāyām tu himālayāt śambhoḥ bhāryā bhavat raurī tasyām jajñe vināyakaḥ kumāraḥ ca eva bhṛṅgīśaḥ kruddhaḥ rudraḥ pratāpavān vidhvaṃsya yajñam dakṣam tu tam śaśāpa pinākadhṛk iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe prajākartrādisṛṣṭiḥ nāma pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam uttānapādāt abhavat surucyām uttamaḥ sutaḥ muni prasādāt ārādhya devadevam janārdanam dhruvasya tanayaḥ śliṣṭiḥ mahā bala parākramaḥ ripoḥ putraḥ tathā śrīmān cākṣuṣaḥ kīrtitaḥ manuḥ ruruḥ tasya sutaḥ śrīmān aṅgaḥ tasya api ca ātmajaḥ a dharṃma kārī munibhiḥ ca kuśaiḥ hataḥ hrasvaḥ atimātraḥ kṛṣṇa aṅgaḥ niṣīda iti tatas abruvan niṣādaḥ tena vai jātaḥ bindhya śaila nivāsakaḥ tatas asya dakṣiṇam pāṇim mamanthuḥ sahasā dvijāḥ tasmāt tasya sutaḥ jātaḥ viṣṇoḥ mānasa rūpadhṛk dudoha pṛthivīm rājā prajānām jīvanāya hi antardhānaḥ pṛthoḥ putraḥ tahavirdhānaḥ tad ātmajaḥ prācīnavahaḥ te putraḥ pṛthivyām ekarāj babhau tasmāt suṣāva sāmudrī daśa prācīnabarhiṣaḥ sarve prācetasāḥ nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi samudrasalileśayāḥ prajāpati tvam saṃprāpya bhāryā teṣām ca māriṣa abhavat hava śāpena tasyām dakṣaḥ abhavat tatas asṛjat manasā dakṣaḥ prajāḥ pūrvam catur vodhāḥ maithunena tatas sṛṣṭim kartum aicchat prajāpatiḥ asikrīm āvahat bhāryām vīraṇasya prajāpateḥ nārada uktāḥ bhuvaḥ ca antam gatāḥ jñātum ca na āgatāḥ dakṣa putra sahasram ca teṣu naṣṭeṣu sṛṣṭavān śavala aśvāḥ te api gatāḥ bhrātṝṇām padavīm hara dakṣaḥ kruddhaḥ śaśāpa atha nāradam janma ca āpsyasi yajñe dhvaste atha dakṣaḥ api śaśāpra ugram maheśvaram stutvā tvām upacāraiḥ ca pūjayiṣyanti śaṅkara asiknyām (mahiṣyām janayāmāsa dakṣaḥ duhitaraḥ hi atha ṣaṣṭim kanyāḥ rūpa yutāḥ dve ca eva aṅgirase dadau dve prādāt sa kṛśāśvāya daśa dharṃmāya ca api atha caturdaśa kaśyapāya aṣṭāviṃśā atimindave pradadau bahuputrāya suprabhām bhāminīm tathā manoramām bhānumatīm viśālām bahudām atha dakṣaḥ prādāt mahādeva catasraḥ ariṣṭanemaye sa kṛśāśvāya ca prādāt suprajām ca tathā jayām arundhatī lambā bhānuḥ marudvatī saṅkalpā ca muhūrtā ca sādhyā viśvā ca tāḥ daśa dharṃma patnyaḥ samākhyātāḥ kaśyapasya vadāmi aham aditiḥ ditiḥ danuḥ kālā hi anāyuḥ siṃhikā muniḥ kadrūḥ sādhyā harā krodhā vinatā surabhiḥ khagā viśvedevāḥ tu viśvāyāḥ sādhyā sādhyān vyajāyata bhānoḥ tu bhānavaḥ rudra muhūrtāt ca muhūrta jāḥ lambāyāḥ ca eva ghoṣaḥ atha nāgavīthiḥ tu yā pṛthivī viṣayam sarva marutvatyām vyajāyata saṅkalpāyāḥ tu sarvātmā jajñe saṃkalpaḥ eva hi āpaḥ dhruvaḥ ca somaḥ ca dharaḥ ca eva anilaḥ analaḥ pratyūṣaḥ ca prabhāsaḥ ca vasavaḥ nāmabhiḥ smṛtāḥ āpasya putraḥ vetuṇḍiḥ śramaḥ śrāntaḥ dhvaniḥ tathā manoharāyām śiśiraḥ prāṇaḥ atha ramaṇaḥ tathā anilasya śivā bhāryā tasyāḥ putraḥ pulomajaḥ tasya śākhaḥ viśākhaḥ ca naigameyaḥ ca pṛṣṭajaḥ apatyam kṛttikānām tu kārtikeyaḥ iti smṛtaḥ pratyuṣasya viduḥ putram ṛṣim nāmnā tu devalam ajaikapād ahirbudhnyaḥ tvaṣṭā rudraḥ ca vīryavān tvaṣṭuḥ ca api ātmajaḥ putraḥ viśvarūpaḥ mahā tapāḥ haraḥ ca bahurūpaḥ ca tryambakaḥ ca aparājitaḥ vṛṣākapiḥ ca śambhuḥ ca kaparde raivataḥ tathā mṛgavyādhaḥ ca śarvaḥ ca kapālī ca mahā mune ekādaśā ete kathitāḥ rudrāḥ tribhuvana īśvarāḥ adityām kaśyapāt ca eva sūryāḥ dvādaśa jajñire viṣṇuḥ dhātā tvaṣṭā pūṣā tathā eva ca aśumān ca bhagaḥ ca eva ādityāḥ dvādaśa smṛtāḥ saptaviṃśatiḥ somasya patnyaḥ nakṣatra saṃjñitāḥ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ dityām hiraṇyākṣaḥ abhavat tadā hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāḥ catvāraḥ pṛthula ojasaḥ anuhrādaḥ ca hrādaḥ ca prahrādaḥ ca eva vīryavān saṃhrādaḥ ca avamaḥ teṣām prahrādaḥ viṣṇu tatparaḥ saṃhrāda putraḥ āyuṣmān śibiḥ vāṣkalaḥ eva ca baleḥ putra śatam tu āsīt vāṇa jyeṣṭham vṛṣadhvaja hiraṇyākṣa sutāḥ ca āsan sarve eva mahā balāḥ utkuraḥ śakuniḥ ca eva bhūtasantāpanaḥ tathā mahānāgaḥ mahābāhuḥ kālanābhaḥ tathā aparaḥ abhavan danu putrāḥ ca dvimūrdhā śaṅkaraḥ tathā ayomukhaḥ śaṅkuśirāḥ kapilaḥ śambaraḥ tathā ekacakraḥ mahābāhuḥ tārakaḥ ca mahā balaḥ svarbhānuḥ vṛṣaparvā ca pulomā ca mahā asuraḥ ete danoḥ sutāḥ khyātāḥ vipracittiḥ ca vīryavān svarbhānoḥ suprabhā kanyā śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī upadānavī hayaśirāḥ prakhyātāḥ vara kanyakāḥ vaiśvānara sute ca ubhe pulomā kālakā tathā tābhyām putra sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiḥ dānava sattamāḥ paulomāḥ kālakañjāḥ ca mārīca tanayāḥ smṛtāḥ siṃhikāyām samutpannāḥ vipracitti sutāḥ tathā vyaṃśaḥ śalyaḥ ca balavān nabhaḥ ca eva mahā balaḥ vātāpiḥ namuciḥ ca eva ilvalaḥ khasṛmān tathā ṣaṭ sutāḥ ca mahā sattvāḥ tāmrāyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ śukī śyenī ca bhāsī ca sugrīvī śuci gṛdhrike śukī śukān ajanayat ulūkī pratyalūkakān śyenī śyenān tathā bhāsī bhāsān gṛdhrān ca gṛdhrī api śukī audakān pakṣi gaṇān sugrīvī tu vyajāyata gardabhān ca tāmrā vaṃśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ surasāyāḥ sahasram tu sarpāṇām amita ojasām kādraveyāḥ ca phaṇinaḥ sahasram amita ojasaḥ teṣām bhūteśa śaṅkhaḥ śvetaḥ mahāpadmaḥ kambala aśvatarau tathā elāpatraḥ tathā nāgaḥ karkoṭaka dhanañjayau gaṇam krodha vaśam viddhi te ca sarve ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ krodhā tu janayāmāsa piśācān ca mahā balān gāḥ tu vai janayāmāsa surabhiḥ mahiṣān tathā irā vṛkṣa latā ballīḥ tṛṇa jātīḥ ca sarvaśas khagā ca yakṣa rakṣāṃsi muniḥ apsarasaḥ tathā ariṣṭā tu mahā sattvān gandharvān samajījanat ekaśukraḥ dviśukraḥ ca triśukraḥ ca mahā balaḥ īdṛś sadṛś tathā anyādṛś tatas pratisadṛś tathā ṛta ca ṛta dharṃmā ca vihartā varuṇaḥ dhruvaḥ vidhāraṇaḥ ca durmedhāḥ ayam eka gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ īdṛśaḥ ca sadṛkṣaḥ ca etādṛkṣaḥ mita aśanaḥ prasadṛkṣaḥ ca surataḥ ca mahā tapāḥ hetumān prasavaḥ tadvat surabhaḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ dyutiḥ vasuḥ anādhṛṣyaḥ lābha kāmaḥ jayī virāj etat sarvam hare rūpam rājānaḥ dānavāḥ surāḥ sūrya ādi parivāreṇa manu ādyāḥ ījire harim iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe uttānapādavaṃśādivarṇanam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūrya ādi pūjanam brūhi kṛtam svāyambhuva ādibhiḥ bhukti mukti pradam sāram vyāsa saṃkṣepataḥ param sūrya ādi pūjām vakṣyāmi dharṃma kāma ādi kārikām om sūrya āsanāya namaḥ om namaḥ sūrya mūrtaye om hrāṃ hrīṃ saḥ sūryāya namaḥ om somāya namaḥ om maṅgalāya namaḥ om budhāya namaḥ om bṛhaspataye namaḥ om śukrāya namaḥ om śanaiścarāya namaḥ om rāhave namaḥ om ketave namaḥ om tejaḥ caṇḍāya namaḥ āsana āvāhanam pādyam arghyam ācamanam tathā snānam vastra upavītam ca gandha puṣpam ca dhūpakam dīpakam ca naskāram pradakṣiṇa visarjane sūrya ādīnām sadā kuryāt iti mantraiḥ vṛṣadhvaja om hrāṃśivāya namaḥ om hrāṃ śiva mūrtaye śivāya namaḥ om hrāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ om hrīṃ śirase svāhā om hrūm śikhāyai vaṣaṭ om hrai kavacāya hum om netratrayāya vauṣaṭ om hraḥ astrāya namaḥ om hrāṃ sadyojātaye namaḥ om hrīṃ vāmadevāya namaḥ om hrūm aghorāya namaḥ om tatpuruṣāya namaḥ om hrauṃ īśānāya namaḥ om hrīṃ gauryai namaḥ om hrauṃ gurubhyaḥ namaḥ om hrauṃ indrāya namaḥ om hrauṃ caṇḍāya namaḥ om hrāṃ aghorāya namaḥ om vāsudeva āsanāya namaḥ om vāsudava mūrtaye namaḥ om aṃ om namaḥ bhagavate vāsudevāya namaḥ om āṃ om namaḥ bhagavate saṅkarṣaṇāya namaḥ om nārāyaṇāya namaḥ om hrāṃ viṣṇave namaḥ om namaḥ bhagavate narasiṃhāya namaḥ om bhūḥ om namaḥ bhagavate varāhāya namaḥ om kaṃ ṭaṃ paṃ śam vainateyāya namaḥ om jaṃ khaṃ raṃ sudarśa nāya namaḥ om khaṃ ṭhaṃ phaṃ ṣaṃ gadaiyau namaḥ om vaṃ laṃ maṃ pāñcajanyāya namaḥ om ghaṃ ḍhaṃ bhaṃ haṃ śriyai namaḥ om gaṃ ḍaṃ vaṃ saṃ puṣṭyai namaḥ om dhaṃ ṣaṃ vaṃ saṃ vanamālāyai namaḥ om sam daṃ laṃ śrīvatsāya namaḥ om ṭhaṃ caṃ bhaṃ yaṃ kaustubhāya namaḥ om indra ādi dikpālebhyaḥ namaḥ om viṣvaksenāya namaḥ viṣṇu śaktyāḥ sarasvatyāḥ pūjām śṛṇu śubha pradām om hrīṃ sarasvatyai namaḥ om hrāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ om hrīṃ śirase namaḥ om hrūm śikhāyai namaḥ om hraiṃ kavacāya namaḥ om netratrayāya namaḥ om hraḥ astrāya namaḥ śraddhā ṛddhiḥ kalā medhā tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ prabhā matiḥ om hrīṅkāra ādyāḥ namaḥ antāḥ ca sarasvatyāḥ ca śaktayaḥ kṣetrapālāya namaḥ padma sthāyāḥ sarasvatyāḥ āsana ādyam prakalpayet sūrya ādīnām svakaiḥ prantraiḥ pavitra ārohaṇam tathā iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe sūrya ādīnām sarasvatyāḥ ca pūjanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam bhūmiṣṭhe maṇḍape snātvā maṇḍale viṣṇum arcayet pañca raṅgika cūrṇena vajra nābham tu maṇḍalam ṣoḍaśaiḥ koṣṭhakaiḥ tatra saṃmitam rudra kārayet caturtha pañca koṇeṣu sūtra pātam tu kārayet koṇa sūtrāt ubhayatas koṇāḥ ye tatra saṃsthitāḥ teṣu ca eva prakurvīta sūtra pātam vicakṣaṇaḥ prathamā nābhiḥ uddiṣṭā madhye rekhā prasaṃgame antareṣu ca sarveṣu aṣṭau ca eva tunābhayaḥ pūrva madhyama nābhi bhyāmatham sūtram tu bhrāmayet antarā sa dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ pāda ūnam bhrāmayet hara anena nābhi sūtrasya karṇikām bhrāmayet śiva karṇikāyāḥ dvi bhāgena kesarāṇi vicakṣaṇaḥ sarveṣu mānena anena suvrata padmāni tāni kurvīta deśikaḥ para mā artha vid ādi sūtra vibhāgena dvārāṇi parikalpayet karṇikām pīta varṇena sita rakta ādi kesaraiḥ kṛṣṇa varṇena rajasā caturaśram prapūrayet dvārāṇi śukla varṇena rekhāḥ pañca ca maṇḍale sitā raktā tathā pītā kṛṣṇā ca eva yathākramam kṛtvā eva maṇḍalam ca ādau nyāsam kṛtvā arcayet harim hṛd madhye tu nyaset viṣṇum kaṇṭhe saṅkarṣaṇam tathā brahmāṇam sarva gātreṣu karayoḥ śrīdharam tathā aham viṣṇuḥ iti dhyātvā karṇikāyām nyaset harim nyaset saṅkarṣaṇam pūrve pradyumnam ca eva dakṣiṇe śrīdharam rudra koṇeṣu indra ādīn dikṣu vinyaset iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe viṣṇupūjopayogivajranābhamaṇḍalanirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam samaye dīkṣitaḥ śiṣyaḥ baddha netraḥ tu vāsasā aṣṭa āhuti śatam tasya mūlamantreṇa homayet dviguṇam putrake homam triguṇam sādhake matam nirvāṇa deśike rudra caturguṇam udāhṛtam guru viṣṇu dvija strīṇām hantā badhyaḥ tvam a dīkṣitaiḥ atha dīkṣām pravakṣyāmi dharma adharma kṣayaṅkarīm upaveśya bahis śiṣyān dhāraṇam teṣu kārayet vāyavyā kalayā rudra śoṣyamāṇān vicintayet āgreyyāḥ dahyamānān ca plāvitān ambhasā punar tejaḥ teja asi tam jīvam ekīkṛtya samākṣipet cintayet dyomni śarīre anyat tu kāraṇam ekaikam yaḥ jayet tatra kṣetrajñam deha kāraṇāt utpādya yojayet paścāt ekaikam vṛṣabhadhvaja hastam padmam samākhyātam patrāṇi aṅgulayaḥ smṛtāḥ tam hastam pātayet mūrdhni śiṣyasya tu samāhitaḥ naśyanti sparśanāt tasya pātakāni akhilāni ca puṣpam nipatitam yatra mūrdhnaḥ devasya śārṅgiṇaḥ tad nāma kārayet tasya strīṇām nāma aṅkitam svayam śūdrāṇām dāsa saṃyuktam kārayet tu vicakṣaṇaḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam śyā ādi pūjām sthaṇḍila ādiṣu siddhaye śrīṃ hrīṃ mahālakṣmyai namaḥ śrāṃ śrīṃ śrūṃ śraiṃ śrauṃ śraḥ kramāt hṛdayam ca śiraḥ śikhām catuḥ ṣaṣṭi antam aṣṭa ādi kha akṣe kha akṣi ādi maṇḍalam kha akṣi indu sūrya gam sarvam kha ādi veda indu vartanāt lakṣmīm aṅgāni ca ekasmin koṇe durgām gaṇam gurum kṣetrapālam atha agni ādau homān juhāva kāma bhāj om ghaṃ ṭaṃ ḍaṃ haṃ śrī mahālakṣmyai namaḥ anena pūjayet lakṣmīm pūrva ukta parivārakaiḥ om hrīṃ saiṃ sarasvatyai namaḥ om om sarasvatyai namaḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe lakṣmyarcananirūpaṇam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam hariḥ uvāca navavyūha arcanam vakṣye yat uktam kaśyapāya hi jīvam utkṣipya mūrdhanyam nābhyām vyomni niveśayet dvādaśa akṣara bījena ukta bījaiḥ anantaram ṣaḍaṅgena tatas kuryāt sākṣāt yena hariḥ bhavet dakṣiṇa aṅguṣṭham ārabhya madhya aṅguṣṭhan dale nyaset hṛd śirasi bāhvoḥ ca karayoḥ jānvoḥ pādayoḥ ca api vinyaset padma ākārau karau kṛtvā madhye aṅguṣṭham niveśayet kramāt ca etāni bījāni tarjanī ādiṣu vinya set tatas mūrdha akṣi vakkreṣu kaṇṭhe ca hṛdaye tathā pāṇyoḥ ṣaḍaṅga bījāni nyasya kāye tatas nyaset aṅguṣṭha ādi kaniṣṭhā antam vinyaset vīja pañcakam hṛdaye hṛdayam nyasya śiraḥ śirasi vinyaset śikhāyām tu śikhām nyasya kavacam sarvatas tanau hṛdaye cintayet pūrvam yogapīṭham samāhitaḥ āgneya ādau ca pūrva ādau adharma ādīn ca vinyaset ebhiḥ paricchanna tanum pīṭha bhūtam tad ātmakam tatas vidyāt saraḥ jātam dala aṣṭa sama diś dalam sita abjam śata patra āḍhyam viprakīrṇa ūrdhva karṇikam dhyātvā vedādinā paścāt sūrya soma anala ātmanām tatas pūrva ādi diś saṃsthāḥ śaktīḥ keśava gocarāḥ vimalā ādyāḥ nyaset aṣṭau navamīm karṇikā gatām manasā āvāhya tatra īśam harim śārṅgam nyaset punar hṛdaya ādīni pūrva ādi catur diś dala yogataḥ saṅkarṣaṇa ādi bījāni pūrva ādi krama yogataḥ sudarśanam sahasra aram dakṣiṇe dvāri vinyaset śriyam dakṣiṇatas nyasya lakṣmīm uttaratas tathā dvāri attare gadām nyasya śaṅkham koṇeṣu vinyaset deva dakṣiṇatas śārṅgam vāme ca eva sudhīḥ nyaset sarvam dhyātvā iti saṃpūjya mudrāḥ sandarśayet tatas añjaliḥ prathamā mudrā kṣipram deva prasādhanī vandanī hṛdaya āsaktāt sārdham dakṣiṇatas unnatā vāma muṣṭiḥ dakṣiṇa aṅguṣṭha bandhanaḥ savyasya tasya ca aṅguṣṭhaḥ yaḥ saḥ prakīrtitaḥ tisraḥ sādhāraṇāḥ hi etāḥ mūrti bhedena kalpitāḥ kaniṣṭhā ādi pramokeṇa aṣṭau mudrāḥ yathākramam aṣṭānām pūrvabījānām kramaśas tu avadhārayet aṅguṣṭhena kaniṣṭhā antam nāmayitvā aṅguli trayam navamī iyam smṛtā mudrā varāha abhimatā sadā muṣṭi dvayam atho baddhā evam eva anupūrvaśas daśānām lokapālānām mudrāḥ ca krama yogataḥ suram ādyam dvitīyam ca upāntyam ca antyam eva ca praṇavaḥ tat sat iti etat hum kṣaiṃ bhūḥ iti mantrakāḥ nārāyaṇaḥ tathā brahmā viṣṇuḥ siṃhaḥ varāha rāj sita aruṇa haridrā ābhāḥ nīla śyāma lohitāḥ varṇataḥ nava nāmakāḥ kaṃ ṭaṃ paṃ śam garutmān syāt jaṃ khaṃ vaṃ ca sudarśanam proktaḥ ca anantaḥ hi aham eva ca iti aṅgāni yathāyogam devadevasya vai daśā garuḍaḥ ambuja saṃkāśaḥ gadā ca eva asita ākṛtiḥ puṣṭiḥ śirīṣa puṣpa ābhā lakṣmīḥ kāñcana sannibhā pūrṇa candra nibhaḥ śaṅkhaḥ kaustubhaḥ tu aruṇa dyutiḥ cakram sūrya sahasra ābham śrīvatsaḥ kunda sannibhaḥ vidyut rūpāṇi ca astrāṇi yāni na uktāni varṇataḥ arghya pādya ādi vai dadyāt puṇḍarīkākṣa vidyayā iti śrī gāruḍe atha ūrdham anantakaḥ ete eka ādibhiḥ cakraiḥ vijñeyāḥ lakṣitāḥ surāḥ cakra aṅkitaiḥ pūjitaḥ rakṣet sadā naraiḥ om cakrāya svāhā om vicakrāya svāhā om sucakrāya svāhā om mahācakrāya svāhā om nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam pravakṣyāmi adhunā hi etat vaiṣṇavam pañjaram śubham prācyām rakṣasva mām viṣṇo tvām aham śaraṇam gataḥ gadām kaumodakīm gṛhṇa padmanābha namaḥ asta te ādāya astra śāstra ādikam hare namaḥ te rakṣa rakṣaḥ ghna aiśānyām śaraṇam gataḥ pāñcajanyam mahā śaṅkham anughoṣyam ca paṅkajam pragṛhya rakṣa mām viṣṇo āgnyeyyām rakṣa sūkara candra sūryam samāgṛhya ca udānasya patiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ samānasya patiḥ tathā śabdasya ca patiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sparśasya patiḥ eva ca rūpāṇām ca patiḥ ca ādyaḥ khaṅga pāṇiḥ halāyudhaḥ cakrapāṇiḥ kuṇḍalī ca śrīvatsāṃkaḥ tathā eva ca prakṛtiḥ kaustubha grīvaḥ pīta ambara dharaḥ tathā sukapolaḥ vibhuḥ jiṣṇuḥ bhrājiṣṇuḥ ca aiṣudhīḥ tathā hiraṇyakaśipoḥ hantā hiraṇyākṣa vimardakaḥ nihantā pūtanāyāḥ ca bhāskara anta vināśanaḥ kaṃsa dānava bhettā ca cāṇūrasya pramardakaḥ akrūraḥ krūrarūpaḥ ca akrūrapriyavanditaḥ aham kārā upamāḥ cittam gaganam pṛthivī jalam vāyuḥ cakṣuḥ tathā śrotram jihvā ca ghrāṇam eva ca vāc pāṇi pāda javanaḥ pāyu upasthaḥ tathā eva ca śaṅkaraḥ ca eva sarvaḥ ca kṣānti daḥ kṣānti kṛt naraḥ kīrtiḥ deptiḥ kṣamā kāntiḥ bhaktaḥ ca eva dayā parā dānam dātā ca kartā ca devadeva priyaḥ śuciḥ śucimān sukha daḥ mokṣaḥ kāmaḥ ca arthaḥ sahasrapād sahasra śīrṣā vaidyaḥ ca mokṣadvāram tathā eva ca prajādvāram sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrakaraḥ eva ca śukraḥ ca sukirīṭī ca sugrīvaḥ kaustubhaḥ tathā pradyumnaḥ ca aniruddhaḥ ca hayagrīvaḥ ca sūkaraḥ śaraṇyaḥ ca eva nityaḥ ca buddhaḥ muktaḥ śarīra bhṛt khara dūṣaṇa hantā ca rāvaṇasya pramardanaḥ narāntaka antakaḥ ca eva devāntaka vināśanaḥ duṣṭa asura nihantā ca śambarāriḥ tathā eva ca narakasya nihantā ca triśīrṣasya vināśanaḥ prāṇaḥ apānaḥ tathā vyānaḥ rajaḥ sattvam tamaḥ śarad udānaḥ ca samānaḥ ca bheṣajam ca bhiṣaj tathā hasta indriya vihīnaḥ ca pādābhyām ca vivarjitaḥ pāyu upastha vihīnaḥ ca maru tāpa vivarjitaḥ ākāśena vihīnaḥ ca vāyunā parivarjitaḥ pṛthivyā ca vihīnaḥ ca śabdena ca vivarjitaḥ sūkṣmaḥ ca eva su sūkṣmaḥ ca sthūlāt sthūlataraḥ tathā viśāradaḥ bala adhyakṣaḥ sarvasya kṣobhakaḥ tathā prakṛteḥ kṣobhakaḥ ca eva mahataḥ kṣobhakaḥ tathā bhūtānām kṣobhakaḥ ca eva buddheḥ ca kṣomakaḥ tathā indriyāṇām kṣobhakaḥ ca viṣaya kṣobhakaḥ tathā tvacā na gamyaḥ kūrṃmaḥ ca jihvā grāhyaḥ tathā eva ca grāṇa indriya a gamyaḥ eva vācā a grāhyaḥ tathā eva ca aham buddhyā tathā grāhyaḥ cetasā grāhyāḥ eva ca śaṅkhapāṇiḥ ca avyayaḥ ca gadā pāṇiḥ tathā eva ca śārṅgapāṇiḥ ca kṛṣṇaḥ ca jñāna mūrtiḥ parantapaḥ tapasvī jñāna gamyaḥ hi jñānī jñāna vid eva ca jñeyaḥ ca jñeya hīnaḥ ca jñaptiḥ caitanya rūpakaḥ bhāvaḥ bhāvyaḥ bhava karaḥ bhāvanaḥ bhava nāśanaḥ upendraḥ ca nṛsiṃhaḥ ca śauriḥ ca eva janārdanaḥ āraṇeyaḥ bṛhadbhānuḥ bṛhaddīptiḥ tathā eva ca dāmodaraḥ tnikālaḥ ca kālajñaḥ kālavarjitaḥ trisandhyaḥ dvāparam tretā prajādvāram tri vikramaḥ vikramaḥ daṇḍa hastaḥ ca hi ekadaṇḍī tridaṇḍa dhṛk sāma bhedaḥ tathā upāyaḥ sāmarūpī ca sāmagaḥ sāmaveda ūḍhī atharvaḥ ca sukṛtaḥ suta rūpaṇaḥ ṛc rūpī ca eva ṛgvedaḥ ṛgvedeṣu pratiṣṭhitaḥ catuṣpād ca dvipād ca eva smṛtiḥ nyāyaḥ yamaḥ balī sannyāsī sannayāsaḥ catur āśramaḥ eva ca brahmacārī gṛhasthaḥ ca vānaprasthaḥ ca bhikṣukaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdraḥ varṇaḥ tathā eva ca śīla daḥ śīla sampannaḥ śīla parivarjitaḥ mokṣaḥ adhyātma samāviṣṭaḥ stutiḥ stotā ca pūjakaḥ karaṇam ca eva vācyam ca eva tu vācakaḥ vettā vyākaraṇam ca eva vākyam ca eva ca vākya vid vākya gamyaḥ tīrtha vāsī tīrthaḥ ca tīrtha vid tīrtha ādi bhūtaḥ sāṃkhyaḥ ca niruktam tu adhidaivatam praṇavaḥ praṇava īśaḥ ca praṇavena pravanditaḥ praṇavena ca lakṣyaḥ vai gāyatrī ca gadādharaḥ śālagrāma nivāsī ca śālagrāmaḥ tathā eva ca jalaśāyī yogaśāyī śeṣaśāyī kuśeśayaḥ mahībhartā ca kāryam ca kāraṇam pṛthivīdharaḥ prajāpatiḥ śāśvataḥ ca kāmyaḥ kāmayitā virāj samrāj pūṣā tathā svargaḥ ratha sthaḥ sārathiḥ balam dhanī dhana pradaḥ dhanyaḥ yādavānām hite rataḥ parākramaḥ durviṣahaḥ sarva śāstra viśāradaḥ sārasvataḥ mahā bhīṣmaḥ pārijāta haraḥ tathā amṛtasya pradātā ca kṣīrodaḥ kṣīram eva ca śipiviṣṭaḥ prasannaḥ ca sarva loka ārti nāśanaḥ śrotrā śrotra niyantā ca śrotavyaḥ śravaṇam tathā tvac sthitaḥ ca sparśayitvā spṛśyam ca sparśanam tathā rūpa draṣṭā ca cakṣuḥ sthaḥ niyantā cakṣuṣaḥ tathā dṛśyam ca eva tu jihvā sthaḥ rasajñaḥ ca niyāmakaḥ vāc sthaḥ vaktā ca vaktavyaḥ vacanam vāc niyāmakaḥ prāṇi sthaḥ śilpa kṛt śilpaḥ hastayoḥ ca niyāmakaḥ niyantā pādayoḥ ca eva pādya bhāj ca visarga kṛt dhūmakṛt dhūma rūpaḥ ca devakīputraḥ uttamaḥ aṭṭahāsapriyaḥ ca eva sarvādhyakṣaḥ kṣaraḥ akṣaraḥ acyutaḥ ca eva satyeśaḥ satyāyāḥ ca priyaḥ varaḥ rukmiṇyāḥ ca patiḥ ca eva rukmiṇyāḥ vallabhaḥ tathā gopīnām vallabhaḥ ca eva puṇyaślokaḥ ca viśrutaḥ grāhasya vinihantā ca grāmī rakṣakaḥ tathā viśvarūpaḥ viśālākṣaḥ daityasūdanaḥ eva ca suṣupti sthaḥ suṣuptiḥ ca sthānam sthāna antaḥ eva ca jagatsthaḥ ca eva jāgartā sthānam jāgaritam tathā vijñānam vedya rūpam ca jīvaḥ jīvayitā tathā bhuvana adhipatiḥ ca eva bhuvanānām niyāmakaḥ pātāla vāsī pātālam sarva jvara vināśanaḥ paramānanda rūpī ca dharṃmāṇām ca pravartakaḥ sulabhaḥ durlabhaḥ ca eva prāṇāyāma paraḥ tathā pratyāhāraḥ dhārakaḥ ca pratyāhāra karaḥ tathā agrāhaḥ ca eva gauraḥ ca sarvaḥ śuciḥ abhiṣṭutaḥ vaṣaṭkāraḥ vaṣaṭ vauṣaṭ svadhā svāhā ratiḥ tathā paktā nandayitā a bhoktā boddhā bhāvayitā tathā jñāna ātmā ca eva deha ātmā bhū mā sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ nadī nandī ca nandīśaḥ bhārataḥ tarunāśanaḥ cakrapaḥ śrīpatiḥ ca eva nṛpāṇām cakravartinām īśaḥ ca sarva devānām dvārakā saṃsthitaḥ tathā puṣkaraḥ puṣkarādhyakṣaḥ puṣkaradvīpaḥ eva ca nirākāraḥ nirnimittaḥ nirātaṅkaḥ nirāśrayaḥ devasya viṣṇoḥ īśaśya sarva pāpa vināśanam paṭhan dvijaḥ ca viṣṇu tvam kṣatriyaḥ jayam āpnuyāt vaiśyaḥ dhanam sukham śūdraḥ viṣṇu bhakti samanvitaḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe śrīviṣṇusahasranāmastotranirūpaṇam nāma pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam punar dhyānam samācakṣva śaṅkha cakra gadā dhara viṣṇoḥ īśasya devasya śuddhasya paramātmanaḥ śṛṇu rudra hareḥ dhyānam saṃsāra taru nāśanam sarva ādhāram nirādhāram sarva kāraṇa kāraṇam sthūla deha vihīnam ca cakṣuṣā parivarjitam buddhyā vihīnam deveśam cetasā parivarjitam vyāna ākhya vāyu hīnam vai prāṇa dharṃma vivarjitam punar sūri arcanam vakṣye yat uktam bhṛgave purā om khakholkāya namaḥ om khakholkāya tridaśāya namaḥ om vici ṭha ṭha śirase namaḥ om jñānine ṭha ṭha śikhāyai namaḥ om sahasraraśmaye ṭha ṭha kavacāya namaḥ agni prākāra mantraḥ ayam sūryasya agha vināśanaḥ om ādityāya vidmahe viśva bhāvāya dhīmahi tat naḥ sūrya pracodayāt sakalīkaraṇam kuryāt rāyatryā bhāskarasya ca dharṃma ātmane ca pūrvasmin yamāḥ yā iti ca dakṣiṇe śyāma piṅgalam aiśānyām āgneyyām dīkṣitam yajet vajrapāṇim ca nairṛtyām bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar ca vāyave om candrāya nakṣatra adhipataye namaḥ om aṅgārakāya kṣitisutāya namaḥ om budhāya somasutāya namaḥ om vāc īśvarāya sarva vidyā adhipataye namaḥ om śukrāya mahā ṛṣaye bhṛgusutāya namaḥ om śanaiścarāya sūryātmajāya namaḥ om rāhave namaḥ om ketave namaḥ pūrva ādi īśāna paryantāḥ ete pūjyāḥ vṛṣadhvaja om anūkāya namaḥ om prathama nāthāya namaḥ om buddhāya namaḥ anena āvāhya mantreṇa tatas sūryam visarjayet iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe haridhyānasūryārcanayornirūpaṇam nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam punar sūrya arcanam vakṣye yat uktam dhanadāya hi aṣṭa patram likhet padmam śucau deśe sa karṇikam āvāhanīm tatas baddhā mudrām āvāhayet ravim khakholkam sthāpya mudrām tu sthāpayet mantra rūpiṇīm āgneyyām diśi devasya hṛdayam sthāpayet śiva aiśānyām tu śiraḥ sthāpyam nairṛtyām vinyaset śikhām vāyavyām ca eva netram tu vāruṇyām astram eva ca aiśānyām sthāpayet somam paurandaryām tu lohitam āgneyyām soma tanayam yāmyām ca eva bṛhaspatim nairṛtyām dānavagurum vāruṇyām tu śanaiścaram vāyavyām ca tathā ketum kauberyām rāhum eva ca dvitīyāyām tu kakṣāyām sūryān dvādaśa pūjayet savitā ca eva dhātā ca vivasvān ca mahā balaḥ tvaṣṭā pūṣā tathā ca indraḥ dvādaśaḥ viṣṇuḥ ucyate pūrva ādau arcayet devān indra ādīn śraddhayā naraḥ śeṣaḥ ca vāsukiḥ ca eva nāgān ityādi pūjayet iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe sūryārcanavidhiḥ nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca garuḍa uktam kaśyapāya vakṣye mṛtyuñjaya arcanam uddhāra pūrvakam puṇyam sarva deva mayam matam oṅkāram pūrvam uddhṛtya ju huṅkāṃram tad anantaram sa visargam tṛtīyam syāt mṛtyu dāridraya mardanam īśa viṣṇava ṛka devī ādi kavacam sarva sādhakam amṛta īśam pūjanam samam japanāt mṛtyu hīnāḥ syuḥ sarva pāpa vivarjitāḥ aṣṭottaraśatāt jāpya atrisandhyam dvābhyām ca amṛta kumbham tu cintayet amṛta īśvaram tasya eva aṅga gatām devīm amṛta amṛta bhāṣiṇī m jarā mṛtyu mahā vyādhi śatru śiva śānti dam āhvānam sthāpanam rodham sannidhānam niveśanam dīpa aṃbaram bhūṣaṇam ca naivadyam pāna vījanam mātrā mudrā japa dhyānam dakṣiṇā ca āhutiḥ stutiḥ vādyam gatim ca nṛtyam ca nyāsa yogam pradakṣiṇam ṣaḍaṅga ādi prakāreṇa pūjanam tu krama uditam jānāti arghya pātra arcanam ca ādau astreṇa eva tu tāḍanam śodhanam kavacena eva amṛtīkaraṇam tatas pūjā ca ādhāra śakti ādeḥ prāṇāyāmam tathā āsane pīṭha suddhim tatas kuryāt śoṣaṇa ādyaiḥ tatas smaret ātmānam deva rūpam ca kara aṅga nyāsakam caret ātmānam pūjayet paścāt hṛd abjataḥ mūrtau vā sthaṇḍile vā api kṣipet puṣpam tu bhāsvaram āhvāna dvāra pūjā artham pūjā ca ādhāra śaktitaḥ aṅga ṣaṭkasya pūjā vai kartavyā ca vipaścitaiḥ dharma ādayaḥ ca śakra ādyāḥ sa āyudhāḥ parivārakāḥ yuga veda muhūrtāḥ ca pūjā iyam bhukti mukti kṛt mātṛkāḥ ca gaṇān ca ādau nandi gaṅge ca pūjayet mahākālam ca yamanām dehalyām pūjayet purā om amṛta īśvara om bhairavāya namaḥ evam om juṃ haṃsaḥ sūryāya namaḥ evam śivāya kṛṣṇāya brahmaṇe ca gaṇāya ca caṇḍikāyai sarasvatyai mahā lakṣma ādi pūjayet iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa āvye ācāra kāṇḍe amṛteśamṛtyuñjayapūjanam nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca prāṇeśvaram gāruḍam ca śiva uktam pravadāmi aham sthānāni ādau pravakṣyāmi nāga daṣṭaḥ na jīvati ṣaṣṭhyām ca karkaṭe meṣe mūla āśleṣā maghā ādiṣu kakṣa śroṇi gale sandhau śaṅkha karṇa udara ādiṣu daṇḍī śastradharaḥ bhikṣuḥ na gna ādiḥ kāla dūtakaḥ bāhau ca vakkre grīvāyām daṣṭāyām na hi jīvati śeṣāḥ grahāḥ pratidinam ṣaṣ saṃkhyā parivartanaiḥ nāgabhogaḥ kramāt jñeyaḥ rātrau bāṇa vivartanaiḥ śeṣaḥ arakaḥ phaṇipaḥ candraḥ takṣakaḥ bhaumaḥ īritaḥ karkoṭaḥ jñaḥ guruḥ padmaḥ mahāpadmaḥ ca bhārgavaḥ śaṅkhaḥ śanaiścaraḥ rāhuḥ kulikaḥ ca ahayaḥ grahāḥ rātrau divā suraguroḥ bhāge syāt amara antakaḥ paṅgoḥ kāle divā rāhuḥ kulikena saha sthitaḥ yāma ardha sandhi saṃsthām ca velām kālavatīm caret bāṇa dvi ṣaṣ vahni vāji yuga bhūḥ eka bhāgataḥ divā pādāṅguṣṭhe pāda pṛṣṭhe pāda pṛṣṭhe gulphe jānuni liṅgake nābhau hṛdi stana taṭe kaṇṭhe nāsāpuṭe akṣiṇi tiṣṭhat candraḥ ca jīvet ca puṃsaḥ dakṣiṇa bhāgake kāyasya vāma bhāge tu striyāḥ vāyu vahāt karāt ātmanaḥ paramam bījam haṃsa ākhyam sphaṭika amalam dātavyam viṣa pāpa ghnam bījam tasya caturvidham ṣaṣṭha ārūḍham tṛtīyam syāt sa visargam caturthakam om kuru kule svāhā vidyā trailokya rakṣā artham garuḍena dhṛtā purā vadha īpsuḥ nāga nāgānām mukhe atha praṇavam nyaset svāhā pāda yuge ca eva yuga hā nyāsaḥ īritaḥ gṛhe yatra tat nāgāḥ saṃtyajanti ca sahasra mantram japtvā tu karṇe sūtram dhṛtam tathā yad ṛhe śarkarā japtā kṣiptāḥ nāgāḥ tyajanti tat sapta lakṣasya japyāt hi siddhiḥ prāptā sura asuraiḥ om suvarṇarekhe kukkuṭa vigraha rūpiṇi svāhā evam ca aṣṭadale padma dale varṇa yugam likhet nāma etat vāri dhārābhiḥ snātaḥ daṣṭaḥ viṣam tyajet om pakṣi svāhā aṅguṣṭha ādi kaniṣṭhā antam kare nyasya atha dehake na ākrāmanti ca tad chāyām svapne api viṣa pannagāḥ yaḥ tu lakṣam japet ca asyāḥ sa dṛṣṭvā nāśayet viṣam om hrī hrau hrīṃ bhi ruṇḍāyai svāhā karṇe japtā tu iyam vidyā daṣṭakasya viṣam haret kaṭi taṭe nābhau hṛdi nyaset vakkre am uttamāṅge aḥ nyaset vai haṃsa saṃyutāḥ haṃsaḥ viṣa ādi ca haret japtaḥ dhyātaḥ atha pūjitaḥ garuḍaḥ aham iti dhyātvā kuryāt viṣa harām kriyām haṃ mantram gātra vinyastam viṣa ādi haram īritam nyasya haṃsam vāma kare nāsā mukha nirodha kṛt mantraḥ haret daṣṭakasya tvac māṃsa ādi gatam viṣam sa vāyunā samākṛṣya daṣṭānām garalam haret tanau nyaset daṣṭakasya nīlakaṇṭha ādi saṃsmaret pītam pratyaṅgirā mūlam taṇḍuladbhiḥ viṣa apaham punarnavā phalinīnām mūlam vakkra jam īdṛśam mūlam śukla bṛhatyāḥ tu karkoṭyā gairika ṛṇikam adbhiḥ ghṛṣṭa ghṛta upeta lepaḥ ayam viṣa mardanaḥ viṣam ṛddhim na vrajet ca uṣṇam pibati yaḥ ghṛtam pañcāṅgam tu śirīṣasya mūlam gṛñjana jam tathā sarva aṅga lepataḥ śacā api pānāt vā viṣa hṛt bhavet hrīṃ gonasa ādi viṣa hṛt hṛd lalāṭa visarga antam dhyātam vaśyā di kṛt bhavet japtvā sapta aṣṭa sāhasram garutmān iva sarva gaḥ kaviḥ ca vaśyāḥ strīḥ ca āyuḥ āpnuyāt viṣa hṛt syāt kathā tadvat maṇiḥ vyāsaḥ smṛtaḥ dhruvam iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe sarpaviṣaharopāya prāṇeśvaravidyā nirūpaṇam nāma ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca pāśam dhanuḥ ca cakram ca śūla paṭṭiśam etaiḥ eva āyudhaiḥ yuddhe mantraiḥ śatrūn jayet nṛpaḥ aṣṭa vargam ca aṣṭamam ca khyātam īśāna patrake om kāraḥ brahma bījam syāt hrīṅkāraḥ viṣṇuḥ eva ca hrīṅkāḥ raḥ ca śivaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca gopāla pūjām vakṣyāmi bhukti mukti pradāyinīm dvāre dhātā vidhātā ca gaṅgā yamunayā saha śaṅkha padma nidhī ca eva sāraṅgaḥ śarabhaḥ śriyā pūrve bhadraḥ subhadraḥ dvau dakṣe caṇḍa pracaṇḍakau uttare śrīḥ catur dvāre gaṇaḥ durgā sarasvatī kṣetrasya agni ādi koṇeṣu dikṣu nārada pūrvakam pūrve viṣṇum viṣṇu tapaḥ viṣṇu śaktim samarcayet tatas viṣṇu parīvāram madhye śaktim ca kūrṃmakam anantam pṛthivīm dharmam jñānam vairāgyam agnitaḥ aiśvaryam vāyu pūrvam ca prakāśa ātmānam uttare vimalā ādyāḥ āsanam ca prācyām śrīṃ hrīṃ prapūjayet hṛd ādi pūrva koṇaṣu astram śaktim ca pūrvatas rukmiṇī satyabhāmā ca sunandā nāgnajitī api lakṣmaṇā mitravindā ca jāmbavatyā śuśīlayā śaṅkha cakra gadā padmam musalam śārṅgam arcayet khaṅgam pāśa aṅkuśam prācyām śrīvatsam kaustubham yajet mukuṭam vala mālām ca aindra ādyān dhvaja mukhyakān kumuda ādyān viṣvaksenam śriyā kṛṣṇam saha arcayet japyāt dhyānāt pūjanāt ca sarvān kāmān avān puyāt iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe śrīgopālapūjānirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam pūjā mantrān śrīdhara ādyān dharṃma kāma ādi dāyakān om hrīṃ śrīṃ klīṃ hrūm om namaḥ puruṣottama apratirūpa lakṣmī nivāsa jagat kṣobhaṇa sarva strī hṛdaya dāraṇa tribhuvana mada unmādana kara sura asura manuja suṃdarī jana manāṃsi tāpaya tāpaya śoṣaya śoṣaya māraya māraya stambhaya stambhaya drāvaya drāvaya ākarṣaya ākarṣaya parama subhaga sarva saubhāgya kara sarva kāma prada amukam hana hana cakreṇa gadayā khaḍgena sarva bāṇaiḥ bhidhi bhindhi pāśena kuṭṭa kuṭṭa aṅkuśena tāḍaya tāḍaya turu turu kim tiṣṭhasi tāray om śrīṃ śrīdharāya trailokya mohanāya namaḥ klīṃ puruṣottamāya trailokya mohanāya namaḥ om viṣṇave trailokya mohanāya namaḥ om śrīṃ klīṃ trailokya mohanāya vipṇave namaḥ trailokya mohanāḥ mantrāḥ sarve sarva artha sādhakāḥ sarve cintyā pṛthak vā api vyāsāt saṃkṣepataḥ atha vā āsanam mūrti mantram ca homa ādi aṅga ṣaṣ aṅgakam cakram gadām ca khaḍgam ca musalam śam makha śarṅgakam śaram pāśam ca aṅkuśam ca lakṣmī garuḍa saṃyutam viṣvaksenam vistarāt vānaraḥ sarvam avāpnuyāt iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye trailokyamohinīpūjanavidhiḥ nāma ekonatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca vistareṇa pravakṣyāmi śrīdharasya arcanam śubham parivāraḥ ca sarveṣām hi paṇḍitaiḥ om śrāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ om śrīṃ śirase svāhā om śrū śikhāyai vaṣaṭū om śraiṃ kavacāya hum om śrauṃ netratrayāya vauṣaṭ om śraḥ astrāya phaṭ iti darśayet ātmanaḥ mudrām śaṅkha cakra gadā ādikām dhyātvā ātmānam śrīdhara ākhyam śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam tatas tam pūjayet devam maṇḍale svastika ādike āsanam pūjayet ādau devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ebiḥ mantraiḥ mahādeva tān matrān śṛṇu śaṅkara om śrīdhara āsana devatāḥ om samasta parivārāya cyuta āsanāya namaḥ om dhātre namaḥ om vidhātre namaḥ om gaṅgāyai namaḥ om yamunāyai namaḥ om ādhāra śaktayai namaḥ om kūrṃmāya namaḥ om anantāya namaḥ om pṛthivyai namaḥ om dharṃmāya namaḥ om jñānāya namaḥ om vairāgyāya namaḥ om aiśvaryāya namaḥ om adharṃmāya namaḥ om ajñānāya namaḥ om avairāgyāya namaḥ om anaiśvaryāya namaḥ om kandāya namaḥ om nālāya namaḥ om padmāya praṇāśanaiḥ om hrīṃ śrīdharāya trailokya mohanāya viṣṇave namaḥ āgaccha om śriyai namaḥ om śrāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ om śrīṃ śirase namaḥ om śrūṃ śikhāyai namaḥ om śraiṃ kavacāya namaḥ om śrauṃ netratrayāya namaḥ om śraḥ astrāya namaḥ om śaṅkhāya namaḥ om padmāya namaḥ om cakrāya namaḥ om gadāyai namaḥ om śrī vatsāya namaḥ om vanamālāyai namaḥ om pītāmbarāya namaḥ om vrahmaṇe namaḥ om nāradāya namaḥ om om tamase namaḥ om viṣvaksenāya namaḥ abhiṣekam tathā vasttram tatas yajñopavītakam gandham puṣpam tathā dhūpam dīpam annam pradakṣiṇam śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam sūrya koṭi sama prabham kirīṭinam udāra aṅgam vanamālā samanvitam para brahma svarūpam ca śrīdharam cintayet sudhīḥ śrīnivāsāya devāya namaḥ śrīpataye namaḥ śrīdharāya sa śārṅgāya śrī pradāya namaḥ namaḥ śrī vallabhāya śāntāya śrīmate ca namaḥ namaḥ śrīparvata nivāsāya namaḥ śreyaskarāya ca śreyasām pataye ca eva hi āśramāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ śreyaḥ svarūpāya śrīkarāya namaḥ namaḥ śaraṇyāya vareṇyāya namaḥ bhūyas namaḥ namaḥ iti rudra samākhyātā pūjā viṣṇoḥ mahātmanaḥ iṃ yaḥ paṭhate adhyāyam viṣṇu pūjā prakāśakam sa vidhūya iha pāpāni yāti viṣṇoḥ param padam iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe śrīdharācanavidhiḥ nāma triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam bhūyas evam jagannātha pūjām kathaya me prabho yayā tareyam saṃsāra sāgaram hi ati dustaram arcanam viṣṇu devasya vakṣyāmi vṛṣabhadhvaja tat śṛṇuṣva mahābhāga bhukti mukti pradam śubham kṛtvā snānam tatas sandhyām tatas yāga gṛham vrajet prakṣālya pāṇī pādau ca ācamya ca viśeṣataḥ mūlamantram ca devasya śṛṇu rudra vadāmi te om śrīṃ hrīṃ śrīdharāya viṣṇave namaḥ ayam mantraḥ sureśasya viṣṇoḥ īśasya vācakaḥ aṅganyāsam tatas kuyyāt debhiḥ mantrauḥ vicakṣaṇaḥ om hāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ om hīṃ śirase svāhā om śikhāyai vaṣaṭ om haiṃ kavacāya hum om hauṃ netratrayāya vauṣaṭ om haḥ astrāya phaṭ iti mantraḥ samākhyātaḥ mayā te prabhaviṣṇunā nyāsam kṛtvā ātmanaḥ mudrām darśayet vijita ātmavān tatas dhyāyet param viṣṇu tdṛt koṭara samāśritam ratna hāra kirīṭena saṃyuktam parameśvaram aham viṣṇuḥ iti dhyātvā kṛtvā vai śodhana ādikam yaṃ kṣaiṃ ram iti bījaiḥ ca kaṭhinī kṛtya nāmabhiḥ tatra pūrva ukta rūpam tu bhāvayitvā vṛṣadhvaja ātma pūjām tatas kuryāt randha puṣpa ādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ āvāhya pūjayet sarvāḥ devatāḥ āsanasya yāḥ mantraiḥ ebhiḥ mahādeva tat mantram śṛṇu śaṅkara viṣṇo āsana devatāḥ āgacchata om samasta aṅga ādayaḥ naraiḥ pūjayitvā mahātmānam viṣṇum brahma svarūpiṇam stuvīta ca anayā stutyā paramātmānam avyayam viṣṇave vāsudevāya namaḥ sthiti karāya ca grasiṣṇave namaḥ ca eva namaḥ pralaya śāyine devānām prabhave ca eva yajñānām prabhave namaḥ munīnām prabhave nityam yakṣāṇām prabhaviṣṇave jiṣṇave sarva devānām sarvagāya mahātmane sarvaloka hita arthāya loka adhyakṣāya vai namaḥ vara pradāya śāntāya vareṇyāya namaḥ namaḥ śaraṇyāya su rūpāya dharma kāma artha dāyine elam tu pūjayet viṣṇum mūlamantreṇa śaṅkara etat yaḥ ca paṭhet vidvān viṣṇu bhaktaḥ pumān hara śṛṇuyāt śrāvayet vā api viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe viṣṇupūjāvidhiḥ nāma ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam pañcatattva arcanam brūhi śaṅkha cakra gadā dhara yena vijñāna mātreṇa naraḥ yāti param padam maṅgalyam maṅgalam divyam rahasyam kāma dam param tat śṛṇuṣva mahādeva pavitram kali nāśanam ekaḥ eva avyayaḥ śāntaḥ parama ātmā sanātanaḥ vāsudevaḥ dhruvaḥ śuddhaḥ sarva vyāpī nirañjanaḥ saḥ eva māyāyāḥ deva pañcadhā saṃsthitaḥ hariḥ loka anugraha kṛt viṣṇuḥ sarva duṣṭa vināśanaḥ vāsudeva sva rūpeṇa tathā saṅkarṣaṇena ca nārāyaṇa sva rūpeṇa pañcadhā hi advayaḥ sthitaḥ eteṣām vācakān mantrān etān śṛṇu vṛṣadhvaja om aṃ vāsudevāya namaḥ om āṃ saṃkarṣaṇāya namaḥ om aṃ pradyumnāya namaḥ om aniruddhāya namaḥ om om nārāyaṇāya namaḥ pañca mantrāḥ samākhyātāḥ devānām vācakāḥ tava sarva pāpa harāḥ puṇyāḥ sarva roga vināśanāḥ adhunā saṃpravakṣyāmi pañcatattva arcanam śubham ādau snānam prakurvīta snātvā sandhyām samācaret arcana āgāram āsādya prakṣālya ārṅghya ādikam tathā ācamya upaviśet prājñaḥ baddha āsanam abhīpsitam śoṣaṇa ādi tatas kuryāt aṃ kṣaiṃ ram iti mantrakaiḥ sāmānyam kaṭhinīkṛtya ca aṇḍam utpādayet tatas vibhidya aṇḍam tatas hi aṇḍe bhāvayet parameśvaram vāsudevam jagannātham pītakauśeyavāsasam sahasra āditya saṅkāśam sphurat makara kuṇḍalam tatas saṃkarṣaṇam devam ātmānam cintayet prabhum pradyumnam aniruddham ca śrīmat nārāyaṇam tatas indra ādīn ca surān tasmāt devadevāt samutthitān vyāpakam mūlamantreṇa ca aṅganyāsam tatas param aṅgamantraiḥ mahādeva tān mantrān śṛṇu suvrata om āṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ om īṃ śirase svastika ādike om padmāya namaḥ aṅganyāsam ca kṛtvā tu mudrāḥ sarvāḥ pradaśayat ātmānam vāsudevam ca dhyātvā ca eva para īśvaram āsanam pūjayet paścāt āvāhya vidhivat naraḥ dvāre dhātuḥ vidhātuḥ ca pūjā kāryā vṛṣadhvaja garuḍam pūjayet agre vāsudevasya śaṅkara dharmam jñānam ca vairāgyam aiśvaryam pūrva deśataḥ āgneya ādiṣu arcayet vai adharma ādi catuṣṭayam pūrva ādi padma patreṣu pūjyāḥ saṃkarṣaṇa ādayaḥ karṇikāyām vāsudevam pūjayet parameśvaram pāñcajanya ādayaḥ pūjyāḥ aiśānī ādiṣu saṃsthitāḥ śaktayaḥ ca eva pūrva ādau devadevasya śaṅkara indra ādayaḥ lokapālāḥ pūjyāḥ pūrva ādiṣu sthitāḥ adhas nāga tu brahmāṇam pūjayet sudhīḥ iti sthāna kramaḥ jñeyaḥ maṇḍale śaṅkara tvayā āvāhya maṇḍale devam kṛtvā nyāsam tu tasya ca mudrām pradarśya pādī adīn dadyāt mūlena śaṅkara snānam vastram tathā ācāmam gandham puṣpam ca dhūpakam dīpam naivedyam ācāmam namaskāram pradakṣiṇam om namaḥ vāsudevāya namaḥ sakarṣaṇāya ca pradyumnāya ādidevāya aniruddhāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ nārāyaṇāya eva pataye namaḥ nara pūjyāya kīrtyāya stutyāya vara dāya ca an ādi nidhanāya eva purāṇāya namaḥ namaḥ sṛṣṭi saṃhāra kartre ca brahmaṇaḥ pataye namaḥ saṃkāra vṛkṣa chetre ca māyā bhetre namaḥ namaḥ vahu rūpāya tīrthāya triguṇāya aguṇāya ca mokṣa dāya namaḥ namaḥ mokṣadvārāya dharmāya nirmāṇāya namaḥ namaḥ saṃsāra sāgare ghore nimagnam mām samuddhara tvām ava sarvagam viṣṇum gataḥ aham śaraṇam gataḥ jñāna dīpa pradānena tamaḥ muktam prakāśaya evam stuvīta deveśam sarva kleśa vināśanam stātraiḥ stutvā vai nīlalohita pañcatattva samāyuktam dhyāyot viṣṇum naraḥ hṛdi sarva kāma pradā śreṣṭhā vāsudevasya śaṅkara etad pūjana mātreṇa kṛtakṛtyaḥ bhavet naraḥ idam ca yaḥ paṭhet rudra pañcatattva arcanam naraḥ śṛṇuyāt śravāyet vā api viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe ca navidhiḥ nāma dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sudarśanasya pūjām me vada śaṅkha gadā dhara graha roga ādikam sarvam yat kṛtvā nāśam eti vai sudarśanasya cakrasya śṛṇu pūjām vṛṣadhvaja mūlamantreṇa vai nyāsam mūlamantram śṛṇuṣva ca sahasrāram hum phaṭ namaḥ mantraḥ praṇava pūrvakaḥ kathitaḥ sarva duṣṭānām nāśakaḥ mantra bhedakaḥ dhyāyet mudarśanam devam hṛdi padme amale śubhe śaṅka cakra gadā padma dharam saumyam kirīṭinam āvāhya maṇḍale devam pūrva ukta vidhinā hara pūjayitvā japet mantram śatam aṣṭa uttaram naraḥ jvālā mālā pradīptāya sahasra ārāya cakṣuṣe sarva duṣṭa vināśāya sarva pātaka mardine pālana arthāya lokānām duṣṭa asura vināśine ugrāya ca eva saumyāya caṇḍāya ca namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ cakṣuḥ kva rūpāya saṃsāra bhaya bhedine māyā pañjara bhetre ca śivāya ca namaḥ namaḥ graha ati graha rūpāya grahāṇām pateya namaḥ kālāya mṛtyave ca eva bhīmāya ca namaḥ namaḥ viṣṇu rūpāya śāntāya ca āyudhānām dharāya ca viṣṇu śastrāya cakrāya namaḥ bhūyas namaḥ namaḥ yaḥ paṭhet parayā bhaktyā viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati sa pāpam bhasmasātkṛtvā viṣṇu lokāya kalpate iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe sudarśanapūjāvidhiḥ nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam punar deva arcanam brūhi hṛṣīkeśa gadādhara śṛṇvataḥ nā asti tṛptiḥ me gadataḥ tava pūjanam tat śṛṇuṣva jagannāthaḥ yena viṣṇuḥ pratuṣyati pravakṣyāmi param puṇyam tat ādau śṛṇu śaṅkara om saiṃ kṣaiṃ śirase namaḥ iti praṇava saṃyutaḥ ayam nava akṣaraḥ mantraḥ sarva vidyā pradāyakaḥ asya aṅgāni mahādeva tān śṛṇuṣva vṛṣadhvaja om kṣāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ om śirase svāhā śiraḥ proktam vaṣaṭ tathā om kāra yuktā devasya śikhā jñeyā vṛṣadhvaja om kṣaiṃ kavacāya hum vai kavacam parikīrtitam om netratrayāya vauṣaṭ netram devasya kīrtitam om haḥ astrāya phaṭ astram devasya kīrtitam pūjā vidhim pravakṣyāmi nat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ādau snātvā tathā ācamya tatas yāga gṛham vrajet tatas praviśya vidhivat śoṣaṇa ādikam yaṃ kṣaiṃ ram iti bījaiḥ ca kaṭhinīkṛtya lam iti aṇḍam utpādya ca tatas om kāreṇa eva bhedayet aṇḍa madhye hayagrīvam ātmānam paricintayet go kṣīra sadṛśam tadvat sūrya koṭi samagra bham śaṅkham cakram gadām padmam dhārayantam caturbhujam kirīṭinam kuṇḍalinam vanamālā samaṃnvitam su cakram su kapolam ca ṣīta ambara dharam vibhum tatas ca darśayet mudrām śaṅkhapadma ādikām śubhām dhyāyet dhyātvā arcayet viṣṇum mūlamantreṇa śaṅkara tatas ca āvāhayet rudra devatāḥ āsanasya yāḥ om hayagrīva āsanasya āgacchata ca devatāḥ āvāhya maṇḍale tāḥ tu pūjayet svastika ādike dvāre dhātuḥ vidhātuḥ ca pūjā kāryā vṛṣadhvaja asya madhyeḥ acanam kāryam dvāre gaṅgām ca pūjayet yamunām ca mahā devīm śaṅkha padma nidhī tathā garuḍam pūjayet agre madhye śaktim ca pūjayet ādhāra ākhyām mahādeva tatas kūrmam samarcayet anantam pṛthivīm paścāt dharma jñāne tatas vairāgyam atha ca aiśvaryam āgneya ādiṣu pūjayet adharma ajñāna avairāgya anaiśrargya ādīn tu pūrvatas arka soma agni saṃjñānām maṇḍalānām hi pūjanam vimala utkarṣiṇī jñānā kriyā yoge vṛṣadhvaja prahvī satyā tathā īśānā anugrahau śaktayaḥ hi amūḥ pūrva ādiṣu ca patreṣu pūjyāḥ ca vimalā ādayaḥ anugrahā karṇikāyām pūjyā śreyaḥ arthibhiḥ naraiḥ snāna gandha pradānena puṣpa dhūpa pradānataḥ dīpa naivedya dānena āsanasya arcanam śubham tatas ca āvāhayet devam hayagrīvam sureśvaram vāma nāsā puṭena eva āgacchantam vicintayet āgacchataḥ prayogeṇa mūlamantreṇa śaṅkara āvāhanam prakartavyam devadevasya śaṅkhinaḥ āvāhya maṇḍale tasya nyāsam kuryāt atandritaḥ hayagrīvam mahādevam sura asura namaskṛtam indra ādi lokapālaiḥ ca saṃyuktam viṣṇum avyayam pradarśayet mudrāḥ śaṅkha cakra ādikāḥ śubhāḥ pādya arghya ācamanīyāni tatas dadyāt ca viṣṇave devam saṃsthāpya vidhivat vastram dadyāt vṛṣadhvaja tatas hi ācamanam dadyāt upavītam tatas śubham dhyātvā pādya ādikam bhūyas dadyāt devāya śaṅkara dadyāt bhairava devāya mūlamantreṇa śaṅkara om kṣāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ anena hṛdayam yajet om kṣīṃ śirase namaḥ ca śirasaḥ pūjanam bhavet om kṣūṃ śikhāyai namaḥ ca śikhām etena pūjayet om kṣaiṃ kavacāya namaḥ kavacam paripūjayet om kṣaiṃ netrāya namaḥ ca netram ca anena pūjayet om kṣaḥ astrāya namaḥ iti astram ca anena pūjayet hṛdayam ca śiraḥ ca eva śikhām ca kavacam tathā pūrva ādiṣu pradeśeṣu hi etāḥ tu paripūjayet pūjayet paramām devīm lakṣmīm lakṣmī pradām śubhām śaṅkham padmam tathā cakram gadām pūrva āditaḥ racayet khaḍgam ca musalam pāśam aṅkuśam sa śaram dhanuḥ śrīvatsam kaustubham mālām tathā pīta ambaram śubham brahmāṇam nāradam siddham gurum para gurum tathā indram sa vāhanam ca atha parivāra yutam tathā agnim yamam nirṛtim ca varuṇam vāyum eva ca somam īśānam evam vai brahmāṇam paripūjayet vajram śaktim tathā daṇḍam khaṅgam pāśam dhvajam gadām triśūlam cakra padme ca āyudhāni atha pūjayet viṣvaksenam tatas devam aiśānyām diśi pūjayet pūjā kāryā mahādeva hi anantasya vṛṣadhvaja devasya mūlamantreṇa pūjā kāryā vṛṣadhvaja gandham puṣpam tathā dhūpam dīpam naivedyam eva ca stuvīta ca anyā stutyā praṇava ādyaiḥ vṛṣadhvaja om namaḥ haya śirase vidyā adhyakṣāya vai namaḥ namaḥ vidyā svarūpāya vidyā dātre namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ śāntāya devāya triguṇāya ātmane namaḥ namaḥ ca īśvara vandyāya śaṅka cakra dhāraya ca triguṇāya aguṇāya eva brahma viṣṇu svarūpiṇe iti evam saṃstavam kṛtvā devadevam vicintayet sūrya koṭi pratīkāśam sarva avayava sundaram hayagrīvaḥ mahī īśa īśam paramātmānam avyayam iti te kathitā pūjā hayagrīvasya śaṅkara iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe hayagrīvapūjāvidhiḥ nāma catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam nyāsa ādikam pravakṣyāmi gāyattryāḥ śṛṇu śaṅkara viśvāmitra ṛṣiḥ ca eva savitā ca atha devatā brahma śīrṣā rudra śikhā viṣṇoḥ hṛdaya saṃśritā trailokya caraṇā jñeyā pṛthivī kukṣi saṃsthitā evam jñātvā tu gāyattrīm japet dvādaśa lakṣakam tripadā aṣṭa akṣarā jñeyā catuṣpādā ṣaṣ akṣarā gāyattrīm vinyaset nityam sarva pāpa graṇa āśinīm gulpha madhye jaṅghayoḥ viddhi jānunoḥ ūrvoḥ guhye ca vṛṣaṇe nāḍyām nābhau tanū udare stanayoḥ hṛdi kaṇṭha oṣṭha mukhe tāluni ca aṃsayoḥ netre bhuvār lalāṭe ca pūrvasyām dakṣiṇa uttare paścame mūrdhni ca ākāram nyaset varṇān vadāmi aham indranīlam ca vahnim ca pītam śyāmam ca kāpilam śvetam vidyutprabham tāram kṛṣṇam raktam krameṇa tat śyāmam śuklam tathā pītam śvetam vai padmarāga vat śaṅkha varṇam pāṇḍuram ca raktam ca āsava sannibham arka varṇa samam saumyam śaṅkha ābham śvetam eva ca yat yat spṛśati hastena yat ca paśyati cakṣuṣā pūtam bhavati tat sarvam gāyattryāḥ na param viduḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe gāyattrīnyāsanirūpaṇam nāma pañcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sandhyā vidhim pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu rudra agha nāśanam prāṇāyāma trayam kṛtvā sandhyā snānam upakramet sa praṇavām sa vyāhṛtim gāyattrīm śirasā saha tris paṭhet āyata praṇaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ saḥ ucyate manaḥ vāk rāya jam doṣam prāṇāyāmaiḥ dahet dvijaḥ tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu prāṇāyāma paraḥ bhavet sāyam agniḥ ca mā iti uktā prātar sūrya iti apaḥ pibet āpaḥ punantu madhyāhne upaspṛśya yathāvidhi āpohiṣṭhā iti ṛcā kuryāt mārjanam tu kuśa udakaiḥ vāc manaḥ karma jān doṣān nava etān navabhiḥ dahet samuddhṛtya udakam pāṇau japtvā ca drupadām kṣipet tri paṭ aṣṭau dvādaśadhā vartayet agham arpaṇam divā rātrau ca yat pāpam sarvam naśyati tad kṣaṇāt pūrva saṃdhyām japan tiṣṭhet paścimām upaviśya ca mahāvyāhṛti saṃyuktām gāyattrīm praṇava anvitām tri yugam tu sahasreṇa gāyattrī hanti duṣkṛtam raktā bhavati gāyattrī sāvitrī śukla varṇikā kṛṣṇā sarasvatī jñeyā saṃdhyā trayam udāhṛtam om bhūḥ vinyasya hṛdaye om bhuvaḥ śirasi nyaset om svar iti śikhāyām ca gāyattryāḥ prathamam padam tṛtīyena aṅga vinyāsam caturtham sarvatas nyaset śivaḥ tasyāḥ tu sarva ahne prāṇāyāma param nyaset tripadā yā tu gāyattrī brahma viṣṇu maheśvarī viniyogam ṛṣicchandaḥ jñātvā tu japam ārabhet tam hanti sūryaḥ sandhyāyām na upāstim kurute tu yaḥ chandaḥ tu devī gāyattrī paramātmā ca devatā iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe saṃdhyāvidhiḥ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam gāyattrī paramā devī bhukti mukti pradā ca tām aṣṭa uttaram sahasram vā athavā aṣṭaśatam japet saṃdhyāyām sarva pāpa ghnīm devīm āvāhya pūjayet bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar sva mantreṇa yutām dvādaśa nāmabhiḥ vedamātre ca brahmāṇī kauśikī kramāt aṣṭottarasahasram ghṛtam yathā lakṣam tu japtavyam uttare śikhare jātā bhūmyām parvata vāsinī brahmaṇā samanujñātā gaccha devi yathāsukham iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe gāyattrīkalpanirūpaṇam nāma saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam navamī ādau yajet durgām hrīṃ durge rakṣiṇi iti ca gaurī kālī umā durgā bhadrā kāntiḥ sarasvatī maṅgalā vijayā lakṣmīḥ śivā nārāyaṇī kramāt mārge tṛtīyām ārabhya pūjayet na viyoga bhāj aṣṭādaśa bhujām kheṭakam ghaṇṭām darpaṇam tarjanīm dhanuḥ dhvajam ḍamarukam paraśum pāśam eva ca kapāla śaraka aṅkuśān vajra cakram śalākām ca aṣṭādaśa bhujām smaret mantraḥ śrī bhagavatyāḥ ca pravakṣyāmi japa ādikam om namaḥ bhagavati cāmuṇḍe śmaśāna vāsini kapāla haste mahāpreta samārūḍhe mahā vimāna mālā ākule kālarātri bahu gaṇa parivṛte mahā mukhe bahubhuje su ghaṇṭā ḍamaru kiṅkiṇīke aṭṭa aṭṭahāse kili kili hum sarva nāda śabda bahule gaja carma prāvṛta śarīre rudhira māṃsa digdhe mahā rākṣasi raudra daṃṣṭrā karāle bhīma aṭṭa aṭṭahāse sphurita vidyut sama prabhe cala cala karāla netre hili hili lalat jihve daṃṣṭrayā daṃśaya daṃśaya kīlakena kīlaya kīlaya kartārikayā pāṭaya pāṭaya aṅkuśena gṛhṇa gṛhṇa brahmāṇi ehi ehi māheśvari ehi ehi kaumāri ehi ehi vārāhi ehi ehi aṣṭa uttara padānām hi mālā mantra mayī japaḥ ekaikra padam aṣṭa sahasradhā tri madhura akta tila aṣṭa sahasra hā ameḥ tilān trimadhura aktān ca sahasram ca aṣṭa homayet mahāmāṃsam trimadhurāt atha vā sarva karma kṛt vāri sarṣapa bhasma ādi kṣepāt yuddha ādike jayaḥ aṣṭāviṃśa bhujā dhyeyā aṣṭādaśa bhujā athavā dvādaśa aṣṭa bhujā vā api dhyeyā vā api catur bhujā khaṅkha ghaṇṭā anvitau ca anyau dhvaja daṇḍa yutau parau anyau paraśu cakra āḍhyau ḍamaru darpaṇa anvitau śakti hasta āśritau ca anyau musala anvitau pāśa tomara saṃyuktau ḍhakrā paṇava saṃyutau jaya tvam kila bhūta īśe sarva bhūta samāvṛte rakṣa mām nija bhūtebhyaḥ valim gṛhṇa namaḥ astu te iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe durgājapapūjābalimantranirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam punar deva arcanam brūhi saṃkṣepeṇa janārdana vāsudevaḥ uvāca śṛṇu sūryasya rudra tvam punar vakṣyāmi pūjanam om uccais śravase namaḥ om aruṇāya namaḥ om daṇḍine namaḥ om piṅgalāya namaḥ om aṃ prabhūtāya namaḥ imam tu pūjayet madhye prabhūtāmala saṃjñakam om aṃ vimalāya namaḥ om aṃ sārāya namaḥ om aṃ ādhārāya namaḥ om aṃ parama mukhāya namaḥ iti āgneya ādi koṇeṣu pūjyāḥ vai vimalā ādayaḥ om padmāya namaḥ om karṇikāyai namaḥ dīptā ādyāḥ pūjayet madhye pūjayet sarvatomukhīḥ om vām rāṃ dīptāyai namaḥ om vīṃ rīṃ sūkṣmāyai namaḥ om vūṃ rūṃ bhadrāyai namaḥ om vaiṃ (raiṃ jayāyai namaḥ om vauṃ vibūtyai namaḥ om vaṃ adhorāyai namaḥ om vaṃ vaidyutāyai namaḥ om vaḥ vijayāyai namaḥ om arka āsanāya namaḥ om hrāṃ sūrya mūrtaye namaḥ etāḥ tu pūjayet madhye hrat mantrān śṛṇu śaṅkara om haṃ sam khaṃ khakholkāya krāṃ krīṃ saḥ svāhā sūrya mūrtaye namaḥ anena āvāhanam kuryāt sthāpanam sannidhāpanam mudrāyāḥ darśanam rudra mūlamantreṇa vā hara eka cakra ratha ārūḍham dvi bāhum dhṛta paṅkajam evam dhyāyet sadā sūryam mūlamantram śṛṇuṣva ca om hrāṃ hrīṃ saḥ sūryāya namaḥ vāra trayam padma mudrām bimba mudrām ca darśayet om āṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ om arkāya śirase svāhā om aḥ bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar jvālini śikhāyai vaṣaṭ om hum kavacāya hum om bhām netrābhyām vauṣaṭ om vaḥ astrāya phaṭ iti āgneyyām atha vaiśānyām nairṛtyām arcayet hara hi vāyavyām netram ca antar prapūjayet dakṣiṇe pūjayet rudra pati varṇam gurum yajet paścime ca eva bhūteśam uttare bhārgavam sitam śanaiścaram kṛṣṇa varṇam nairṛtyām diśi pūjayet rāhum vāyavya deśe tu nandyāvarta nibhim hara aiśānyām dhūmra varṇam tu ketum sam paripūjayet om soṃ somāya namaḥ om buṃ budhāya namaḥ om bṛṃ bṛhaspataye namaḥ om bhaṃ bhārgavāya namaḥ om aṃ aṅgārakāya namaḥ om śam śanaiścarāya namaḥ om raṃ rāhave namaḥ pādya ādīn mūlamantreṇa dattvā sūryāya śaṅkara aiśānyām diśi bhūteśa tejaḥ caṇḍam tu pūjayet om tejaścaṃṇḍāya hum phaṭ svadhā svāhā pauṣaṭ kṛtvā śirasi tat pātram jānubhyām avanim gataḥ darghyam tu sūryāya vṛṣadhvaja gaṇam gurūn prapūjya atha sarvān devān an prapūjayet om gaṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ om aṃ gurubhyaḥ namaḥ sūryasya kathitā pūjā kṛtvā etām viṣṇu loka bhāj iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe sūryārcanaprakāraḥ nāma ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam śaṅkaraḥ uvāca māheśvarīm ca me pūjām vada śaṅkha gadā dhara yām jñātvā mānavāḥ siddhim gacchanti parameśvara śṛṇu māheśvarīm pūjām kathyamānām vṛṣadhvaja ādau snātvā tathā ācamya hi āsane ca upaviśya ca nyāsam kṛtvā maṇḍale vai maheśvaram om hāṃ śiva āsana devatāḥ āgacchata iti anena āvāhayet rudra devatāḥ āsanasya yāḥ om hāṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ om hāṃ sarasvatyai namaḥ om hāṃ nandine namaḥ om hāṃ mahākālāya namaḥ om hāṃ gaṅgāyai namaḥ om hāṃ lakṣmyai namaḥ om hāṃ mahākalāyai namaḥ om hāṃ astrāya namaḥ iti om hāṃ brahmaṇe vāstu adhipataye namaḥ om hāṃ gurubhyaḥ namaḥ om hāṃ ādhāra śaktyai namaḥ om hāṃ anantāya namaḥ om hāṃ dharmāya namaḥ om hāṃ jñānāya namaḥ om hāṃ vairāgyāya namaḥ om hāṃ aiśvaryāya namaḥ om hāṃ adharmāya namaḥ om hāṃ ajñānāya namaḥ om hāṃ avairāgyāya namaḥ om hāṃ anaiśvaryāya namaḥ om hāṃ urdhva chandāya namaḥ om hāṃ adhas chandāya namaḥ om hāṃ padmāya namaḥ om hāṃ karṇikāyai namaḥ om hāṃ vāmāyai japa pūjā samarpaṇam māheśī kathitā pūjā rudra pāpa vināsinī iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe maheśvarapūjāvidhiḥ nāma catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam om kāraḥ candramāḥ vahniḥ brahnā nāgaḥ śikhidhvajaḥ raviḥ viṣṇuḥ śivaḥ proktaḥ kramāt tantuṣu devatāḥ aṣṭottaraśatam kuryāt pañcāśat pañcaviṃśatim rudraḥ attamādi vijñeyam mānam ca granthayaḥ daśa dānavān abravīt hariḥ viṣṇu ukte hi abravīt nāgaḥ vāsukeḥ anujaḥ tadā vṛṇīta ca vapitṛ ākhyam varam ca idam vṛṣadhvaja prāvṛṣ kāle tu ye martyāḥ na arciṣyanti pavitrakaiḥ teṣām sāṃvatsarī pūjā viphalā surāḥ catuḥ ṣaṣṭi padāḥ devāḥ iti evam parikīrtitāḥ carakī ca vidārī ca pūtanā pāpa rākṣasī īśāna ādyāḥ tatas bāhye deva ādyāḥ hetuka ādayaḥ agnijihvaḥ kālakaḥ ca karālaḥ aiśānyām bhīma rūpaḥ tu pātāle preta nāyakaḥ ākāśe gandhamālī syāt kṣetrapālān tatas yajet vistāra abhihatam dairghyam rāśim vāstoḥ tu kārayet kṛtvā ca vasubhiḥ bhāgam śeṣam baddhā yam ādiśet punar guṇitam aṣṭābhiḥ ṛ bhāgam tu bhājayet yat śeṣam tat bhavet ṛkṣam bhāgaiḥ hṛtvā avyayam bhavet ṛkṣam caturguṇam kṛtvā navabhiḥ bhāga hāritam śeṣam aṃśam vijānīyāt devalasya matam yathā aṣṭābhiḥ guṇitam piṇḍam ṣaṣṭibhiḥ bhāgāharitam yat śeṣam tat bhavet jīvam maraṇam vāstu kroḍe gṛham kuryāt na pṛṣṭhe mānavaḥ sadā vāma pārśvena na atra kāryā vicāraṇā siṃha kanyā tulāyām ca dvāram śudhyet atha uttaram evam ca vṛścika ādau syāt pūrva dakṣiṇa paścimam dvāram dīrgha ardha vistāram dvārāṇi aṣṭau smṛtāni ca santāna preṣya nīca tvam sva yānam svarṇa bhūṣaṇam suta hīnam tu raudreṇa vīrya ghnam dakṣiṇe tathā vahnau badhaḥ ca āyuḥ vṛddhiṃ puttra lābha su tṛpti daḥ dhanade nṛpa pīḍā dam artha ghnam roga dam jale dvārāṇi uttara saṃjñāni pūrva dvārāṇi vacmi aham rāja ghnam kopa dam pūrve phalataḥ dvāram īritam īśāna ādau bhavet pūrvam agneyī ādau tu dakṣiṇam nairṛtya ādau paścimam syāt vāyavī ādau tu ca uttaram aṣṭa bhāge kṛte bhāge dvārāṇām ca phala aphalam aśvattha plakṣa nyagrodhāḥ pūrva ādau syāt udumbaraḥ gṛhasya śobhanaḥ proktaḥ īśāne ca eva sālmaliḥ pūjitaḥ vigna hārī syāt prāsādasya gṛhasya ca iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe vāstumānalakṣaṇam nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca prāsādānām lakṣaṇam ca vakṣye śaunaka tat śṛṇu catuḥ ṣaṣṭi padam kṛtvā diś vidikṣu upalakṣitam catuṣkoṇam caturbhiḥ ca dvārāṇi sūrya saṃkhyayā bhittīnām kalpanā bhavet ūrdhva kṣetra samā jaṅghā jaṅghā ardha dviguṇam bhavet garbha vistāra vistīrṇaḥ śuka aṅghriḥ ca vidhīyate nirgamaḥ tu śuka aṅghreḥ ca ucchrāyaḥ śikhara ardha gaḥ atha vā api samam vāstum kṛtvā ṣoḍaśa bhāgikam catur bhāgena bhittīnām ucchrāyaḥ syāt pramāṇataḥ dviguṇaḥ śikhara ucchrāyaḥ bhitti ucchāyāt ca mānataḥ śikhara ardhasya vidheyāḥ tu pradakṣiṇāḥ pañca bhāgena saṃbhajya garbha mānam vicakṣaṇaḥ bhāgam ekam gṛhītvā tu nirgamam klapayet punar garbha sūtra samaḥ bhāgāt agratas mukhamaṇḍapaḥ etat sāmānyam uddiṣṭam prāsādasya hi lakṣaṇam liṅga mānam atho vakṣye pīṭhaḥ liṅga samaḥ bhavet dviguṇam śikharam proktam jaṅghāyāḥ ca eva śaunaka pīṭha garbha avaram karma tad mānena śuka aṅghrikam niḥ gamaḥ tu samākhyātaḥ śeṣam pūrvavat eva tu liṅga mānam smṛtam hi etat dvāra mānam atha ucyate kara agram veda vat kṛtvā dvāram bhāga aṣṭamam bhavet vistareṇa samākhyātam dviguṇam sva icchayā bhavet dvāra vat pīṭha madhye tu śeṣam suṣirakam bhavet pādikam śeṣikam bhittiḥ dvāra ardhena parigrahāt tad vistāra samā jaṅghā sikharam dviguṇam bhavet śuka aṅghriḥ pūrva vat jñeyā nirgama ucchrāyakam bhavet maṇḍape mānam etat tu svarūpam ca aparam vade traiva idam kārayet kṣetram yatra tiṣṭhanti devatāḥ nemiḥ pādena vistīrṇā prāsādasya samantataḥ garbham tu dviguṇam kuryāt nemyāḥ mānam bhavet iha prāsādānām ca vakṣyāmi mānam yonim ca mānataḥ vairājaḥ puṣpaka ākhyaḥ ca kailāsaḥ mālikā āhvayaḥ triviṣṭapam ca pañca ete prāsādāḥ sarva yonayaḥ vṛttaḥ vṛttāyataḥ ca anyaḥ aṣṭāśraḥ ca iha ca pañcamaḥ etebhyaḥ eva sambhūtāḥ prāsādāḥ su manoharāḥ meruḥ ca mandaraḥ ca eva vimānaḥ ca tathā aparaḥ nandivardhana saṃjñaḥ ca śrīvatsaḥ ca navā iti amī caturaśrāḥ samudbhūtāḥ vairājāt iti gamyatām valabhī gṛha rājaḥ ca śā lāgṛham ca mandiram uttambham śibikā veśma navā ete puṣpaka udbhavāḥ mukulī ca asya uṣṇīṣī śaṅkhaḥ ca kalaśaḥ tathā guvāvṛkṣaḥ tathā anyaḥ ca vṛttāḥ kailāsa sambhavāḥ gajaḥ atha vṛṣabhaḥ haṃsaḥ garuḍaḥ siṃha nāmakaḥ bhūmukhaḥ bhūdharaḥ ca eva śrījayaḥ pṛthivīdharaḥ vṛtta āyatāḥ samudbhūtāḥ navā ete maṇika āhvayāt vajram cakram tathā anyat ca muṣṭikam vabhru saṃjñitam vakraḥ svastika khaḍgau ca gadā śrīvṛkṣaḥ eva ca vijayaḥ nāmataḥ śvetaḥ triviṣṭipa samudbhavāḥ trikoṇam padmam ardhenduḥ catuṣkoṇam dvis aṣṭakam yatra tatra vidhātavyam saṃsthānam maṇḍapasya tu putra lābhaḥ striyaḥ puṣṭiḥ trikoṇa ādi kramāt bhavet kuryāt haja ādikam khyāta dvāri garbhagṛham tathā maṇāḍapaḥ sama saṃkhyābhiḥ guṇitaḥ sūtrakaḥ tathā maṇḍapasya caturtha aṃśāt bhadraḥ kāryaḥ vijānatā sārdha bhitti pramāṇena bhiti mānena vā punar bhitteḥ dvaiguṇyataḥ vā api kartavyāḥ maṇḍapāḥ kracid prāsāde mañcarī kāryā citrā viṣama bhūmikā parimāṇa virodhena rekhā vaiṣamya bhūṣitā ādhāraḥ tu catur dhāraḥ catur maṇḍapa śobhitaḥ śata śṛṅga samāyuktaḥ meruḥ prāsādaḥ uttamaḥ maṇḍapāḥ tasya kartavyāḥ bhadraiḥ tribhiḥ alaṅkṛtāḥ gha cana ākāra mānānām bhinna abhinnāḥ bhavanti te kiyantaḥ yeṣu ca ādhārāḥ nirādhārāḥ ca kecana anyonya asaṃkarāḥ teṣām ghaṭanānām abhedataḥ devatānām viśeṣāya prāsādāḥ bahavaḥ smṛtāḥ prāsāde niyamaḥ na asti devatānām svayambhuvām tān eva devatānām ca pūrva mānena kārayet caturaśra āyatāḥ tattra catuṣkoṇa samanvitāḥ candraśālā anvitā kāryā bherī śikhara saṃyutā puratas vāhanānām ca kartavyāḥ lagna maṇḍapāḥ nāṭya śālā ca kartavyā dvāra deśa samāśrayā prasāde devatānām ca kāryā dikṣu vidikṣu api dvārapālāḥ ca kartavyāḥ mukhyāḥ gatvā pṛthak pṛthak kiñcid adūrataḥ kāryāḥ maṭhāḥ tatra upajīvinām prāvṛtā jagatī kāryā phala puṣpa jala anvitā prasādeṣu surān sthāpya pūjābhiḥ pūjayet naraḥ vāsudevaḥ sarva devaḥ sarva bhāj tad gṛha ādi kṛt iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśe ācāra kāṇḍe prāsādaliṅgamaṇḍapādilakṣaṇanirūpaṇaṃnāma saptacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca pratiṣṭhām sarva devānām saṃkṣepeṇa vadāmi aham su tithi ādau su ramyām ca pratiṣṭhām kārayet guruḥ mantra nyāsam guruḥ kṛtvā tatas karma samārabhet prāsādasya agratas kuryāt maṇḍapam daśa hastakam kuryāt dvādaśa hastam vā stambhaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ yutam dhvaja aṣṭakaiḥ catur hastām madhye vedim ca kārayet vālukām tatra dāpayet caturaśram kārmuka ābham vartulam kamala ākṛti pūrva āditaḥ samārabhya kartavyam kuṇḍa pañcakam athavā caturaśrāṇi sarvāṇi etāni kārayet śiraḥ sthāne tu devasya ācāryaḥ homam ācaret aiśānyām kecid icchanti upalipya avanim śubhām dvārāṇi ca eva catvāri kṛtvā vai toraṇa antike nyagrodha udumbara aśvattha bailva pālāśa khādirāḥ toraṇāḥ pañca hastāḥ ca vastra puṣpa ādi alaṅkṛtāḥ pūrva dvāre mṛga indram tu haya rājam tu dakṣiṇe mantreṇa dakṣiṇasyām dvitīyakam agnāyāhi mantreṇa paścimasyām tṛtīyakam pūrve ambuda vat kāryā āgnoyyām dhūma rūpiṇī yāmyām vai kṛṣṇa rūpā tu śyāmalā bhavet vāruṇyām pāṇḍurā jñeyā vāyavyām pīta varṇikā uttare rakta varṇā tu śukla īśī ca patākikā ā agnim saṃsupti mantreṇa yamaḥ nāga iti dakṣiṇe tam īśānam atas ca eva viṣṇoḥ nukā iti madhyame vastra yugma samāyuktāḥ candana ādyaiḥ su alaṅkṛtāḥ puṣpaiḥ vitānaiḥ bahulaiḥ ādi varṇa abhimantritāḥ dikpālāḥ ca tatas pūjyāḥ śāstra dṛṣṭena karmaṇā asmin vṛkṣe ca eva pracārī iti parā smṛtā kiñca id adhātu ca saptamī imāḥ rudra iti dikyālān pūjayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ homa dravyāṇi vāyavye kuryāt sa upaskarāṇi ca śaṅkhān śāstra uditān śvetān netrābhyām vinyaset guruḥ ālokanena dravyāṇi śuddhim yānti na saṃśayaḥ tdṛdaya ādīni ca aṅgāni vyāhṛti praṇavena ca astram ca eva samastānām nyāsaḥ ayam sarvakāmikaḥ akṣatān viṣṭaram ca eva astreṇa eva abhimantritān viṣṭareṇa spṛśet duvyān yāga maṇḍapa saṃbhṛtān akṣatān vikiret paścāt astra pūtān samantataḥ śakrīm diśam atha ārabhya yāvat īśāna gocaram avakīrya akṣatārn saṃvān lepayet maṇḍapam tatas pratiṣṭhā yasya devasya tad ākhyam kalaśam nyaset aiśānyām pūjayet yāmye astreṇa eva ca bardhanīm kalaśam vardhanīm ca eva grahān vāsttoṣpatim tathā āsana itāni sarvāṇi praṇava ākhyam japet guruḥ sarva oṣadhī gandha liptam pūjayet kalaśam guruḥ vardhanyā tu samāyuktam kalaśam bhrāmayet anu ghaṭam ca āvāhya vāyavyām gaṇānām tvā iti sat gaṇam devam īśāna koṇe tu japet vāstoṣpatim budhaḥ vāstoṣpatī iti mantreṇa vāstu doṣa upaśāntaye paṭhet iti ca vidyāḥ ca kuryāt ālambhanam budhaḥ yogeyoga iti mantreṇa āstaraṇam śādvalaiḥ kuśaiḥ ṛtvigbhiḥ sārdham ācāryaḥ snāna pīṭhe guruḥ tadā kṛtvā brahma rathe devam pratiṣṭhanti tatas dvijāḥ aiśānyām ānayet pīṭha maṇḍape vinyaset guruḥ saṃsnāpya lakṣaṇa uddhāram kuryāt tūrya ādi dūra abhi vādanaiḥ madhu sarpiḥ samāyuktam kāṃsye vā tāmra bhājane akṣiṇī ca añjayet ca asya suvarṇasya śalākayā agniḥ jyotiḥ iti mantreṇa tu kārayet lakṣaṇe kriyamāṇe tu nāma ekam sthāpakaḥ imaṃmegaṅgemantreṇa netrayoḥ śītala kriyā bilva udumbaram aśvattham vaṭam pālāśam eva ca yajña ayajña iti mantreṇa dadyāt pañca kaṣāyakam sahadevī balā ca eva śatamūlī śatāvarī kumārī ca guḍūcī ca siṃhī vyāghrī tathā eva ca yā oṣadhī iti mantreṇa snānam oṣadhimat jalaiḥ yāḥ phalinī iti mantreṇa phala snānam vidhīyate ratnāni ca eva dhānyāni oṣadhīm śatapuṣpikām samudrān ca eva vinyasya caturaḥ caturaḥ diśaḥ kṣīram dadhi kṣīrodasya ghṛtodasya iti vā punar āpyāyasva dadhikrāvṇaḥ yāḥ auṣadhīḥ iti iti ca samudra ākhyaiḥ caturbhiḥ ca snāpayet kalaśaiḥ punar snātaḥ ca eva su veṣaḥ ca dhūpaḥ deyaḥ ca gugguluḥ pṛthivyām yāni tīrthāni saritaḥ sāgarāḥ tathā mantreṇa ānayet maṇḍapam śubham śambhavāya iti mantreṇa śayyāyām viniveśayet vastreṇa ācchādayitvā tu pūjanīyaḥ svabhāvataḥ yathāśāstram nivedyāni pāda mūle tu dāpayet kalaśam sa hiraṇyam ca śiraḥ sthāne nivedayet sthitvā kuṇḍa samīpe atha agneḥ sthāpanam ācaret śrīsūktam pāvamānyam ca vā āsadāmi a sa vājinam vṛṣākapim ca mitram bahu a caḥ pūrvatas japet rudram puruṣasūktam ca śloka adhyāyam ca śukriyam brahmāṇam pitṛ maitram ca adhvaryuḥ dakṣiṇe japet bheruṇḍāni ca sāmāni chandogaḥ paścime japet kuṇḍam ca astreṇa saṃprokṣya ācāryaḥ tu viśeṣataḥ tāmra pātre śarāve vā yathā vibhavataḥ api vā amṛtīkṛtya tam paścāt mantraiḥ sarvaiḥ ca deśikaḥ pātram gṛhya karābhyām ca kuṇḍam bhrāmya tatas punar dakṣiṇe sthāpayet brahma praṇītān ca uttareṇa tu sādhāraṇena mantreṇa sva sūtra vihitena vā dikṣu dikṣu tatas dadyāt paridhim viṣṭaraiḥ saha brahma viṣṇu hara īśānāḥ pūjyāḥ sādhāraṇena tu ācāryāḥ kecid icchanti jātakarma ādi anantaram pavitram tu tatas kṛtvā kuryāt ājyasya saṃskṛtim ācāryaḥ atha nirīkṣya api nīrājyam abhimantritam ājyabhāga abhighāra antam avekṣeta ājya siddhaye pañca pañca āhutīḥ hutvā ājyena tad anantaram garbhādhāna āditas tāvat yāvat gaudānikam bhavet tatas pūrṇāhutim dattvā pūrṇāt pūrṇam an ārethaḥ pūjayitvā tatas vahnim kuṇḍeṣu viharet tathā indra ādīnām sva mantraiḥ ca tathā āhuti śatam śatam purṇāhutim śatasya ante sarveṣām ca eva homayet svām āhutim atha ājyeṣu hotā tad kalaśe nyaset ātmānam ekatas kṛtvā tatas pūrṇām pradāpayet niṣkṛṣya bahis ācāryaḥ dikpālānām balim haret bhūtānām ca eva devānām nāgānām ca prayogataḥ ājyam tayoḥ sahakāri tat pradhānam yat aṅka (kṣa yoḥ jyeṣṭhasāma ca bhāruṇḍam tat nayāmi iti paścime evam madhye tathā pāde pūrṇāhutyā tathā punar śiraḥ sthāneṣu juhuyāt āviśet ca api anukramāt vedānām ādi mantraiḥ vā mantraiḥ vā deva nāmabhiḥ sva śāstra vihitaiḥ vā api gāyattryā vā atha te dvijāḥ gāyattryā vā athavā ācāryaḥ vyāhṛti praṇavena tu evam homa vidhim kṛtvā nyaset mantrān tu deśikaḥ caraṇau agnim īḍe tu gulphayoḥ sthitāḥ agne āyāhi jaṅghe dve śannodevī iti jānunī dīrgha āyuḥ tvāya hṛdaye śrīḥ ca te galake nyaset tathā mūrdhni ālagnāt homam ācaret veda puṇya aha śabdena prāsādānām pradakṣiṇam piṇḍikā ālaṃbhanam kṛtvā devasya tvā iti mantra vid dikpāḥ lān saha ratnaiḥ ca dhātūn oṣadhayaḥ tathā lauha bījāni siddhāni paścāt devam tu vinyaset īṣat madhyam parityajya tatas doṣa apaham tu tat tilasya tuṣa mātram tu uttaram kiñcid ānayet tattva varṇa kalā mātram prajāni bhuvana ātmaje pātram vastra yugam chatram tathā divya aṅgulīyakam ṛttvigbhyaḥ ca pradātavyā dakṣiṇā ca eva śaktitas caturthau juhuyāt paścāt yajamānaḥ samāhitaḥ āhutīnām śatam hutvā tatas pūrṇām pradāpayet niṣkramya bahis ācāryaḥ dikpālānām balim haret yāga ante kapilām dadyāt ācāryāya ca cāmaram mukuṭam kuṇḍalam chatram keyūram kaṭi sūtrakam vyajanam grāma vastra ādīn sa upaskāram su maṇḍapam bhojanam ca mahāt kuryāt kṛtakṛtyaḥ ca jāyate iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe devapratiṣṭhādinirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam iti pratiṣṭhā prakaraṇam samāptam sarga ādi kṛt hariḥ ca eva pūjyaḥ svāyambhuva ādibhiḥ vipra ādyaiḥ svena dharmeṇa tad dharmam vyāsa vai śṛṇu yajanam yājanam dānam brāhmaṇasya pratigrahaḥ adhyāpanam ca adhyayanam ṣaḍ karmāṇi dvijottame dānam adhyayanam yajñaḥ dharmaḥ kṣattriya vaiśyayoḥ daṇḍaḥ tasya kṛṣiḥ vaiśyasya śasyate śuśrūṣā eva dvijātīnām śūdrāṇām dharma sādhanam kāru karma pākayajñaḥ api dharmataḥ bhikṣā caryā atha śuśrūṣā guroḥ svādhyāyaḥ eva ca sandhyā karma agni kāryam ca dharmaḥ ayam brahmacāriṇaḥ sarveṣām āśramāṇām ca dvaividhyam tu caturvidham upakurvāṇakaḥ jñeyaḥ naiṣṭhikaḥ maraṇa antikaḥ agnayaḥ atithi śuśrūṣā yajñaḥ dānam sura arcanam udāsīnaḥ sādhakaḥ ca gṛhasthaḥ dvividhaḥ bhavet kuṭumba bharaṇe yuktaḥ sādhakaḥ asau gṛhī bhavet ṛṇāni trīṇi apākṛtya tyaktvā bhāryā dhana ādikam ekākī yaḥ tu vicaret udāsīnaḥ sa maukṣikaḥ bhūmau mūla phala āśi tvam svādhyāyaḥ tapaḥ eva ca saṃvibhāgaḥ yathānyāyam dharmaḥ ayam vana vāsinaḥ sa nyāsī sa hi vijñeyaḥ vānaprastha āśrame sthitaḥ jñānāya vartate bhukṣuḥ procyate pārameṣṭhikaḥ bhaikṣyam śrutam ca mauni tvam tapaḥ dhyānam viśeṣataḥ samyak ca jñāna vairāgyam dharmaḥ ayam bhikṣuke mataḥ karma sanyāsinaḥ kecid trividhaḥ pārameṣṭhikaḥ tṛtīyaḥ antya āśramī proktaḥ yoga mūrtim samāsthitaḥ prathamā bhāvanā pūrve mokṣe tu akṣa ra bhāvanā tṛtīye ca antimā proktā bhāvanā pārameśvarī dharmāt saṃjāyate mokṣaḥ hi arthāt kāmaḥ abhijāyate jñānam pūrvam nivṛttam syāt pravṛttam ca agni deva kṛt kṣamā damaḥ dayā dānam alobhāḥ abhyāsaḥ eva ca ārjavam ca ansūyā ca tīrtha anusaraṇam tathā satyam saṃtoṣaḥ āstikyam tathā ca indriya nigrahaḥ devatā abhyarcanam pūjā brāhmaṇānām viśeṣataḥ ahiṃsā priya vādi tvam apaiśunyam arūkṣa tā ete āśramikāḥ dharmāḥ caturvarṇyam bavīmi atas prājāpatyam brāhmaṇānām smṛtam sthānam kriyāvatām sthānam aindram kṣattriyāṇām saṃgrāmeṣu apalāyinām vaiśyānām mārutam sthānam gāndharvam śūdra jātīnām paricāre ca vartatām aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇām ṛṣīṇām ūrdhvaretasām smṛtam teṣām tu yat sthānam tat eva vana vāsinām saptarṣīṇām tu yat sthānam sthānam tat vai vanaukasām yatīnām yata cittānām nyāsinām ūrdhvaretasām ānandam brahma tat sthānam yasmāt na āvartate muniḥ yoginām amṛta sthānam vyoma ākhyam parama akṣaram ānandam aiśvaram yasmāt muktaḥ na āvartate naraḥ muktiḥ aṣṭa aṅga vijñānāt saṃkṣepāt tat vade śṛṇu yamāḥ pañca tu ahiṃsā ādyāḥ ahiṃsā prāṇi ahiṃsanam satyam bhūta hitam vākyam asteyam sva agraham param niyamāḥ pañca satya ādyāḥ bāhmam ābhyantaram dvidhā śaucam tuṣṭiḥ ca santoṣaḥ tapaḥ ca indriya nigrahaḥ svādhyāyaḥ syāt mantra jāpaḥ praṇidhānam hareḥ yajiḥ āsanam padmaka ādi uktam prāṇāyāmaḥ marut jayaḥ evam dvidhā tridhā api uktam puraṇāt pūrakaḥ sa ca laghuḥ dvādaśa mātraḥ syāt caturviṃśatikaḥ paraḥ ṣaṭtriṃśat mātrikaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ pratyāhāraḥ ca rodhanam brahma ātma cintā dhyānam syāt dhāraṇā manasaḥ dhṛtiḥ aham brahma iti avasthānam samādhiḥ
