brahmaṇaḥ sthitiḥ aham ātmā param brahma satyam jñānam anantakam yaḥ asau āditya puruṣaḥ saḥ asau aham akhaṇḍitam iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe varṇāśramadharmanirūpaṇam nāma ekonapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam ahani ahani yaḥ kuryāt kriyām sa jñānam āpnuyāt uṣaḥ kāle tu saṃprāpte kṛtvā ca āvaśyakam budhaḥ strāyāt nadīṣu śuddhāsu śaucam kṛtvā yathāvidhi pratas snānena pūyante ye api pāpa kṛtaḥ janāḥ prātar snānam praśaṃsanti hi tat sukhāt suptasya satatam lālā ādyāḥ saṃstravanti hi atas na eva ācaret karmāṇi a kṛtvā snānam āditas alakṣmīḥ kālakarṇo ca dus svapnam durvicintitam pratas snānena pāpāni dhūyante na atra saṃśayaḥ na ca snānam vinā puṃsām prāśastyam karma saṃsmṛtam home japye viśeṣeṇa tasmāt snānam samācaret aśaktau aśiraskam tu snānam asya vidhīyate ārdreṇa vāsasā vā api mārjanam kāyikam smṛtam brāhmam āgneyam uddiṣṭam vāyavyam divyam eva ca vāruṇam yaugikam tadvat ṣaṣ aṅgam snānam ācaret brāhmam tu mārjanam mantraiḥ kuśaiḥ sa udaka bindubhiḥ āgreyam bhasmanā a pāda mastakāt deha dhūnanam gavām hi rajasā proktam vāyavyam snānam uttamam vāruṇam ca avagāham ca tu ātma vedanam ātmatīrtham iti khyātam sevitam brahma vādibhiḥ kṣīravṛkṣa samudbhūtam mālatī sambhavam śubham apāmārgam ca vilvam ca karavīram ca dhāvane udak mukhaḥ prāc mukhaḥ vā bhakṣayet dantadhāvanam prakṣālya bhuktvā tat jahyāt śucau deśe samāhitaḥ snātvā santarpayet devān ṛṣīn pitṛ gaṇān tathā saṃmārjya mantraiḥ rātmānam kuśaiḥ sa udaka bindubhaiḥ āpohiṣṭhā vyāhṛtibhiḥ sāvitryā vāruṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ oṅkāra vyāhṛti yutām gāyattrīm vedamātaram japtvā jala añjalim dadyāt bhāraskaram prati tad manāḥ prāc kūleṣu tatas sthitvā darbheṣu su samāhitaḥ prāṇāyāmam tatas kṛtvā dhyāyet sandhyām iti śrutiḥ yā sandhyā sā jagat sūtiḥ māyā atītā hi niṣkalā dhyātvā raktām sitām kṛṣṇām gāyattrīm vai japet vudhaḥ prāc mukhaḥ satatam vipraḥ sandhyā upāsanam ācaret an anya cetasaḥ santaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vedapāragāḥ upāsya vidhivat sandhyām prāptāḥ pūrva parām gatim vihāya sandhyā praṇatim sa yāti naraka ayutam sahasra paramām nityām śata madhyām daśa avarām gāyattrīm vai japet vidvān prāc mukhaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ atha upatiṣṭhet ādityam udaya stham samāhitaḥ mantraiḥ tu vividhaiḥ sauraiḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma saṃjñitaiḥ kurvīta praṇatim bhūmau mūrdhānam abhimantritaḥ om khakholkāya śāntāya kāraṇa traya hetave nivedayāmi ca ātmānam namaḥ te jñāna rūpiṇe bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar tvam oṅkāraḥ sarvaḥ rudraḥ sanātanaḥ atha āgamya gṛham vipraḥ (paścāt samācamya yathāvidhi ṛtvij putraḥ atha patnī vā śiṣyaḥ vā api sahodaraḥ prāpya anujñām viśeṣeṇa juhuyāt vā yathāvidhi gurum ca eva api upāsīta hitam ca asya samācaret veda abhyāsam tatas kuryāt prayatnāt śaktitaḥ dvijaḥ avekṣeta ca śāstrāṇi dharma ādīni dvijottamaḥ vaidikān ca eva nigamān vedāṅgāni ca sarvaśas upayāt īśvaram ca eva yogakṣema prāsiddhaye sādhayet vividhān arthān kuṭumba artham tatas dvijaḥ tatas madhyāhna samaye snāna artham mṛdam āharet puṣpa akṣatān tila kuśān gomayam śuddham eva ca nadīṣu devakhāteṣu taḍāgeṣu saraḥ su ca pañca piṇḍān an uddhṛtya snānam duṣyanti nityaśas mṛdā ekayā śiraḥ kṣālyam dvābhyām nābheḥ tathā upari adhas ca tisṛbhiḥ kṣālyam pādau ṣaṭbhiḥ tathā eva ca mṛttikā ca samuddiṣṭā gomayasya pramāṇam tu tena aṅgam lepayet tatas prakṣālya ācamya vidhivat tatas snāyāt samāhitaḥ abhimantrya jalam mantraiḥ āliṅgaiḥ vāruṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ tnāna kāle smaret viṣṇamā apaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ yatas prekṣya oṅkāram ādityam tris nimajjet jalāśaye ācāntaḥ punar ācāmet mantreṇa anena mantra vid antar carasi bhūteṣu guhāyām viśvatomukhaḥ tvam yajñaḥ tvam vaṣaṭkāraḥ āpaḥ jyotiḥ rasaḥ amṛtam drupadām vā tris abhyasyet dyāhṛti praṇava anvitām sāvitrīm vā jape dvidvān tathā ca eva aghamarṣaṇam tatas saṃmārjanam kuryāt āpohiṣṭhā mayobhuvaḥ drupadām vā atha sāvitrarim tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam apaḥ pāṇau samādāya japtvā vai mārjane kṛte atha upatiṣṭhet ādityam ūrdhva puṣpa anvita añjalim haṃsaḥ śuciṣad etena sāvitryā ca viśeṣataḥ mantrān ca vividhān paścāt prāc kūle ca tiṣṭhan ca vīkṣyamāṇaḥ urakam japam kuryāt samāhitaḥ sphaṭika abja akṣa rudrākṣaiḥ putrajīva samudbhavaiḥ kartavyā syāt antarā tatra sā smṛtā anyathā ca śucau bhūmyām darbheṣu ca samāhitaḥ pradakṣiṇam samāvṛtya namaskṛtya tatas kṣitau ācamya ca yathāśāstram śaktyā svādhyāyam ācaret tatas santarpayet devān ṛṣīn pitṛ gaṇān tathā ādau oṅkāram uccārya namaḥ ante tarpayāmi ca devān brahma ṛṣīn ca eva tarpayet akṣata udakaiḥ pitṝn devān munīn bhaktyā sva sūtra ukta vidhānataḥ deva ṛṣoṃ tarpayet dhīmān udaka añjalibhiḥ yajña upavītī devānām nivītī ṛṣi tarpaṇe prācīnāvītī pitrye tu tena tīrthena bhārata niṣpīḍya snāna vastram vai samācamya ca vāgyataḥ brahmāṇam śaṅkaram sūryam tathā eva madhusūdanam anyān ca abhimatān devān bhaktyā ca akrodhanaḥ hara pradadyāt vā atha puṣpa ādi sūktena puruṣeṇa tu āpaḥ vā devatāḥ sarvāḥ tena samyak samarcitāḥ dhyātvā praṇava pūrvam vai devam vāri samāhitaḥ namaskāreṇa puṣāpāṇi vinyaset vai pṛthak pṛthak tat viṣṇoḥ iti mantreṇa sūktena puruṣeṇa tu tadā adhyātma manāḥ śāntaḥ tat viṣṇoḥ iti mantrataḥ devayajñam pitṛyajñam tathā eva ca mānuṣam brahmayajñam ca pañca yajñān samācaret yadi syāt tarpaṇāt arvāk brahma yajñam kutas bhavet kṛtvā manuṣyayajñam vai tatas svādhyāyam ācaret bhūta yajñaḥ sa vai jñeyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ yaḥ tu ayam baliḥ ekam tu bhojayet vipram pitṝn uddiśya sattamāḥ nitya śrāddham tat uddiśya pitṛ yajñaḥ gati pradaḥ uddhṛtya vā yathāśakti kiñcid annam samāhitaḥ manaḥ vāc karmabhiḥ śāntam svāgataiḥ sva gṛham tatas bhikṣām āhuḥ grāsa mātram annam tat syāt caturguṇam abhyāgatān yathāśakti pūjayet atithim tathā bhikṣām vai bhikṣave dadyāt vidhivat brahyacāriṇe a kṛtvā tu dvijaḥ pañca mahāyajñān dvijottamaḥ veda abhyāsaḥ anvaham śaktyā mahāyajña kriyā kṣamāḥ nāśayanti āśu pāpāni devānām arcanam tathā yaḥ mohāt atha vā ālasyāt a kṛtvā devatā arcanam bhuṅkte sa yāti narakān sūṃkareṣu eva jāyate aśaucam saṃpravakṣyāmi aśuciḥ pātakī sadā aśaucam ca eva saṃsargāt śuddhiḥ saṃsarga varjanāt daśa aham prāhuḥ āśaucam sarve viprāḥ vipaścitaḥ mṛteṣu vā atha jāteṣu brāhmaṇānām dvijottama ā danta jananāt sadyas ācūḍāt eka rātrakam kṣattriyaḥ dvādaśahena daśabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ viśaḥ śudhyet māsena vai śūdraḥ yatīnām na asti pātakam iti gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe nityakarmāśaucayornirūpaṇam nāma pañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam arthānām ucite pātre śraddhayā pratipādanam adhyāpanam yājanam ca vṛttam āhuḥ pratigraham kusīdam kṛṣi vāṇijyam kṣattra vṛttaḥ atha varjayet nityam naimittikam kāmyam vimalam dānam īritam an uddiśya phalam tasmāt brāhmaṇāya tu nityaśas yat tu pāpa upaśāntyai ca dīyate vidupām kare naimittikam tat uddiṣṭan dānam sadbhiḥ anuṣṭhitam dānam tat kāmyam ākhyātam ṛṣibhiḥ dharma acintakaiḥ īśvara prīṇana arthāya ikṣubhiḥ santatām bhumim yava godhūma śālinīm bhūmi dānāt param dānam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati vidyām dattvā brāhmaṇāya brahma loke mahīyate dadyāt aharahar tāḥ tu śraddhayā brahmacāriṇe vaiśākhyām paurṇamāsyām tu brāhmaṇān sapta pañca ca upoṣya abhyarcayet vidvān madhunā tila sarpiṣā yāvajjīvam kṛtam pāpam tat kṣaṇāt eva naśyati kṛṣṇājine tilān kṛtvā hiraṇya madhu sarpiṣā ghṛta annam udakam ca eva vaiśākhyām ca viśeṣataḥ dvādaśyām arcayet viṣṇum upoṣya agha praṇāśanam yaḥ hi yām devatām icchet samārādhayitum naraḥ brāhmaṇān pūjayet datnāt bhojayet yoṣitaḥ surān ārogya kāmaḥ atha ravim dhana kāmaḥ hutāśanam karmaṇām siddhi kāmaḥ tu pūjayet vai vināyakam bhoga kāmaḥ hi śaśinam bala kāmaḥ samīraṇam akāmaḥ sarva kāmaḥ vā pūjayet tu gadādharam tila pradaḥ prajām iṣṭām dīpa daḥ cakṣuḥ uttamam bhūmi daḥ sarvam āpnoti dīrgham āyuḥ hiraṇya daḥ gṛha daḥ agryāṇi veśmāni rūpya daḥ rūpam uttamam vāsaḥ daḥ cāndra sālokyam aśvi sālokyam aśva daḥ anaḍuh daḥ śriyam puṣṭām go daḥ bradhnasya viṣṭapam yāna śayyā pradaḥ bhāryām aiśvaryam abhaya pradaḥ dhānya daḥ śāvatam saukhyam brahma daḥ brahma śāśvatam gavām ghāsa pradānena sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate indhanānām pradānena dīpta agniḥ jāyate naraḥ auṣadham sneham āhāram rogi roga praśāntaye asipatravanam mārgam kṣura dhārā samanvitam tīkṣṇā tapam ca tarati chatra upānah pradaḥ naraḥ yat yat iṣṭatamam loke yat ca asya dayitam gṛhe saṃkrānti ādiṣu kāleṣu dattam bhavati ca akṣayam prayāga ādiṣu tīrtheṣu gayāyām ca viśeṣataḥ dāna dharmāt paraḥ dharmaḥ bhūtānām na he vidyate svarga āyuḥ bhūti kāmena dānam pāpa upaśāntaye dīyamānam tu yaḥ mohāt go vipra agni sureṣu ca nivārayati pāpa ātmā tiryagyonim vrajet naraḥ mriyamāṇeṣu vipreṣu brahma hā sa tu garhitaḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe dānadharmanirūpaṇam nāma ekapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam atas param pravakṣyāmi prāyaścitta vidhim dvijāḥ pañca pātakinaḥ tu ete tad saṃyogī ca pañcamaḥ upapāpāni gohatyā prabhṛtīni surāḥ jaguḥ brahma hā dvādaśa abdāni kuṭīm kṛtvā vane vaset kuryāt anaśanam vā atha bhṛgoḥ patanam eva ca jvalantam vā viśet agnim jalam vā praviśet svayam brāhmaṇa arthe gavā arthe vā samyak prāṇān parityajet aśvamedha avabhṛthake snātvā vā mucyate dvijaḥ sarva svam vā veda vide brāhmaṇāya pradāpayet sarasvatyāḥ taraṅgiṇyāḥ saṅgame loka viśrute śuddhe triṣavaṇa snātaḥ tri rātra upoṣitaḥ dvijaḥ kapālamocane snātvā vārāṇasyām tathā eva ca surāpaḥ tu surām pītvā agni varṇām dvijottamaḥ payaḥ ghṛtam vā go mūtram tasmāt pāpāt pramucyate suvarṇa steyī muktaḥ syāt musalena hataḥ nṛpaiḥ guru bhāryām samāruhya brāhmaṇaḥ kāma mohitaḥ avagūhet striyam taptām dīptām kārṣṇāyasīm kṛtām cāndrāyaṇāni vā kuryāt pañca catvāri vā punar cāndrāyaṇam ca vidhinā kṛtam ca eva atikṛcchrakam puṇya kṣetre gayā ādau ca gamanam pāpa nāśanam amāvasyām tithim prāpya yaḥ samārādhayet bhavam upoṣitaḥ caturdaśyām kṛṣṇa pakṣe samāhitaḥ yamāya dharmarājāya mṛtyave ca antakāya ca vaivasvatāya kālāya sarva bhūta kṣayāya ca pratyekam tila saṃyuktān dadyāt sapta jala añjalīn snātvā nadyām tu pūrvāhne mucyate sarva pātakaiḥ vrateṣu eteṣu kurvīta śāntaḥ saṃyata mānasaḥ paṣṭhyām upoṣitaḥ devam śukla pakṣe samāhitaḥ ekādaśyām nirāhāraḥ samabhyarcya janārdanam dvādaśyām śukla pakṣasya mahā pāpaiḥ pramucyate grahaṇa ādiṣu kāleṣu mahāpātaka nāśanam yaḥ sarva pāpa yuktaḥ api puṇya tīrtheṣu mānavaḥ brahma ghnam vā kṛtaghnam vā mahāpātaka dūṣitam bhartāram uddharet nārī praviṣṭā saha pāvakam pativratā tu yā nārī bhartuḥ śuśrūṣaṇa utsukā tathā rāmasya subhagā sītā trailokya viśrutā patnī dāśaratheḥ devī vijigye rākṣaseśvaram phalgutīrtha ādiṣu snātaḥ sarva ācāra phalam labhet iti āha bhagavān viṣṇuḥ purā mama yata vratāḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe prāyaścittanirūpaṇam nāma dvipañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca evam brahmā abravīt śrutvā hareḥ aṣṭa nidhīn tathā mukunda kundau nīlaḥ ca śaṅkhaḥ ca eva aparaḥ nidhiḥ dākṣiṇya sāraḥ puruṣaḥ suvarṇa ādika saṃgraham mahāpadma aṅkitaḥ dadyāt dhana ādyam dhārmikāya ca nīdhī padma mahāpadmau sāttvikau puruṣau smṛtī makareṇa aṅkitaḥ khaḍga bāṇa kunta ādi saṃgrahī dadyāt śrutāya maitrīm ca yāti nityam ca rājabhiḥ dravya artham śatruṇā nāśam saṃgrāme ca api saṃvrajet nidhānam urvyām kurute nidhiḥ saḥ api eka pūruṣaḥ rājasena mukundena lakṣitā rājya saṃgrahī ca aṅkitaḥ sattva tejasā saṃyutaḥ bhavet vastra dhānya ādi saṃgrāhī taḍāga ādi karoti ca nidhiḥ ca eva āmra ārāma ādi kārayet ekasya syāt nidhiḥ śaṅkhaḥ svayam bhuṅkte dhana ādi sva poṣaṇa paraḥ śaṅkhī dadyāt para nare vṛthā miśra avalokanāt miśra svabhāva phala dāyinaḥ nidhīnām rūpam uktam tu hariṇā api hara ādike iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe navanidhivarṇanam nāma tripañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam agnīdhraḥ ca agnibāhuḥ ca bapuṣmān dhyutimān tathā jyotiṣmān daśamaḥ jātaḥ putrāḥ hi ete priyavratāt medha agnibāhu putrāḥ tu trayaḥ yoga parāyaṇāḥ jātismarāḥ mahābhāgāḥ nairājyāya vibhajya sapta dvīpāni saptānām pradadau nṛpaḥ yojanānām pramāṇena pañcāśat koṭiḥ āplutā jambū plakṣa āhvayau dvīpau śālmalaḥ ca aparaḥ hara kuśaḥ krauñcaḥ tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraḥ ca eva saptamaḥ ete dvīpāḥ samudraiḥ tu sapta saptabhiḥ āvṛtāḥ dvīpāt tu dviguṇaḥ dvīpaḥ samudraḥ ca vṛṣadhvaja praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśa adhastāt dvatriṃśat mūrdhni vistṛtaḥ adhas ṣoḍaśa sāhasraḥ karṇikā ākāra saṃsyitaḥ himavān hemakūṭaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ ca asya dakṣiṇe nīlaḥ śvetaḥ ca śṛṅgī ca uttare varṣaparvatāḥ plakṣa ādiṣu narāḥ rudra ye vasanti sanātanāḥ śaṅkara atha na teṣu asti yuga avasthā kathañcana jambūdvīpa īśvarāt putrāḥ hi agrīdhnāt abhavat nava nābhiḥ kiṃpuruṣaḥ ca eva harivarṣam ilā vṛtaḥ ketumālaḥ nṛpaḥ tebhyaḥ tad saṃjñān khaṇḍakān dadau nābheḥ tu merudevyām tu putraḥ abhūt ṛṣabhaḥ hara indradyumnaḥ ca tad putraḥ parameṣṭhī tatas smṛtaḥ pratīhāraḥ ca tad putraḥ pratihartā tad ātmajaḥ tatas dhīmān mahā tejāḥ bhauvanaḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ tvaṣṭā tvaṣṭuḥ ca virajāḥ rajaḥ tasya api abhūt sutaḥ iti śrā gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe bhuvanakośavarṇanopayogipriyavratavaṃśanirūpaṇam nāma catuḥ pañcaśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam madhye tu ilāvṛtaḥ varṣaḥ bhadrāśvaḥ pūrvatas adbhutaḥ varṣaḥ hiraṇvān vṛṣabhadhvaja tatas kimpuruṣaḥ varṣaḥ meroḥ dakṣiṇatas smṛtaḥ bhārataḥ dakṣiṇe proktaḥ hariḥ dakṣiṇa pāścime uttare ca kuroḥ varṣaḥ kalpavṛkṣa samāvṛtaḥ indradvīpaḥ kaśerumān tāmravarṇaḥ nāgadvīpaḥ kaṭāhaḥ ca siṃhalaḥ vāruṇaḥ tathā ayam tu navamaḥ teṣām dvīpaḥ sāgara saṃvṛtaḥ pūrve kirātāḥ tasyāḥ te paścime yavanāḥ sthitāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣattriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ sūdrāḥ ca antara vāsinaḥ mahendraḥ malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimān ṛkṣa parvataḥ vindhyaḥ ca pāriyātraḥ ca sapta atra kulaparvatāḥ vedasmṛtiḥ narmadā ca varadā surasā śivā tāpī payoṣṇī sarayūḥ kāverī gomatī tathā godāvarī bhīmarathī kṛṣṇaveṇī mahā nadī ketumālā tāmraparṇā candrabhāgā sarasvatī ṛṣikulyā ca kāverī mattagaṅgā payasvinī vidarbhā ca śatadrūḥ ca nadyaḥ pāpa harāḥ śubhāḥ āsām pibanti salilam madhyadeśa ādayaḥ janāḥ pāñcālāḥ kuravaḥ matsyāḥ yaudheyāḥ sa paṭaccarāḥ kuntayaḥ śūrasenāḥ ca madhyadeśa janāḥ smṛtāḥ vṛṣadhvaja janāḥ pādmāḥ sūta māgadha cedayaḥ kāśayaḥ ca videhāḥ ca pūrvasyām kosalāḥ tathā kaliṅga vaṅga puṇḍra aṅgāḥ vaidarbhāḥ mūlakāḥ tathā vindhya antar nilayāḥ deśāḥ pūrva dakṣiṇatas smṛtāḥ pulanda aśmaka jīmūta naya rāṣṭra nivāsinaḥ dakṣiṇāpatha vāsinaḥ ambaṣṭha draviḍāḥ lāṭāḥ kāmbhojāḥ strīmukhāḥ śakāḥ ānarta vāsinaḥ ca eva jñeyāḥ yakṣiṇa paścime strī rājyāḥ saindhavāḥ mlecchāḥ na asti kāḥ yavanāḥ tathā paścimena ca vijñeyāḥ māthurāḥ naiṣadhaiḥ saha māṇḍavyāḥ ca tuṣārāḥ ca mūlika aśvamukhāḥ khaśāḥ mahākeśāḥ mahānāsāḥ deśāḥ tu uttara paścime lamba stana nāgāḥ ca mādra gāndhāra bāhlikāḥ himācala ālayāḥ mlecchāḥ udīcīm diśam āśritāḥ brahmaputrāḥ sa ṭaṅkaṇāḥ abhīṣāhāḥ sa kāśmīrāḥ udak parveṇa kīrtitāḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe bhuvanakośavarṇanam nāma pañcapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sapta medhātitheḥ putrāḥ plakṣadvīpa īśvarasya ca jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhavaḥ nāma śiśiraḥ tad antaraḥ dhruvaḥ ca saptamaḥ teṣām plakṣadvīpa īśvarāḥ hi te somakaḥ sumanāḥ śailaḥ baibhrājaḥ ca atra saptamaḥ anutaptā śikhī ca eva vipāśā tridivā kramuḥ amṛtā sukṛtā ca eva saptā etāḥ tatra nimnagāḥ vapuṣmān śālmalasya īśaḥ tad sutāḥ varṣa nāmakāḥ yonitoyā vitṛṣṇā ca candrā śukla vimocanī vidhṛtiḥ saptamī tāsām smṛtāḥ pāpa praśānti dāḥ jyotiṣmataḥ kuśadvīpe sapta putrāḥ vidrumaḥ hemaśailaḥ ca dyutimān puṣpavān tathā dhūta pāpā śivā ca eva pavitrā sanmatiḥ tathā vidyudabhrā mahī ca anyā sarva pāpa harāḥ tu imāḥ krauñcadvīpe dyutimataḥ putrāḥ sapta mahātmanaḥ kuśalaḥ mandagaḥ ca uṣṇaḥ pīvaraḥ atha undhakārakaḥ krauñcaḥ ca vāmanaḥ ca eva tṛtīyaḥ ca andha kārakaḥ divāvṛt pañcamaḥ ca anyaḥ dundubhiḥ puṇḍarīkavān khyātiḥ ca puṇḍarīkā ca saptā etāḥ varṣa nimnagāḥ śākadvīpa īśvarāt bhavyāt sapta putrāḥ prajajñire jaladaḥ ca kumāraḥ ca sukumāra ūruṇī bakaḥ kusumodaḥ samodārkiḥ saptamaḥ ca mahādrumaḥ sukumārī kumārī ca nalinī dhenukā ca yā ikṣuḥ ca veṇukā ca eva gabhastī saptamī tathā śabalāt puṣkara īśāt ca mahāvīraḥ ca dhātakiḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi ūrdhvam pañcāśat ucchritaḥ tāvat ca eva ca vistīrṇaḥ sarvatas parimaṇḍalaḥ svādu udakena udadhinā puṣkaraḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ svādu udakasya puratas dṛśyate loka saṃsthitiḥ dviguṇā kāñcanī bhūmiḥ sarva jantu vivarjitā lokālokaḥ tatas śailaḥ yojana ayuta avistṛtaḥ tamasā parvataḥ vyāptaḥ tamaḥ api aṇḍa kaṭāhataḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe bhuvanakośavarṇanam nāma ṣaṭpañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam daśa sāhasram ekaikam pātālam vṛṣabhadhvaja mahā ākhyam sutalam ca agryam pātālam ca api saptamam kṛṣṇā śuklā aruṇā pītā śarkarā śailakāñcanā raudre tu puṣkaradvīpe narakāḥ santi tān śṛṇu rudhira ākhyaḥ vaitaraṇī kṛmiśaḥ kṛmibhaḥ janaḥ asipatravanaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ nānā bhakṣaḥ ca dāruṇaḥ tathā pūyavahaḥ pāpaḥ vahnijvālaḥ tu adhas sirāḥ saṃdaṃśaḥ kṛṣṇasūtraḥ ca tamaḥ ca avīciḥ eva ca śvabhojanaḥ atha apratiṣṭha uṣṇavīciḥ narakāḥ smṛtāḥ pāpinaḥ teṣu pacyante viṣa śastra agni dāyinaḥ upari upari vai lokāḥ rudra bhūta ādayaḥ sthitāḥ vāri vahni anila ākāśaiḥ vṛtam bhūtādinā ca tat tat aṇḍam mahatā rudra pradhānena ca veṣṭitam aṇḍam daśaguṇam vyāptam nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ iti gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe bhuvanakośagatāpātalanarakādinirūpaṇam nāma saptapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam vakṣye pramāṇa saṃsthāne sūrya ādīnām śṛṇuṣva me yojānānām sahasrāṇi bhāskarasya rathaḥ nava īṣā daṇḍaḥ tathā eva asya dviguṇaḥ vṛṣabhadhvaja yojanānām tu tasya akṣaḥ tatra cakram pratiṣṭhitam tri nābhimati pañca āre ṣaṣ nemini akṣaya ātmake saṃvatsara maye kṛtsnam kālacakram pratiṣṭhitam catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi dvitīyaḥ akṣaḥ vivasvataḥ pañca anyāni tu sārdhāni syandanasya vṛṣadhvaja akṣa pramāṇam ubhayoḥ pramāṇam tu yuga ardhayoḥ dvitīye akṣe tu tat cakram saṃsthitam mānasa acale gāyattrī sa bṛhatī uṣṇih jagatī triṣṭubh eva ca anuṣṭubh paṅktiḥ iti uktāḥ chandāṃsi harayaḥ raveḥ aryamā pulahaḥ ca eva rathojāḥ puñjikasthalā prahetiḥ kacchanīraḥ ca nāradaḥ ca eva mādhave hāhā rathasvanaḥ ca eva jyeṣṭhe bhānoḥ rathe sthitāḥ varuṇaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ rambhā sahajanyā kuhūḥ budhaḥ rathacitraḥ tathā śukraḥ vasanti āṣāḍha saṃjñite indraḥ viśvāvasuḥ srota śrotraḥ elāpatraḥ tathā aṅgirāḥ vivasvān ugrasenaḥ ca bhṛguḥ āpūraṇaḥ tathā anumlocā śaṅkhapālau vyāghraḥ bhādrapade pūṣā ca suruciḥ dhātā gautamaḥ atha dhanañjayaḥ suṣeṇaḥ anyaḥ dhṛtācī ca vasanti āśvayuje ravau viśvācī senajit cāpaḥ kārtike ca adhikāriṇaḥ aṃśuḥ ca kāśyapaḥ tārkṣyaḥ mahāpadmaḥ tathā urvaśī citrasenaḥ tathā vidyut mārgaśīrṣa adhikāriṇaḥ ariṣṭanemiḥ ca eva anyā brahmāpetaḥ atha ṛtajit dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ca saptamaḥ viṣṇuḥ aśvataraḥ rambhā sūryavarcāḥ ca satyajit viśvāmitraḥ tathā rakṣaḥ yajñāpetaḥ hi phālgune savituḥ maṇḍale brahman viṣṇu śakti upabṛṃhitāḥ nṛtyantyaḥ apsarasaḥ yānti sūryasya anu niśācarāḥ vahanti pannagāḥ yakṣaiḥ kriyate abhīṣu saṃgrahaḥ piśaṅgeḥ turagaiḥ yuktaḥ saḥ aṣṭābhiḥ vāyu vegibhiḥ sa upāsaṃga patākaḥ tu śukrasya api rathaḥ mahān aṣṭa aśvaḥ kāñcanaḥ śrīmān bhaumasya api rathaḥ mahān padmarāga aruṇaiḥ aśvaiḥ saṃyuktaḥ vahni saṃbhavaiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ pāṇḍaraiḥ yuktaiḥ vājibhiḥ kāñcane rathe tiṣṭhan tiṣṭhati varṣam vai rāśau rāśau bṛhaspatiḥ ākāśa sambhavaiḥ aśvaiḥ śavalaiḥ syandanam yutam samāruhya śanais yāti manda gāmī śanaiścaraḥ svarbhānoḥ turagāḥ hi aṣṭau bhṛṅga ābhāḥ dhūsaram ratham sakṛt yaktāḥ tu bhūteśa bahanti aviratam śiva tathā ketu rathasya aśvāḥ aṣṭau te vāta raṃhasaḥ palāla dhūma varṇa ābhāḥ lākṣā rasa nibha aruṇāḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe bhuvanakośanirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam atha jyotiḥ śāstram sūtaḥ uvāca jyotiḥ cakram bhuvaḥ mānam uktvā provāca keśavaḥ catur lakṣam jyotiṣasya sāram rudrāya sarva daḥ kṛttikāḥ tu agni devatyāḥ rohiṇyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ilvalāḥ soma devatyāḥ raudram ca ārdram udāhṛtam aśleṣāḥ sarpa devatyāḥ maghāḥ ca pitṛ devatāḥ sāvitraḥ ca tathā hastā citrā tvaṣṭā prakīrtitaḥ svātī ca vāyu devatyā nakṣatram parikīrtitam indra agni devatā proktā viśākhā vṛṣabhadhvaja maitram ṛkṣam anūrādhā jyeṣṭhā śākram prakīrtitam tathā nirṛti devatyaḥ mūlaḥ tad jñaiḥ udāhṛtaḥ āpyāḥ tu āṣāṭhapūrvāḥ tu uttarāḥ vaiśvadevatāḥ brāhmaḥ ca eva abhijit proktaḥ śravaṇāḥ vaiṣṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ vāsavaḥ tu tathā ṛkṣam dhaniṣṭhā procyate budhaiḥ tathā śatabhiṣā proktam nakṣatram vāruṇam śiva ājam bhādrapadā pūrvā ahirbrudhnyaḥ tathā uttarā pauṣṇam ca revatī ṛkṣam aśvayuj ca aśva daivatam bharaṇī ṛkṣam tathā yāmyam proktāḥ te ṛkṣa devatāḥ brahmāṇī saṃsthitā pūrve pritapat navamī tithau māheśvarī ca uttare ca dvitīyā daśāmī tithau pañcamyām ca trayodaśyām vārāhī dakṣiṇe sthitā ṣaṣṭhyām ca eva caturdaśyām indrāṇī paścime sthitā saptamyām paurṇamāsyām ca cāmuṇḍāḥ vāyugocare aṣṭamī amāvāsyā yoge mahālakṣmīśa gocare ekādaśyām tṛtīyāyām agnikoṇe tu vaiṣṇavī dvādaśyām ca caturthyām tu kaumārī nairṛte tathā puṣyā hastā tathā jyeṣṭhā prasthāne śreṣṭham ucyate hasta ādi pañca ṛkṣāṇi uttarā trayam eva ca aśvinī rohiṇī puṣyā dhaniṣṭhā ca punarvasū vastra prāvaraṇe śreṣṭhaḥ nakṣatrāṇām gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ kṛttikā bharaṇī aśleṣāḥ maghāḥ mūla viśākhayoḥ trīṇi pūrvā tathā ca eva adhovakrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ eṣu vāpī taḍāga ādi kūpa bhūmi tṛṇāni ca devāgārasya khananam nidhāna khananam tathā gaṇitam jyotiṣā ārambham khani bila praveśanam revatī ca aśvinī citrā svātī hastā punarvasū anurādhā mṛgaḥ jyeṣṭhāḥ ete pārśvamukhāḥ smṛtāḥ gaja uṣṭra aśva balīvarda damanam mahiṣasya ca bījānām vapanam kuryāt gamana āgamana ādikam cakra yantra rathānām ca nāvā ādīnām pravāhaṇam pārśveṣu yāni karmāṇi kuryāt eteṣu tāni api rohiṇī ārdrām tathā puṣyā dhaniṣṭhā ca uttarā trayam vāruṇam śravaṇam ca eva nava ca ūrdhva mukhāḥ smṛtāḥ eṣu rājya abhiṣekam ca paṭṭabandham ca kārayet ūrdhva mukhyāni ucchritāni sarvāṇi eteṣu kārayet ca aśubhā ṣaṣṭhī aṣṭamī navamī tathā amāvāsyā pūrṇimā ca tat dvādaśī ca caturdaśī aśuklā pratipad śreṣṭhā dvitīyā candra sūnunā tṛtīyā bhūmiputreṇa caturthā ca śanaiścare gurau śubhā pañcamī syāt ṣaṣṭī maṅgala śukrayoḥ saptamī somaputreṇa aṣṭamī kuja bhāskarau navamī candra vāreṇa daśamī tu gurau śubhā ekādaśyāḥ guru śukrau dvādaśyām ca punar budhaḥ trayodaśī śukra bhaumau śanau śreṣṭhā caturdaśī paurṇamāsī api amāvāsyā śreṣṭhā syāt ca bṛhaspatau dvādaśīm dahate bhānuḥ śaśī ca ekādaśīm dahet kujaḥ dahet ca daśāmīm navamīm ca budhaḥ dahet aṣṭamīm dahate jīvaḥ saptamīm bhārgavaḥ dahet sūryaputraḥ dahet ṣaṣṭhīm gamana ādyāsu nā asti vai pratipad navamīṣu eva caturdaśī aṣṭamīṣu ca budhavāreṇa prasthānam dūratas parivarjayet meṣe karkaṭake ṣaṣṭhī kanyāyām mithune aṣṭamī daśamī vṛścike siṃhe dhanuḥ mone caturdaśī etāḥ dagdhāḥ na gantavyam pīḍā ādiḥ kila mānavaiḥ viśākhā trayam āditye pūrvāṣāḍhā traye śaśī eṣu yogeṣu ca utpāta mṛtyu roga ādikam bhavet mūleḥ akaḥ śravaṇe candraḥ proṣṭhapadī uttare kujaḥ pūrvaphalgunī śukre ca svātiḥ ca eva śanaiśvare etaiḥ ca amṛta yogāḥ syuḥ sarva kārya prasādhakāḥ kālam parva ādiḥ tu jñeyaḥ kālaḥ kāla viśāradaiḥ ekīkṛtya akṣarāt mātram nāmnoḥ strīpuṃsayoḥ tribhiḥ bhāge dvi śeṣe strī nāśaḥ pusaḥ syāt eka śūnyayoḥ viṣkambhe ghaṭikāḥ pañca śūle sapta prakīrtitāḥ ṣaḍgaṇḍe ca atigaṇḍe ca nava vyāghāta vajrayoḥ guruḥ puṣye anurādhā budhe śubhā rohiṇī ca śanau śreṣṭhā saumam somena vai śubham śukre ca revatī śreṣṭhā aśvinī maṅgale śubhā eteṣu siddhi yogāḥ vai sarva doṣa vināśanāḥ bhaume vā uttarāṣāḍhā dhaniṣṭhā ca budhe hara garau śatabhiṣā rudra śukre vai rohiṇī tathā śanau ca revatī śambho viṣa yogāḥ prakīrtitāḥ śravaṇam ca dhaniṣṭhā ca hasta aśvanī mṛgāḥ tathā kuryāt śatabhiṣāyām ca jātakarma ādi mānavaḥ viśākhā ca uttarā trīṇi maghā ārdrā bharaṇī tathā āśleṣā kṛttikā rudra prasthāne maraṇa pradāḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe jyotiḥ śāstre nakṣatrataddevatādagdhayogādinirūpaṇam nāma ekonaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam ṣaṣ āditye daśā jñeyā some pañcadaśa smṛtāḥ aṣṭau aṅgārake cava budhaiḥ spatadaśa smṛtāḥ śanaiścare daśa jñeyāḥ guroḥ ekonaviṃśatiḥ rāhoḥ dvādaśa varṣāṇi ekaviṃśatiḥ bhārgave raveḥ daśā duḥ kha dā syāt udvega nṛpa nāśa kṛt vibhūti dā soma daśā sukham iṣṭa anna dā tathā duḥ kha pradā kuja daśā rājya ādeḥ syāt vināśinī divya strī dā budha daśā rājya dā kośa vṛddhi dā śaneḥ daśā rājya nāśa bandhu duḥkha karī bhavet guroḥ daśā rājya dā syāt sukha dharma ādi dāyinī rāhoḥ daśā rājya nāśa vyādhi dā duḥ kha dā bhavet hasti aśva dā śukra daśā rājya strī lābha dā bhavet meṣa aṅgāraka kṣetram vṛṣaḥ śukrasya kīrtitaḥ sūrya kṣetram bhavet siṃhaḥ kanyā kṣetram budhasya ca bhārgavasya tulā kṣetram vṛścika uṅgārakasya ca paurṇamāsyāḥ dvayam tatra pūrvāṣāḍhā dvayam bhavet dvirāṣāḍhaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ viṣṇuḥ svapiti karkaṭe aśvinī revatī citrā dhaniṣṭhā syāt alaṅkṛtau mṛga ahi kapi mārjāra śvānaḥ sūkara pakṣiṇaḥ nakulaḥ mūṣakaḥ ca eva yātrāyām dakṣiṇe śubhaḥ vipra kanyā śivā eṣām śaṅkha bherī vasundharāḥ veṇu strī pūrṇa kumbhāḥ ca yātrāyām darśanam śubham jambūka uṣṭra khara ādyāḥ ca yātrāyām vāmake śubhāḥ kārpāsa oṣadhi tailam ca pakra aṅgāra bhujaṅgamāḥ mukta keśī rakta mālya nagna ādya śubham īkṣitam lakṣaṇam vakṣye labhat pūrve mahā phalam āgneye śoka santāpau dakṣiṇe hānim āpnuyāt nairṛtya śoka santāpau miṣṭānnam ca eva paścime īśāne maraṇam proktam hikkāyāḥ ca phala aphalam hṛdaye pañca ṛkṣāṇi ekam nābhau pradāpayet nakṣatrāṇi ca śeṣāṇi ravi pāde niyojayet caraṇasyena ṛkṣeṇa alpa āyuḥ jāyate naraḥ nābhi sthena alpa santuṣṭaḥ hṛd sthena syāt maheśvaraḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍam prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe jyotiḥ śāstre grahadaśādinirūpaṇam nāma ṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam saṃpūjyamānaḥ lokaiḥ tu guru vat dṛśyate śaśī candrasya dvādaśa avasthāḥ bhavanti śṛṇu tāḥ api triṣu triṣu ca ṛkṣeṣu aśvinī ādi vadāmi aham pravāsa stham punar dṛṣṭam mṛta avastham jaya āvaham hāsya avastham nata a avastham pramoda avastham eva ca kampa avastham sukha avastham dvādaśa avastha gam bhavet pravāsaḥ ca jayaḥ hāseratiḥ sukham janma sthaḥ kurute tuṣṭim dvitīye na asti nirvṛtiḥ tṛtīye rāja sanmānam caturthe kalaha āgamaḥ pañcamena mṛgāṅkena strī lābhaḥ vai tathā bhavet ghana dhānya āgamaḥ ṣaṣṭhe ratiḥ pūjā ca saptame aṣṭame prāṇa sandehaḥ navame kośa sañcayaḥ daśame kārya niṣpatti dhruvam ekādaśe jayaḥ dvādaśena śaśāṅkena mṛtyuḥ eva na saṃkhayaḥ kṛttikā ādau ca pūrveṇa sapta ṛkṣāṇi ca vai vrajet maghā ādau dakṣiṇe gacchet anurādhā ādi paścime praśastā ca uttara yātrā dhaniṣṭhā ādiṣu saptasu aśvinī revatī citrā dhaniṣṭhā samalaṅkṛtau mṛga aśvi citrā puṣyāḥ ca mūlāḥ hastā śubhāḥ sadā kanyā pradāne yātrāyām pratiṣṭhā ādiṣu karmasu śaśi jña śukra jīvāḥ ca rāśau rāśau ca atha tṛtīyake bhauma manda śaśāṅka arkāḥ budhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ caturthake jña śukrau aṣṭame śreṣṭhau navama sthaḥ guruḥ śubhaḥ arka ārki candrāḥ daśame grahāḥ ekādaśe khilāḥ siṃhena makaraḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kanyayā meṣaḥ uttamaḥ dhanuṣā vṛṣabhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ mithunena ca vṛścikaḥ etat ṣaṣ aṣṭakam prītyai bhavati eva na saṃśayaḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe jyotiḥ śāstre grahāṇām śubhāśubhasthānādinirūpaṇam nāma ekapaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe jyotiḥ śāstre lagnaghaṭikā pramāṇādinirūpaṇam nāma dviṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam nara strī lakṣaṇam vakṣye saṃkṣapāt śṛṇu śaṅkara śliṣṭa aṅgulī tāmra nakhau su gulphau śirayā ujjhitau kūrma unnatau ca caraṇau syātām nṛpa varasya hi virūkṣa pāṇḍura nakhau vakrau ca eva śira ānatau sūrpa ākārau ca caraṇau saṃkhuṣkau virala aṅgulī duḥ kha dāridya dau syātā na atra kāryām vicāraṇā alpa roma yutā śreṣṭhā jaṅghā hasti kara upamā roma ekaikam kūpake syāt bhūpānām tu mahātmanām dve dve romṇī paṇḍitānām śrotriyāṇām tathā eva ca roma trayam daridrāṇām rogī nirmāṃsa jānukaḥ alpa liṅgī ca dhanavān syāt ca putra ādi varjitaḥ sthūla liṅgaḥ daridraḥ syāt dukhī eka vṛṣṇiḥ bhavet viṣame strī cañcalaḥ vai nṛpaḥ syāt vṛṣaṇe same pāṇḍuraiḥ malinaiḥ ca eva maṇibhiḥ ca sukhī naraḥ niḥ svāḥ sa śabda mūtrāḥ syuḥ nṛpāḥ niḥśabda dhārayā bhoga āḍhyāḥ sama jaṭharāḥ niḥ svāḥ syuḥ ghaṭa sannibhāḥ sarpa udarāḥ daridrāḥ syuḥ rekhābhiḥ ca āyuḥ ucyate lalāṭe yasya dṛśyante tisraḥ rekhāḥ samāhitāḥ sukhī putra samāyuktaḥ sa ṣaṣṭim jīvate naraḥ catvāriṃśat ca varṣāṇi dvi rekhā darśanāt naraḥ viṃśati abdam tu eka rekhāḥ ā karṇa antāḥ śata āyuṣaḥ saptati āyuḥ dvi rekhā tu ṣaṣṭi āyuḥ tisṛbhiḥ bhavet vyakta avyaktābhiḥ rekhābhiḥ viṃśati āyūḥ bhavet naraḥ catvāriṃśat ca varṣāṇi hīna rekhaḥ tu jīvati triśūlam paṭṭiśam vā api lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate tarjanyāḥ madhyamā aṅgulyāḥ āyūrekhā tu madhyataḥ saṃprāptā yā bhavet rudra sa jīvet śaradaḥ śatam prathamā jñāna rekhā tu hi aṅguṣṭhāt anuvartate madhyamā ā mūla gā rekhā āyūrekhā atas param kaniṣṭhikām samāśritya āyūrekhā samāviśet a chinnā vā vibhaktā vā sa jīvet śaradaḥ śatam yasya pāṇi tale rekhā āyuḥ tasya prakāśayet śata varṣāṇi jīvet ca bhogī rudra na saṃśayaḥ kaniṣṭhikām samāśritya madhyamāyām upāgatā kuryāt āyūrekhā tu mānavam iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe jyotiḥ śāstre sāmudrike puṃllakṣaṇanirūpaṇam nāma triṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam yasyāḥ tu kuñcitāḥ keśāḥ mukham ca parimaṇḍalam nābhiḥ ca dakṣiṇa āvartā sā kanyā kula vardhinī yā ca kāñcana varṇa ābhā rakta hasta saroruhā sahasrāṇām tu nārīṇām bhavet sā api pativratā vakra keśā ca yā kanyā maṇḍala akṣī ca yā bhavet bhartā ca mriyate tasyāḥ niyatam duḥ kha bhāginī pūrṇa candra mukhī kanyā bāla sūrya sama prabhā viśāla netrā bimboṣṭhī sā kanyā labhate sukham rekhābhiḥ bahubhiḥ kleśam su alpābhiḥ dhana hīna tā raktābhiḥ sukham āpnoti kṛṣṇābhiḥ preṣya tām vrajet kārye ca mantrī sat strī syāt satī syāt karaṇeṣu ca bhāryā mātā syāt veśyā ca śayane śubhā aṅkuśam kuṇḍalam cakram yasyāḥ pāṇi tale bhavet yasyāḥ pāṇi tale rekhā prākāraḥ toraṇam bhavet api dāsa kule jātā rājñī tvam upagacchati yasyāḥ anāmikā aṅguṣṭhau pṛthivyām na eva tiṣṭhataḥ patim mārayate kṣipram sva icchā ācāreṇa vartate yasyāḥ gamana mātreṇa bhūmi kampaḥ prajāyate patim mārayate kṣipram sva icchā ācāreṇa vartate tvacaḥ snehena śāyyām ca pāda snehena vāhanam matsya aṅkuśa abja cihnau ca cakra lāṅgala lakṣitau nābhiḥ praśastā gambhīrā dakṣiṇa āvartikā śubhā iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe jyotiḥ śāstre sāmudrike strīlakṣaṇanirūpaṇam nāma catuḥṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam samudra uktam pravakṣyāmi nara strī lakṣaṇam śubham yena vijñāta mātreṇa atīta anāgata apramā śleṣṭa aṅgulī tāmra nakhau pāda āviṣṇau śira ujjhitau kūrma unnatau gūḍha gulphau supārṣṇaḥ nṛpateḥ smṛtau śū pākārau virūkṣau ca vakrau pādau śira alakau saṃśuṣkau pāṇḍura nakhau niḥ svasya virala aṅgulī mārgāya utkaṇṭakau pādau kaṣāya sadṛśau tathā mṛdu romā samā jaṅghā tathā kari kara prabhā ūravaḥ jānavaḥ tulyāḥ nṛpasya upacitāḥ smṛtāḥ niḥ svasya sṛgāla jaṅghāḥ rauma ekaikam ca kūpake nṛpāṇām śrotriyāṇām ca dve dve śriye ca dhīmatām tri ādyaiḥ niḥ svāḥ mānavāḥ syuḥ duḥ svabhājaḥ ca ninditāḥ keśāḥ ca vai kuñcitāḥ ca pravāse mriyate naraḥ nirmāṃsa jānuḥ saubhāgyam alpaiḥ nimnaiḥ ratiḥ striyāḥ vikaṭaiḥ ca daridrāḥ syuḥ sa māṃsaiḥ rājyam eva ca mahadbhiḥ āyuḥ ākhyātam hi alpa liṅgaḥ dhanī naraḥ kośa gūḍhe dīrghaiḥ bhugnaiḥ ca dhana varjitaḥ balavān yuddha śīlaḥ ca saḥ eva ca durbalaḥ tu eka vṛṣaṇaḥ viṣama ābhyāñcalaḥ striyām samābhyām kṣitipaḥ proktaḥ pralambena śata abdavān tābhyām ca bahu āyūḥ rūkṣaiḥ maṇibhiḥ īśvaraḥ pāṇḍaraiḥ maṇibhiḥ niḥ svāḥ malinaiḥ sukha bhāginaḥ sa śabdaniḥ śabda mūtrāḥ syuḥ aṃridrāḥ ca mānavāḥ eka dvi tri catuḥ pañca ṣaḍbhiḥ dhārābhiḥ eva ca dakṣiṇa āvarta calita mūtrāḥ bhiḥ ca nṛpāḥ smṛtāḥ vikīrṇa mūtrāḥ svāḥ ca pradhāna sukha dāyikāḥ eka dhārāḥ ca vanitāḥ snigdhaiḥ maṇibhiḥ unnataiḥ śuṣkaiḥ niśvāḥ viśuṣkaiḥ ca durbhagāḥ parikīrtitāḥ puṣpa gandhe nṛpāḥ śukre madhu gandhe dhanam bahuḥ daridraḥ kṣāra gandhe ca dīrgha āyuḥ śīghra maithunī māṃsala sphic sukhī syāt ca siṃha sphic bhūpatiḥ smṛtaḥ bhavet siṃha kaṭī rājā niḥ svaḥ kapi kaṭiḥ naraḥ sarpa udarāḥ daridrāḥ syuḥ piṭharaiḥ ca ghaṭaiḥ samaiḥ sama kakṣāḥ ca bhoga āḍhyāḥ nimna kakṣāḥ dhana ujjhitāḥ nṛpāḥ ca unnata kakṣāḥ syuḥ jihnāḥ viṣama kakṣakāḥ matsya udarāḥ bahu dhanāḥ nābhibhiḥ sukhinaḥ smṛtāḥ vistīrṇābhiḥ bahulābhiḥ nimnābhiḥ kleśa bhāginaḥ bali madhya gatā nābhiḥ śūla bādhām karoti hi vāma āvartaḥ ca sādhyam vai medhām dakṣiṇatas tathā pārśva āyatā cira āyuḥ dā tu upaviṣṭā dhaneśvaram adhas gavā āḍhyam kuryāt ca nṛpa tvam padma karṇikā eka baliḥ śata āyuḥ syāt śrī bhogī dvi valiḥ smṛtaḥ tri valiḥ kṣmāpaḥ ācāryaḥ sukhī agamyā gāmī jihma baliḥ bhūpāḥ pārśvaiḥ ca māṃsalaiḥ mṛdubhiḥ su samaiḥ ca eva dakṣiṇa āvarta romabhiḥ viparītaiḥ para preṣyāḥ nirdravyāḥ sukha varjitāḥ nirdhanāḥ viṣamaiḥ derghaiḥ pīta upacitakaiḥ nṛpāḥ sama unnatam ca hṛdayam akampam māṃsalam pṛthu nṛpāṇām adhamānām ca khara roma śirālakam arthavān sama vakṣāḥ syāt pīnaiḥ vakṣobhiḥ ūrjitaḥ vakṣobhiḥ viṣamaiḥ niḥ svar śastreṇanidhanāḥ tathā viṣamaiḥ jatrubhiḥ niḥ svāḥ asthi naddhaiḥ ca mānavāḥ unnataiḥ bhoginaḥ nimnaiḥ niḥ svāḥ pīnaiḥ dhana anvitāḥ niḥ svaḥ cipiṭa kaṇṭhaḥ syāt sirā śuṣka galaḥ sukhī śūraḥ syāt mahiṣa grīvaḥ śāstra āttaḥ mṛga kaṇṭhakaḥ kambu grīvaḥ ca nṛpatiḥ lamba kaṇṭhaḥ ati bhakṣakaḥ aromaśāḥ bhugna pṛṣṭham śubham ca aśubham anyathā kakṣā aśvattha dalā śreṣṭhā sugandhiḥ mṛga romikā anyathā tu artha hīnānām dāridrayasya ca kāraṇam ca eva bhugna alpau śliṣṭau ca vipulau śubhau ājānu lambitau bāhū vṛttau pīnau nṛpa īśvare niḥ svānām romaśau hrasvau śreṣṭhau kari kara prabhau hasta aṅgulayaḥ eva syuḥ vāyu dvāra yutāḥ śubhāḥ medhāvinām ca sūkṣmāḥ syuḥ bhṛtyānām cipiṭāḥ smṛtāḥ sthūla aṅgulībhiḥ niḥ svāḥ syuḥ natāḥ syuḥ su kṛśaiḥ tadā pitṛ vitta vināśaḥ ca nimnāt kara talāt narāḥ maṇibandhaiḥ nigūḍhaiḥ ca su śliṣṭaiḥ śubha gandhibhiḥ nṛpāḥ hīnāḥ kara chaidaiḥ sa śabdaiḥ dhana varjitāḥ saṃvṛtaiḥ ca eva nimnaiḥ ca dhaninaḥ parikīrtitāḥ prottānaka ra dātāraḥ viṣamaiḥ viṣamāḥ narāḥ karaiḥ kara talaiḥ ca eva lākṣā bhaiḥ īśvarāḥ talaiḥ paradāra ratāḥ pītaiḥ ūkṣaiḥ niḥ svāḥ narāḥ matāḥ tuṣa tulya nakhāḥ klībāḥ kuṭilaiḥ sphuṭitaiḥ narāḥ niḥ svāḥ ca kunakhaiḥ tadvat vivarṇaiḥ paratarkakāḥ tāmraiḥ bhūpāḥ dhana āḍhyāḥ ca aṅguṣṭhaiḥ sa yavaiḥ tathā aṅguṣṭha mūla jaiḥ putrī syāt dīrgha aṅguli parvakaḥ dīrgha āyuḥ subhagaḥ ca eva nirdhanaḥ virala aṅguliḥ nṛpateḥ kara tala gāḥ maṇibandhāt samutthitāḥ vajra ākārāḥ ca dhaninām matsya puccha nibhāḥ budhe śaṅkha ātapatra śivikā gaja padma upamāḥ nṛpe kumbha aṅkuśa patākā ābhāḥ mṛṇāla ābhāḥ nidhi īśvare dāma ābhāḥ ca gavā āḍhyānām svastika ābhāḥ nṛpa īśvare cakra asi tomara dhanuḥ kunta ābhāḥ nṛpateḥ kare alu ukhala ābhāḥ yajña āḍhyāḥ vedī bhā ca agnihotriṇi vāpī deva kulyā ābhāḥ trikoṇa ābhāḥ ca dhārmike aṅguṣṭha mūla gāḥ rekhāḥ putrāḥ sūkṣmāḥ ca dārikāḥ pradeśinī gatā rekhā kaniṣṭhā mūla gāminī niḥ svāḥ ca bahu rekhāḥ syuḥ nirdravyāḥ cibukaiḥ kṛśaiḥ māṃsalaiḥ ca dhana upetāḥ āraktaiḥ adharaiḥ nṛpāḥ bimba upamaiḥ ca sphuṭitaiḥ oṣṭhaiḥ ūkṣaiḥ cakaṇḍitaiḥ viṣamaiḥ dhana hīnāḥ ca dantāḥ snigdhāḥ ghanāḥ śubhāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ dantāḥ samāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ jihvā raktā samā śubhā ślakṣṇā dīrghā ca vijñeyā tālū śvete dhana kṣaye kṛṣṇe ca paruṣaḥ vakram samam saumyam ca saṃvṛtam bhūpānām amalam ślakṣṇam viparītam ca duḥ khinām mahā duḥ kham durbhagāṇām strī mukham putram āpnuyāt āḍhyānām vartulam vakram nirdravyāṇām ca dīrghakam bhīru vakraḥ pāpa karmā dhūrtānām caturaśrakam nimnam vakram aputrāṇām kṛpaṇānām ca hrasvakam sampūrṇam bhoginām kāntam śmaśru snigdham śubham mṛdu saṃhatam ca a sphuṭita agram rakta śmaśruḥ ca caurakaḥ rakta alpa paruṣa śmaśru karṇāḥ syuḥ pāpa mṛtyavaḥ nirmāṃsaiḥ cipiṭaiḥ bhogāḥ kṛpaṇāḥ hrasva karṇakāḥ śaṅku karṇāḥ ca rājānaḥ roma karṇāḥ gata āyuṣaḥ bṛhat karṇāḥ ca dhaninaḥ rājānaḥ parikīrtitāḥ karṇaiḥ snigdha avanaddhaiḥ ca vyālambaiḥ māṃsalaiḥ nṛpāḥ bhogī vai nimna gaṇḍaḥ syāt matrī sampūrṇa gaṇḍakaḥ śuka nāsaḥ sukhī syāt ca śuṣka nāsaḥ ati jīvanaḥ chinna agra kūpa nāsaḥ syāt agamyā gamane rataḥ dīrgha nāse ca saubhāgyam cauraḥ ca ākuñcita indriyaḥ mṛtyuḥ cipiṭa nāse syāt hīnaḥ bhāgyavatām bhavet krūre dakṣiṇa vakrā syāt valinām ca kṣutam sakṛt syāt viniṣpiṇḍitam hrādi sa anunādam ca jīva kṛt mārjāra locanaiḥ pāpmā durātmā madhu piṅgalaiḥ krūrāḥ kekara netrāḥ ca harita akṣāḥ sa kalmaṣāḥ jihyaiḥ ca locanaiḥ śūrāḥ senānyaḥ gaja locanāḥ gambhīra akṣāḥ īśvarāḥ syuḥ mantriṇaḥ sthūla cakṣuṣaḥ lākṣāḥ vidvāṃsaḥ saubhāgyam śyāma cakṣuṣām syāt kṛṣṇa tāraka akṣāṇām akṣṇām utpāṭanam kila maṇḍala akṣāḥ ca pāpāḥ syuḥ niḥ svāḥ syuḥ viśāla unnatā sukhinī daridrā viṣama bhruvaḥ āḍhyaḥ niḥ svaḥ ca khaṇḍa bhrṛḥ madhye ca vinata bhruvaḥ strīṣu gamyāsu saktāḥ syuḥ suta arthe parivarjitāḥ an nataiḥ vipulaiḥ śaṅkhaiḥ lalāṭaiḥ viṣamaiḥ tathā ācāryāḥ śukti viśālaiḥ śirālaiḥ pāpa kāriṇaḥ sirābhiḥ ca svastikābhiḥ dhana īśvarāḥ nimnaiḥ lalāṭaiḥ bandha arhāḥ krūra karma ratāḥ tathā saṃvṛtaiḥ ca lalāṭaiḥ ca kṛpaṇāḥ unnataiḥ nṛpāḥ anaśru snigdha ruditam adīnam śubha dam nṛṇām pracura aśru dīnam rūkṣam ca ruditam ca sukha āvaham akampam hasitam śreṣṭham mīlita akṣam agha āvaham asakṛt hasitam duṣṭam sa unmādasya hi anekadhā lalāṭa upasṛtāḥ tisraḥ rekhāḥ syuḥ śata varṣiṇām nṛpa tvam syāt catasṛbhiḥ āyuḥ pañcanavati atha arekheṇa āyuḥ navatiḥ vicchinnābhiḥ ca keśānta upagatābhiḥ ca aśīti āyuḥ naraḥ bhavet pañcabhiḥ saptabhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ pañcāśat vahubhiḥ tathā catvāriṃśat ca vakrābhiḥ triṃśat bhrū lagna gāmibhiḥ viṃśatiḥ vāma vakrāḥ bhiḥ āyuḥ kṣudrābhiḥ alpakam chatra ākāraiḥ śirobhiḥ tu nṛpāḥ nimna śirāḥ dhanī cipiṭaiḥ ca pituḥ mṛtyuḥ go ādyāḥ parimaṇḍalaiḥ ghaṭa mūrdhā pāpa ruciḥ dhana ādyaiḥ parivarjitaḥ kṛṣṇaiḥ ākuñcitaiḥ keśaiḥ snigdhaiḥ ekaika sambhavaiḥ abhinna agraiḥ ca mṛdubhiḥ na ca ati bahubhiḥ nṛpāḥ bahu mūlaiḥ ca viṣamaiḥ sthūla agraiḥ kapilaiḥ tathā yat yat gātram mahā rūkṣam śirālam māṃsa varjitam tat tat syāḥ daśubham sarvam tatas anyathā vipulaḥ triṣu gambhīraḥ dīrghaḥ sūkṣmaḥ ca pañcasu nābhiḥ svaraḥ ca sa sattvam ca trayam gambhīram īritam puṃsaḥ syāt ati vistīrṇam lalāṭam vadanam hi uraḥ cakṣuḥ kakṣāḥ nāsikā ca ṣaṭ syuḥ nṛpa kṛkāṭikāḥ unnatāni ca hrasvani jaṅghā grīvā ca liṅgakam pṛṣṭham catvāri raktāni kara tālu adharāḥ nakhāḥ netra anta pāda jihvā oṣṭhāḥ pañca sūkṣmāṇi santi vai daśana aṅguli parvāṇi nakha keśa tvacaḥ śubhāḥ dīrghāḥ stanāntaram bāhu danta locana nāsikāḥ narāṇām lakṣaṇam proktam vadāmi strīṣu lakṣaṇam śliṣṭa aṅgulī ca unnata agrau tām pāpya nṛpatiḥ bhavet anulbaṇam sandhi deśam samam jānu dvayam śubham ūrū kari kara ākārau aromau ca samau śubhau śroṇī lalāṭakam strīṇām ūru kūrma unnatam śubham gūḍhaḥ maṇiḥ ca śubha daḥ nitambaḥ ca guruḥ śubhaḥ vistīrṇa māṃsa upacitā gambhīrā vipulā śubhā nābhiḥ pradakṣiṇa āvartā madhyam tri bali śobhitam kaṭhinau romaśā śastā mṛdu grīvā ca kambu bhā āraktau adharau śreṣṭhau māṃsalam vartulam mukham kunda puṣpa samāḥ dantāḥ bhāṣitam kokilā samam dākṣiṇya yuktam aśaṭham haṃsa śabda sukha āvaham nāsā samā sama puṭā strīṇām tu rucirā śubhā na pṛthū bāla indu nibhe bhruvau ca atha lalāṭakam śubham ardha indu saṃsthānam atuṅgam syāt alomaśam su māṃsalam karṇa yugmam samam mṛdu samāhitam snigdhāḥ nīlāḥ ca mṛdavaḥ mūrdhajāḥ kuñcitāḥ kacāḥ strīṇām samam śiraḥ śreṣṭham pāde pāṇi tale atha vā vāji kuñjara śrīvṛkṣa yūpa iṣu yava tomaraiḥ dhvaja cāmara mālābhiḥ śaila kuṇḍala vedibhiḥ lakṣaṇaiḥ aṅkuśa ādyaiḥ ca striyaḥ syuḥ rāja vallabhāḥ na nimnam nā unnatam strīṇām bhavet kara talam śubham rekhā anvitam tu avidhavām kuryāt saṃbhoginīm striyam rekhā yā maṇibandha utthā gatā madhyāṅgulim kare gatā pāṇi tale yā ca yā ūrdhva pāda tale sthitā strīṇām puṃsām tathā sā syāt rājyāya ca sukhāya ca kaniṣṭhikā mūla bhavā rekhā kuryāt śata āyuṣam pradeśinī madhyamābhyām antarāla gatā satī ūnāḥ ūna āyuṣam kuryāt rekhāḥ ca aṅguṣṭha mūla gāḥ bṛhatyaḥ putrāḥ tanvyaḥ tu pramadāḥ parikīrtitāḥ su alpa āyuṣaḥ bahu chinnāḥ dīrgha a chinnāḥ mahā āyuṣam śubham tu lakṣaṇam strīṇām proktam tu aśubham anyathā kaniṣṭhikā anāmikā vā yasyāḥ na spṛśate mahīm aṅguṣṭham vā gatā atītya tarjanī kulaṭā ca sā ūrdhvam dvābhyām piṇḍikābhyām jaṅghe ca ati śirālake romaśe ca ati māṃse ca kumbha ākāram tathā udaram vāma āvartam nimnam alpam duḥ khitānām ca guhyakam grīvayā hrasvayā niḥ svāḥ dīrghayā ca kula kṣayaḥ pṛthulayā pracaṇḍāḥ ca striyaḥ syuḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ kekare piṅgale netre śyāme lola īkṣaṇā satī smite kūpe gaṇḍayoḥ ca sā dhruvam vyabhicāriṇī pralambinī lalāṭe tu devaram hanti ca aṅganā yā tu roma uttara oṣṭhī syāt na śubhā bhartuḥ eva hi karālāḥ viṣamāḥ dantāḥ kleśāya ca bhavanti te cauryāya kṛṣṇa māṃsāḥ ca dīrghāḥ bhurtuḥ ca mṛtyave kravyāda rūpaiḥ hastaiḥ ca vṛka kāka ādi sannibhaiḥ śirālaiḥ viṣamaiḥ śuṣkaiḥ vitta hīnāḥ bhavanti hi samunnata uttareṣṭhī yā kalahe rūkṣa bhāṣiṇī strīṣu doṣāḥ virūpāsu patra ākāraḥ guṇāḥ tatas nara strī lakṣaṇam proktam vakṣye tad jñāna dāyakam iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe jyotiḥ śāstre sāmudrike strīnaralakṣaṇam nāma pañcaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam nirlakṣaṇā śubhā syāt ca cakra aṅkita śilā arcanāt ādau sudarśanaḥ mūrtiḥ lakṣmī nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ vāsudevaḥ ca pradyumnaḥ tatas saṅkarṣaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ca aṣṭamaḥ syāt navyūhaḥ daśa ātmakaḥ ekādaśaḥ aniruddhaḥ syāt dvādaśaḥ dvādaśātmakaḥ su darśanāḥ lakṣitāḥ ca pūjitāḥ sarva kāma dāḥ śālagrāma śilā yatra devaḥ dvāravatī bhavaḥ śālagrāmaḥ dvārakā ca naimiṣam puṣkaram gayā vārāṇasī prayāgaḥ ca kurukṣetram ca sūkaram gaṅgā ca narmadā ca eva candrabhāgā sarasvatī puruṣottamaḥ mahākālaḥ tīrthāni etāni śaṅkara aṅgirāḥ śrīmukhaḥ bhāvaḥ yuvā dhātā tathā eva ca īśvaraḥ bahudhānyaḥ ca pramāthī vikramaḥ viṣuḥ citrabhānuḥ svabānuḥ ca tāraṇaḥ pārthivaḥ vyayaḥ sarva jit sarva dhārī ca virodhī vikṛtiḥ kharaḥ hemalambaḥ vilaṃbaḥ ca vikāraḥ śarvarī plavaḥ śubhakṛt śobhanaḥ krodhī paridhāvī pramādī ca ānandaḥ rākṣasaḥ nalaḥ aśobhanāḥ śobhanāḥ ca nāmnā eva ete hi vatsarāḥ kālam vakṣyāmi saṃsiddhyai rudra pañca svara udayāt rājā sā jāḥ udāsā ca pīḍā mṛtyuḥ tathā eva ca ā ī ū ai au svarān ca likhet pañca agni koṣṭhake tithī ekā agni koṣṭheṣu trayaḥ rājā atha sā jayāḥ udāsa amṛtyupīḍāḥ ca kujaḥ somasutaḥ kramāt revatī ādi mṛga antāḥ ca ṛkṣāṇi prathamā kalā dvādaśa ahaiḥ dvayoḥ māsa nāmnoḥ ādi akṣaram tathā kalā liṅgā ca yā tiṣṭhet pañcamaḥ tasya vai mṛtiḥ kalā tithiḥ tathā vāraḥ nakṣatram māsam eva ca nāma udayasya pūrvam ca tathā bhavati na anyathā om kṣaiṃ (kṣauḥ kṣāma ādi aṅga śiva āmīkṣā viṣa graha matiḥ hara mṛtyuñjayaḥ gaṇaḥ lakṣmī rocana ādyaiḥ tu lekhitaḥ bhūrje tu dhāritāḥ kaṇṭhe bāhau ca iti jaya ādi dāḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe jyotiḥ śāstre śālagrāmaṣaṣṭyūbdasvarodayānām nirūpaṇam nāma ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam iti jyotiḥ śāstram samāptam sūtaḥ uvāca hareḥ śrutvā haraḥ gaurīm deha stham jñānam abravīt kujaḥ vahniḥ raviḥ pṛthvī sauriḥ āpaḥ prakīrtitaḥ vāyu saṃsthā sthitaḥ rāhuḥ dakṣa randhra avabhāsakaḥ vāma nāḍīm tu madhya sthām kārayet ātmanaḥ tathā sthāna sevām tathā dhyānam vāṇijyam rāja darśanam anyāni śubha karmāṇi kārayeta prayatnataḥ dakṣa nāḍī pravāhe tu śaniḥ bhaumaḥ ca sa aihikaḥ śubha aśubha vivekaḥ hi jñāyate tu svara udayāt deha madhye sthitāḥ nāḍyaḥ bahu rūpāḥ su vistarāḥ nābheḥ adhastāt yaḥ kandaḥ tu aṅkurāḥ tatra nirgatāḥ cakra vat ca sthitāḥ tāḥ tu sarvāḥ prāṇa harāḥ smṛtāḥ tāsām madhye trayaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ vāma dakṣa eṇa madhyamāḥ vāmā soma ātmikā proktā dakṣiṇā ravi sannibhā madhyamā ca bhavet agniḥ phalantī kāla pūriṇī vāmā hi amṛta rūpā ca jagat āpyāyane sthitā dakṣiṇā raudra bhāgena jagat śoṣayate sadā dvayoḥ vāhe tu mṛtyuḥ syāt sarva kārya vināśinī nirgame tu bhavet vāmā praveśe dakṣā eṇā smṛtā iḍā ācāre tathā saumyam candra sūrya gataḥ tathā kārayet krūra karmāṇi prāṇe piṅgala saṃsthite yātrāyām sarva kāryeṣu viṣa apahāraṇe iḍā uccāṭa māraṇa ādyeṣu karmasu eteṣu piṅgalā śobhaneṣu ca kāryeṣu yātrāyām viṣa karmaṇi śānti mukti artha siddhyai ca iḍā yojyā narādhipaiḥ viṣa vat tam tu jānīyāt saṃsmaret tu vicakṣaṇaḥ saumya ādi śubha kāryeṣu lābha ādi jaya jīvite yuddha ādi bhojane ghāte strīṇām ca eva tu saṃgame praśastā dakṣiṇā nāḍī praveśe kṣudra karmaṇi śubha aśubhāni kāryāṇi lābha alābhau jaya ajayau jīva ajīvāya yat pṛcchet na sidhyati ca madhyamā vāma ācāre athavā dakṣe pratyaye yatra nāyakaḥ vāme vā dakṣiṇe vā api yatra saṃkramate śivā ghore ghorāṇi kāryāṇi saumye vai madhyamāni ca prasthite bhāgataḥ haṃse dvābhyām vai sarva vāhinī tadā mṛtyum vijānīyāt yogī yoga viśāradaḥ yatra yatra sthitaḥ pṛcchet vāma dakṣiṇa saṃmukhaḥ tatra tatra samam sadā agratas vāmikā śreṣṭhā pṛṣṭhatas dakṣiṇā śubhā vāmena vāmikā proktā dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇā śubhā vāme vāmā śubhe ca eva dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇā śubhā yat kiñcid kāryam uddiṣṭam jaya ādi śubha lakṣaṇam tat sarvam pūrṇa nāḍyām tu jāyate nirvikalpataḥ anya nāḍī ādi paryantam pakṣa trayam udāhṛtam yāvat ṣaṣṭhī tu pṛcchāyām pūrṇāyām prathamaḥ jayet riktāyām tu dvitīyaḥ tu kathayet tat aśaṅkitaḥ vāma ācāra samaḥ vāyuḥ jāyate karma siddhi daḥ pravṛtte dakṣiṇe mārge viṣame viṣama akṣaram anyatra vāma vāhe tu nāma vai viṣama akṣaram dakṣa vāta pravāhe tu yadi nāma sama akṣaram na atra sandehaḥ nāḍī maghye tu lakṣayet piṅgalā antargate prāṇe śamanīya āhavam jayet yāvat nāḍī udayam cāraḥ tām diśam yāvat āpayet na dātum jāyate saḥ api nā atra kāryā vicāraṇā atha saṃgrāma madhye tu yatra nāḍī sadā vahet sā diśā jayam āpnoti śūnye bhaṅgam vinirdiśet jāta cāre jayam vidyāt mṛtake mṛtam ādiśet jayam parājayam ca eva yaḥ jānāti sa paṇḍitaḥ vāme vā dakṣiṇe vā api yatra sañcarate śivam kṛtvā tat padam āpnoti yātrā santata śobhanā śaśi sūrya pravāhe tu sati yuddham samācaret yām diśam vahate vāyuḥ tām diśam yāvat ājayaḥ meṣī ādyāḥ daśa yāḥ nāḍyaḥ dakṣiṇāḥ vāma saṃsthitāḥ tad vimārge tādṛśa tādṛśe kramāt pṛcchakasya vacaḥ śrutvā ghaṇṭā ākāreṇa lakṣayet vāme vā dakṣiṇe vā api pañcatattva sthitaḥ śive ūrdhve agniḥ adhas āpaḥ ca tiryak saṃsthaḥ prabhañjanaḥ ūrdhve mṛtyuḥ adhas śāntiḥ tiryak ca uccāṭayet sudhīḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe svarodaye śubhāśubhanirūpaṇam nāma saptaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca parikṣām vacmi ratnānām balaḥ nāma asuraḥ abhavat vara vyājena paśu tām yācitaḥ sa suraiḥ makhe paśu vat sa viśastaḥ taiḥ sva vākya aśani yantritaḥ balaḥ loka uparāya devānām hita kāmyayā kāyasya avayavāḥ sarve ratna bīja tvam āyayuḥ devānām atha yakṣāṇām siddhānām pavanāśinām ratna bījam sva jam ayam grāhaḥ su mahān abhavat tadā teṣām tu patatām vegāt vimānena vihāyasā yat yat papāta ratnānām bījam kracana kiñcana tat tad ākara tām yātam sthānam ādheya gauravāt teṣu rakṣaḥ viṣa vyāla vyādhi ghnāni agha hāni ca vajram muktāmaṇayaḥ sa padmarāgāḥ sa marakatāḥ proktāḥ api ca indranīla maṇi vara vaidūryāḥ puṣparāgāḥ ca vidruma maṇiḥ ca yatnāt uddiṣṭam saṃgrahe tad jñaiḥ ākāra varṇau prathamam guṇa doṣau tad phalam parīkṣā ca mūlyam ca ratna kuśalaiḥ vijñeyam sarva śāstrāṇām parīkṣā pariśuddhānām ratnānām pṛthivībhujā dhāraṇam saṃgrahaḥ vā api kāryaḥ śriyam abhīpsatā śāstra jñaḥ kuśalāḥ ca api ratna bhājaḥ parīkṣakāḥ te eva mūlya mātrāyāḥ vettāraḥ parikīrtitāḥ vajra pūrvā parīkṣā iyam tatas asmābhiḥ prakīrtyate tasya asthi leśaḥ nipapāta yeṣu bhuvaḥ pradeśeṣu kathañcid eva vajrāṇi vajra āyudha nirjigīṣoḥ bhavanti nānā ākṛtimanti teṣu haima mātaṅga saurāṣṭrāḥ pauṇḍra kāliṅga kosalāḥ veṇvātaṭāḥ sasauvīrāḥ vajrasya aṣṭa vihārakāḥ ātāmrāḥ himaśaila jāḥ ca śaśibhāḥ veṇvātaṭīyāḥ smṛtāḥ sauvīre tu asita abja megha sadṛśāḥ tābhrāḥ ca saurāṣṭra jāḥ kāliṅgāḥ kana ka avadāta rucirāḥ pīta prabhāḥ kosale śyāmāḥ puṇḍrabhavāḥ mataṅga viṣaye na atyanta pīta prabhāḥ loke asmin parāmāṇu mātram api yat vajram kracid dṛśyate tasmin deva samāśrayaḥ hi avitathaḥ tīkṣṇa agra dhāram yadi vajreṣu varṇa yuktyā devānām api vigrahaḥ proktaḥ varṇebhyaḥ ca vibhāgaḥ kāryaḥ varṇa āśrayāt eva harita sita pīta piṅga śyāmāḥ tāmrāḥ svabhāvataḥ rucirāḥ hari varuṇa śakra hutavaha pitṛpati marutām svakāḥ varṇāḥ viprasya śaṅkha kumuda sphaṭika avadātaḥ syāt kṣattriyasya śaśa babhru vilocana ābhaḥ vaiśyasya kānta kadalī dala sannikāśaḥ śūdrasya dhauta karavāla samāna dīptiḥ dvau vajra varṇau pṛthivīpatīnām sadbhiḥ pradiṣṭau na tu sārvajanyau yaḥ syāt java avi druma bhaṅga śoṇaḥ yaḥ vā haridrāra sannikāśaḥ īśa tvāt sarva varṇānām guṇavat sārbavarṇikam adhara uttara vṛttayā hi yādṛś syāt varṇa saṅkaraḥ tatas kaṣṭataraḥ vajra varṇānām saṅkaraḥ mataḥ ekam api yasya śṛṅgam vidalitam avalokyate viśīrṇam vā śīrṇa śṛṅga deśam mala varṇaiḥ pṛṣataiḥ upeta madhyam na hi vajrabhṛtaḥ api vajram āśu śriyam api āśraya lālasām na kuryāt koṭyaḥ pārśvani dhārāḥ ca ṣaḍ aṣṭau dvādaśa iti ca uttuṅga sama tīkṣṇa agrāḥ vajrasya ākara jāḥ guṇāḥ ṣaṭkoṭi śudvam amalam sphuṭa tīkṣṇa dhāram varṇa anvitam laghu su pārśvam apeta doṣam vṛddhiḥ tam pratidinam eti yāvadāyus strī sampad suta dhana dhānya go daśūnām dūrāt tasya nivartante karmāṇi ātharvaṇāni ca yadi vajram apeta sarva doṣam bibhṛyāt taṇḍula viṃśatim guru tve tri bhāga hīna ardha tad ardha śeṣam trayodaśam triṃśat atas addha bhāgāḥ aśīti bhāgaḥ atha śata aṃśa bhāgaḥ sahasra bhāgaḥ alpa samāna yogaḥ yat taṇḍulaiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ kṛtasya vajrasya mūlyam prathamam pradiṣṭam dvābhyām kramāt vānim upāgatasya tu eka avamānasya viniścayaḥ ayam na ca api taṇḍulaiḥ eva vajrāṇām dharaṇa kramaḥ aṣṭābhiḥ sarṣapaiḥ gairaiḥ taṃṇḍulam parikalpayet alpena api hi doṣeṇa lakṣya a lakṣyeṇa dvaṣitam sva mūlyāt daśamam bhāgam vajram labhati mānavaḥ spaṣṭa doṣam alaṅkāre vajram yadi api dṛśyate ratnānām parikarma artham mūlyam tasya bhavet laghu alam ābharaṇena tasya rājñaḥ guṇa hīnaḥ api maṇiḥ na bhūṣaṇāya anyatra dīrgha a ci piṭa tri aśra ādi aguṇaiḥ viyuktāt ca ayasā puṣparāgeṇa tathā gomedakena ca vaidūrya sphaṭikābhyām ca kācaiḥ ca api pṛthagvidhaiḥ pratirūpāṇi kurvanti vajrasya kuśalāḥ janāḥ parīkṣā teṣu kartavyā vidvadbhiḥ su parīkṣakaiḥ kṣāra ullekhana śāṇābhiḥ teṣām kāryam parīkṣaṇam pṛthivyām yāni ratnāni ye ca anye loha dhātavaḥ guru tā sarva ratnānām gaurava ādhāra kāraṇam vajre tām vaiparītyena sūrayaḥ paricakṣate vajrāṇi muktāmaṇayaḥ ye ca kecana jātayaḥ na teṣām pratibaddhānām bhā bhavati ūrdhva gāminī tiryak kṣata tvāt keṣāñcid kathañcid yadi jāyate tiryak vilikhyamānānām sā pārśveṣu vihanyate yadi api viśīrṇa koṭiḥ sa bindu rekhā anvitaḥ vivarṇaḥ vā saudāḥ minī visphurita abhirāmam rājā yathoktam kaliśam dadhānaḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe ratnatadviśeṣavajraparīkṣaṇādivarṇanam nāma aṣṭaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca dvipa indra jīmūta varāha śaṅkha matsya ahi śukti udbhava veṇu jāni vedhyam tu śuktayudbhavam eva teṣām śeṣāṇi avedhyāni vadanti tad jñāḥ prāyas vimuktāni bhavanti bhāsā śastāni māṅgalya tayā tathā api yāḥ mauktikānām iha jātaye aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ ratna viniścaya jñaiḥ sva yoni madya chavi tulya varṇam śāṅkham bṛhat lola phala pramāṇam utpadyate vāraṇa kumbha madhyāt āpīta varṇam prabhayā vihīnam ye kambavaḥ śārṅga mukha avamarśa pītasya śaṅkha pravarasya gotre mataṅga jāḥ ca api viśuddha vaṃśyāḥ te mauktikānām prabhavāḥ pradiṣṭāḥ utpadyate mauktikam eṣu vṛttam āpīta varṇam prabhayā vihīnam pāṭhīna pṛṣṭhasya samāna varṇam mīnāt su vṛttam laghu ca ati sūkṣmam utpadyate vāricara ānaneṣu matsyāḥ ce te madhya carāḥ payodheḥ varāha daṃṣṭrā prabhavam pradiṣṭam tasya eva daṃṣṭra aṅkura tulya varṇam kracid kathañcid sa bhuvaḥ pradeśe prajāyate sūkara rāj viśiṣṭaḥ varṣopalānām sama varṇa śobham tvaksāra parva prabhavam pradiṣṭam bhaujam gamam mīna viśuddha vṛttam saṃsthānataḥ ati ujjvala varṇa śobham prāpya ati ratnāni mahā prabhāṇi rājyam śriyam vā mahatīm durāpām jijñāsayā ratna dhanam vidhi jñaiḥ śubhe muhūrte prayataiḥ prayatnāt rakṣā vidhānam su mahat vidhāya harmya upariṣṭham kriyate yadā tat na tam bhujaṅgāḥ na tu yātudhānāḥ na vyādhayaḥ na api upasarga doṣāḥ hiṃsanti yasya ahi śiraḥ samuttham muktāphalam tiṣṭhati kośa madhye divā yathā dīrptiṅkaram tathā eva tamaḥ avagāḍhāsu api tat niśāsu mūlyam na vā syāt iti niścayaḥ me kṛtsnā mahī tasya sāpatnya hīnām sa mahīm samagrām bhunakti tat tiṣṭhati yāvat eva nakṣatra mālā iva divaḥ viśīrṇā danta āvaliḥ tasya mahā murasya vicitra varṇeṣu viśuddha varṇā payaḥ su patyuḥ payasām papāta sampūrṇa candra aṃśu kalāpa kānteḥ māṇipravekasya mahā guṇasya saiṃhalika pāralaukika saurāṣṭrika tāmraparṇa pāraśavāḥ kauvera pāṇḍya hāṭaka hemakam iti ākarāḥ tu aṣṭau śuktyudbhavam na ati nikṛṣṭa varṇam pramāṇa saṃsthāna guṇa prabhābhiḥ cintyāḥ na tasya ākara jāḥ viśeṣāḥ rūpe pramāṇe ca yateta vidvān mūlyam sahasrāṇi tu rūpakāṇām tribhiḥ śataiḥ api ādhikāni pañca yat māṣaka ardhena tatas vihīnam tat pañca bhāga dvaya hīna mūlyam yat māṣakān trīn bibhṛyāt sahasre dve tasya mūlyam paramam pradiṣṭam dvi māṣa ka unmānita gauravasya śatāni ca aṣṭau kathitāni mūlyam ardha adhikam māṣakam unmitasya samam ca viṃśa tritayam śatānām guñjāḥ ca ṣaḍ dhārayataḥ śate dve mūlyam param tasya vadanti tad jñāḥ adhikam daśabhiḥ śatam ca mūlyam samavāpnoti api bāliśasya hastāt dviguṇaiḥ daśabhiḥ bhavet anūnam dharaṇam tad bhavakam vadanti tad jñāḥ triṃśatā dharaṇam pūrṇam śikyam tasya iti kīrtyate catvāriṃśat bhavet tasyāḥ param mūlyam viniścayaḥ bhavet tasyāḥ triṃśat mūlyam labhet sā pañcāśat tu bhavet somaḥ tasya mūlyam tu viṃśatiḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ nikara śīrṣam syāt tasyāḥ mūlyam caturdaśa aśītiḥ navatiḥ ca eva kūpyā iti parikīrtitā ghṛṣṭam tatas mṛdu tanūkṛta piṇḍa mūlaiḥ kuryāt yatheṣṭam anu mauktikam āśu viddham mṛd lipta matsya puṭa madhya gatam tu kṛtvā paścāt pacet tanu tatas ca biḍāla puṭyā vyāḍiḥ jagāda jagatām hi mahā prabhāvaḥ siddhaḥ vidagdha hita tad parayā dayāluḥ śvetakāca samam tāram hema aṃśa śata yojitam evam hi siṃhale deśe kurvanti kuśalāḥ janāḥ uṣṇe sa lavaṇe snehe niśām tat vāsayet jale vrīhibhiḥ mardanīyam vā śuṣka vastra upaveṣṭitam yat tu na āyāti vaivarṇyam vijñeyam tat akṛtrimam pramāṇavat gaurava raśmi yuktam sitam su vṛttam sama sūkṣma vedham iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe muktāphalapramāṇādivarṇanam nāma muktāphala parīkṣā nāma ekonasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca asṛj gṛhītvā caritum pratasthe nistriṃśa nīlena nabhaḥ sthalena jettrā surāṇām samareṣu ajastram vīrya avalepa uddhata mānasena tad siṃhalī cāru nitamba bimba vikṣaḥ bhita agādha mahā hradāyām pūga druma ābaddha taṭa dvayāyām mumoca sūryaḥ sarit uttamāyām tatas prabhṛti sā gaṅgā tulya puṇya phala udayā nāmnā rāvaṇagaṅgā iti prathimānam upāgatā tatas prabhṛti eva ca śarvarīṣu kūlāni ratnaiḥ nicitāni tasyāḥ suvarṇa nārāca śataiḥ iva antar bahis pradīptaiḥ niśitāni bhānti tasyāḥ taṭeṣu ujjva cāru rāgāḥ bhavanti toyeṣu ca padmarāgāḥ saugandhika utthāḥ kuruvinda jāḥ ca mahā guṇāḥ sphāṭika saṃprasūtāḥ bandhū ka guñjā sakala indragopa ja vā sama asṛj sama varṇa śobhāḥ bhrājiṣṇavaḥ dāḍima bīja varṇāḥ tathā apare kiśuka puṣpa bhāsaḥ lākṣā rasasya api samāna varṇaḥ sāṃdre api rāge prabhayā svayā eva bhānti sva lakṣyāḥ sphuṭa madhya śobhāḥ bhānoḥ ca bhāsām anuvedha yogām āsādya raśami prakareṇa dūram pārśvāni sarvāṇi anurañjayanti guṇa apapannāḥ sphaṭika prasūtāḥ tathā apare aruṣkara kaṇṭakāri puṣpa tviṣaḥ hiṅgula vat tviṣaḥ anye cakora puṃskokila sārasānām netra avabhāsaḥ ca bhavanti kecid anye punar santi ca puṣpitānām tulya tviṣā kokanada uttamānām prabhāva kāṭhinya guru tva yogaiḥ prāyas samānāḥ sphaṭika udbhavānām kāmam tu rāgaḥ kuruvinda jeṣu sa nā eva yādṛś sphaṭika udbhaveṣu ye tu rāvaṇagaṅgāyām jāyante kuruvindakāḥ padmarāga ghanam rāgam bibhrāṇāḥ sphaṭika arciṣaḥ varṇa anuyāyinaḥ teṣā māndhra deśe tathā pare tathā eva sphāṭika utthānām deśe tumburu saṃjñake sadharmāṇaḥ prajāyante su alpa mūlyāḥ hi te smṛtāḥ varṇa ādhikyam guru tvam ca snigdha tā sama tā accha tā arciṣmat tā mahat tā ca maṇīnām guṇa saṃgrahaḥ ye karkara chidra mala upadigdhāḥ prabhā vimuktāḥ paruṣāḥ vivarṇāḥ na te praśastāḥ maṇayaḥ bhavanti samānatas jāti guṇaiḥ samastaiḥ doṣa upasṛṣṭam maṇim aprabodhāt vibharti yaḥ kaścana kañcid eva tam śoka cintā āmaya mṛtyu vitta nāśa ādayaḥ doṣa gaṇāḥ bhajante kāmam cārutarāḥ pañca pratirūpakāḥ kalaśapura udbhava siṃhala tumburu deśa uttha muktapāṇīyāḥ śrīpūrṇakāḥ ca sadṛśāḥ vijātayaḥ padmarāgāṇām tuṣa upasargāt kalaśa abhidhānam ātāmra bhāvāt api tumburu uttham kārṣṇyāt tathā siṃhala deśa jātam muktā abhidhānam nabhasaḥ svabhāvāt śrīpūrṇakam dīpti vinā kṛta tvāt vijāti liṅga āśrayaḥ eva bhedaḥ yaḥ tāmrikām puṣyati padmarāgaḥ yogāt tuṣāṇām iva pūrṇa madhyaḥ streha pradigdhaḥ pratibhāti yaḥ ca yaḥ vā praghṛṣṭaḥ prajahāti dīptim ākrānta mūrdhā ca tathā aṅgulibhyām yaḥ kālikām pārśva gatām bibharti saṃprāpya ca utkṣipya yathā anuvṛttim vibharti yaḥ sarva guṇān atīva prāpya api ratna ākara jā sva jātim lakṣet guru tvena guṇena vidvān na aśakyam lekhanam kartum padmarāga indranīlayoḥ jātyasya sarve api maṇeḥ na jātu vijātayaḥ santi samāna varṇāḥ tathā api nānā karaṇa artham eva bheda prakāraḥ paramaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ na kaustubhena api saha avabaddham vidvān vijātim bibhṛyāt kadācid cāṇḍālaḥ ekaḥ api yathā dvijātīn sametya bhūrīn api hanti ayatnāt atho maṇīn bhūri guṇa upapannān śakroti viplāvayitum vijātyaḥ sapatna madhye api kṛta adhivāsam pramāda vṛttau api vartamānam na padmarāgasya mahā guṇasya bhartāram āpad spṛśati iha kācid tābhyām īṣat api bhraṣṭam maṇi mūlyāt prahīyate iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe padmarāgaparīkṣaṇam nāma saptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca dānava adhipateḥ pittam ādāya bhujaga adhipaḥ rājataḥ sa mahān ekaḥ khaṇḍa setuḥ iva ābabhau kalikā ghana gandha vāsitā yām vara māṇikya gireḥ upatyakāyām sthānam kṣiteḥ upa payonidhi tīra lekhaṃyām vara māṇikya gireḥ upatyakāyām tatra ā kaṭhora śuka kaṇṭha śirīṣa puṣpa khadyota pṛṣṭha cara śādvala śaivalānām kalhāra śaṣpaka bhujaṅga bhujān ca patra prāpta tviṣaḥ marakatāḥ śubha dāḥ bhavanti tasya ākarasya atitarām sa deśaḥ duḥ kha upalabhyaḥ ca guṇaiḥ ca yuktaḥ tat sarvam viṣa rogāṇām praśamāya prakīrtyate mahā ahi daṃṣṭrā prabhavam viṣam tat tena śāmyati jāyate tat pavitrāṇām uttamam parikīrtitam kāñcana cūrṇasya antar pūrṇam iva lakṣyate yat ca yuktam saṃsthāna guṇaiḥ sama rāgam gauraveṇa na vihīnam savituḥ kara saṃsparśāt churayati sarva āśramam dīptyā nat marakatam mahā gaṇam iti ratna vidām manaḥ vṛttiḥ varṇa ujjvalayā kāntyā sāndra ākāraḥ vibhāsayā bhāti tat api guṇavat saṃjñām āpnoti hi yādṛśī pūrvam śabala kaṭhora malinam rūkṣam pāṣāṇa karkara upetam digdham śilājatunā marakatam evaṃvidham viguṇam śreyaskāmaiḥ na tat dhāryam kretavyam vā katañcana maṇeḥ marakatasya ete lakṣaṇīyāḥ vijātayaḥ kṣaumeṇa vāsasā mṛṣṭā dīptim tyajati putrikā lāghavena eva kācasya śakyā kartum vibhāvanā teṣām na apratibaddhānām bhās bhavati ūrdhva gāminī ṛju tvāt ca eva keṣāñcid kathañcid upajāyate tiryak ālocya mānānām sadyas ca eva praṇaśyati snāna ācamana japyeṣu rakṣā mantra kriyā vidhau bādhyamāneṣu vividhaiḥ deṣa jātaiḥ viṣa udbhavaiḥ saṃgrāme vicaradbhiḥ ca dhāryam marakatam budhaiḥ tathā ca padmarāgāṇām doṣaiḥ mūlyam prahīyate iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe purva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍa marakataparīkṣaṇam nāma ekasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca tatra asita abja halabhṛt vasana asi bhṛṅga śārṅga āyudha aṅga hara kaṇṭha kaṣāya puṣpaiḥ śuṣka itaraiḥ ca kusumaiḥ girikarṇikāyāḥ tasmāt bhavanti maṇayaḥ sadṛśa avabhāsaḥ eka prakārāḥ vispaṣṭa varṇa śobhā avabhāsinaḥ jāyante maṇayaḥ tasmin indranīlāḥ mahā guṇāḥ mṛd pāṣāṇa śilā randhra karkarā trāsa saṃyutāḥ abhrikā paṭala chāyā varṇa doṣaiḥ ca dūṣitāḥ dhāryamāṇasya ye dṛṣṭā padmarāga maṇeḥ guṇāḥ dhāraṇāt indranīlasya tān eva āpnoti mānavaḥ yathā ca padmarāgāṇām jātaka tritayam bhavet indra nīleṣu api tathā draṣṭavyam aviśeṣatas parīkṣā pratyayaiḥ yaiḥ ca padmarāgaḥ parīkṣyate te eva pratyayāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ indranīla maṇeḥ api tathā api na parīkṣā artham guṇānām abhi vṛddhaye agni mātrā parijñāne dāha doṣaiḥ ca dūpitaḥ kāca utpala karavīra sphaṭika ādyāḥ iha budhaiḥ sa vaidūryāḥ kathitāḥ vijātayaḥ ime sadṛśāḥ maṇinā indranīlena guru bhāva kaṭhina bhāvau eteṣām nityam eva vijñeyau kācāt yathāvat uttara vivardhamānau viśeṣeṇa indranīlaḥ yathā kaścid vibharti ātāmra varṇa tām rakṣaṇayau tathā tāmrau karavīra utpalau ubhau yasya varṇasya bhūyaḥ tvāt kṣīre śataguṇe sthitaḥ nīla tām tat nayet sarvam mahānīlaḥ saḥ ucyate iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe indranīlaparīkṣaṇam nāma dvisaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca vaidūrya puṣparāgāṇām karkete bhīṣmake vade parīkṣām brahmaṇā proktām vyāsena kathitām dvijā kalpa anta kāla kṣubita amburāśeḥ nirhrāda kalpāt ditijasya nādāt tasya nāda samuttha tvāt ākaraḥ su mahā guṇaḥ abhūt uttarītaḥ loke loka traya vibhūṣaṇaḥ tasya eva dānava pateḥ ninada anurūpāḥ pravṛṣ payoda vara darśita cāru rūpāḥ padmarāgam upādāya maṇi varṇāḥ hi ye kṣitau sarvān tān varṇa śobhābhiḥ vaidūryam anugacchati teṣām pradhānam śikhikaṇṭha nīlam yat vā bhavet veṇu dala prakāśam cāṣa agra pakṣa pratima śriyaḥ ye na te praśastāḥ maṇi śāstra vidbhiḥ guṇavān vaidūrya maṇiḥ yojayati svāminam paraṃbhāgyaiḥ doṣaiḥ yuktaḥ doṣaiḥ tasmāt yatnāt parīkṣeta giri kāca śiśupālau kāca sphaṭikāḥ ca dhūma nirbhinnāḥ vaidūrya maṇeḥ ete vijātayaḥ sannibhāḥ santi likhya abhāvāt kācam laghu bhāvāt śaisupālakam vidyāt jātyasya sarve api maṇeḥ tu yādṛś vijātayaḥ santi samāna varṇāḥ tathā api nānā karaṇa anumeya bheda prakāraḥ paramaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ sukha upalakṣyaḥ ca sadā vicāryaḥ hi ayam prabhedaḥ viduṣā nareṇa kuśala akuśalaiḥ prapūryamāṇāḥ pratibaddhāḥ prati satkriyā prayogaiḥ kramaśas samatīta vartamānāḥ pratibaddhāḥ maṇibandhakena yatnāt yadi nāma bhavanti doṣa hīnāḥ maṇayaḥ ṣaḍguṇam āpnuvanti mūlyam ākarān samatītānām udadheḥ tīra sannidhau mūlyam etat maṇīnām tu na sarvatra mahī tale suvarṇaḥ manunā yaḥ tu proktaḥ ṣoḍaśa māṣakaḥ tasya saptatimaḥ bhāgaḥ saṃjñā rūpam kariṣyati śāṇaḥ catur māṣa mānaḥ māṣakaḥ pañca kṛṣṇalaḥ palasya daśamaḥ bhāgaḥ dharaṇaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ittham maṇi vidhiḥ proktaḥ ratnānām mūlya niścaye iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe vaidūryaparīkṣaṇam nāma trisaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca prādurbhavanti tābhyaḥ tu mahā guṇāḥ āpīta pāṇḍu ruciraḥ pāṣāṇaḥ padmarāga saṃjñaḥ tu kaukaṇṭaka nāmā syāt saḥ eva yadi lohita āpītaḥ ālohitaḥ tu pītaḥ su acchaḥ kāṣāyakaḥ saḥ eka uktaḥ ānīla śukla varṇaḥ snigdhaḥ sa guṇaḥ api ca indranīla saṃjñaḥ saḥ eva kathitaḥ su nīlaḥ san mūlyam vaidūrya maṇeḥ iva gāditam hi asya ratna sāra vidā dhāraṇa phalam ca tadvat kim tu strīṇām suta pradaḥ bhavati iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe puṣparāgaparīkṣaṇam nāma catuḥsaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca vāyuḥ nakhān daitya pateḥ gṛhītvā cikṣepa sat padma vaneṣu hṛṣṭaḥ tatas prasūtam pavana upapannam karketanam pūjayatamam pṛthivyām nīlam punar khalu sitam paruṣam vibhinnam vyādhi ādi doṣa karaṇena ca tat vibhāti snigdhāḥ viśuddhāḥ sama rāgiṇaḥ ca āpīta varṇāḥ guravaḥ vicitrāḥ trāsa vraṇa vyāla vivarjitāḥ ca karketanāḥ te paramam pavitrāḥ patreṇa kāñcana mayena tu veṣṭayitvā taptam yadā hutavahe bhavati prakāśam roga praṇāśana karam kali nāśanam tat āyuṣkaram kula karam ca sukha pradam ca evaṃvidham bahu guṇam maṇim āvahanti karketanam śubha alaṅkṛtaye narāḥ ye eke apanahya vikṛta ākula nīla bhāsaḥ pramlāna rāga lulitāḥ kaluṣāḥ virūpāḥ tejaḥ ati dīpti kula puṣṭi vihīna varṇāḥ karketanasya sadṛśam vapuḥ udvahanti iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe karketanaparīkṣaṇam nāma pañcasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca saṃprāptam uttamānām ākaratām bhīṣma ratnānām śuklāḥ śaṅkha abja nibhāḥ syonāka sannibhā prabhāvantaḥ prabhavanti tatas taruṇāḥ vajra nibhāḥ bhīṣma pāṣāṇāḥ bhīṣma maṇim grīvā ādiṣu su sampadam sa sarvadā labhate nirīkṣya palāyante yam tam araṇya nivāsinaḥ samīpa api dvīpi vṛka śarabha kuñjara siṃha vyāghra ādayaḥ hiṃstrāḥ bhīṣma maṇiḥ guṇa yuktaḥ samyak prāpta aṅgulī kalatra tvaḥ pitṝ tarpaṇe pitṝṇām tṛptiḥ bahu vārṣikī bhavati śāmyanti adbhutāni api sarpa aṇḍaja ākhu vṛścika viṣāṇi śaivala balāhaka ābham puruṣam pīta prabham prabhā hīnam malina dyuti ca vivarṇam dūrāt parivarjayet prājñaḥ mūlyam prakalpyam eṣām vibudha varaiḥ daiśa kāla vijñānāt dūre bhūtānām bahu kiñcid nikaṭa prasūtānām iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe vaidūryaparīkṣaṇam nāma ṣaṭsaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca saṃsthāpitāḥ sva nakha bāhu gateḥ prakāśam saṃpūjya dānava patim prathite pradeśe guñjā añjana kṣaudra mṛṇāla varṇāḥ gandharva vahni kadalī sadṛśa avabhāsāḥ ete praśastāḥ pulakāḥ prasūtāḥ śaṅkha abja bhṛṅga arka vicitra bhaṅgā paramāḥ pavitrāḥ kāka aśva rāsabha sṛgāla vṛka ugra rūpaiḥ gṛdhraiḥ sa māṃsa rudhira ārdra mukhaiḥ upetāḥ mṛtyu pradāḥ ca viduṣā parivarjanīyāḥ mūlyam palasya kathitam ca śatāni pañca iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe pulakaparīkṣaṇam nāma saptasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca narmadāyām nicikṣepa kiñcid hīna ādi bhūmiṣu tatra indragopa kalitam śuka vakra varṇam saṃsthānataḥ prakaṭa pīlu samāna mātram madhya indu pāṇḍuram atīva viśuddha varṇam tat ca indranīla sadṛśam paṭalam tule syāt iti śrā gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe rudhirākṣaratnaparīkṣaṇam nāma aṣṭasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca ākāśa śuddham taila ākhyam utpannam sphaṭikam tatas mṛṇāla śaṅkha dhavalam kiñcid varṇa antar anvitam na ttulyam hi ratnānām athavā pāpa nāśanam saṃskṛtam śilpinā sadyas mūlyam kiñcid labhet tatas iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe sphaṭikaparīkṣaṇam nāma ekonāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam sūtaḥ uvāca ādāya śeṣaḥ tasya antram balasya cikṣepa tatra jāyante vidrumāḥ tatra pradhānam śaśa lohita ābham guñjā japā puṣpa nibham pradiṣṭam su nīlakam devaka romakam ca sthānāni teṣu prabhavam su rāgam anyatra jātam ca na tat pradhānam mūlyam bhavet śilpi viśeṣa yogāt dhana dhānya karam loke viṣa ārti bhaya nāśanam parīkṣā pulakasya uktā rudhirākṣasya vai maṇeḥ iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe vidrumaparīkṣaṇam nāma aśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam iti ratnamuktā ādi parīkṣā samāptā sūtaḥ uvāca sarva tīrthāni vakṣyāmi gaṅgā tīrtha uttama uttamā sarvatra sulabhā gaṅgā triṣu sthāneṣu durlabhā gaṅgādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgara saṅgame prayāgam paramam tīrtham mṛtānām bhukti mukti dam sevanāt kṛta piṇḍānām pāpa jit kāma dam nṛṇām vārāṇasī param tīrtham viśveśaḥ yatra keśavaḥ kurukṣetram param tīrtham dāna ādyaiḥ bhukti mukti dam prabhāsam param tīrtham somanāthaḥ hi tatra ca dvārakā ca purī ramyā bhukti mukti pradāyikā prācī sarasvatī puṇyā saptasārasvatam param kedāram sarva pāpa ghnam sa mbhalagrāmaḥ uttamaḥ naranarāyaṇam tīrtham muktyai vadarikāśramaḥ śvetadvīpam purī māyā naimiṣam puṣkaram param ayodhyā ca arghyatīrtham tu citrakūṭam ca gomatī vaināyakam mahī tīrtham rāmagiri āśramam param kāñcī purī tuṅgabhadrā śrīśailam setubandhanam rāmeśvaram param tīrtham kārtikeyam tathā uttamam bhṛgutuṅgam kāmatīrtham tīrtham ca amarakaṇṭakam ujjayinyām mahākālaḥ kubjake śrīdharaḥ hariḥ kubjāmrakam mahā tīrtham kālasarpiḥ ca kāma dam mahā keśī ca kāverī candrabhāgā vipāśayā ekāmram ca tathā tīrtham brahmeśam devakoṭakam mathurā ca purī ramyā śoṇaḥ ca eva mahā nadaḥ jambūsaraḥ mahā tīrtham tāni tīrthāni viddhi ca sūryaḥ śivaḥ gaṇaḥ devī hariḥ yatra ca tiṣṭhati eteṣu ca yathā anyeṣu snānam dānam japaḥ tapaḥ pūjā śrāddham piṇḍa dānam sarvam bhavati ca akṣayam śālagrāmam sarva dam syāt tīrtham paśupateḥ param kokāmukham ca vārāham bhāṇḍīram svāmi saṃjñakam lo hadaṇḍe mahāviṣṇuḥ mandāre madhusūdanaḥ kāmarūpam mahā tīrtham kāmākhyā yatra tiṣṭhati puṇḍravardhanakam tīrtham kārtikeyaḥ ca yatra ca virajaḥ tu mahā tīrtham tīrtham śrīpuruṣottamam mahendra parvataḥ tīrtham kāverī ca nadī parā godāvarī mahā tīrtham payoṣṇī varadā nadī vindhyaḥ pāpa haram tīrtham narmadā bhedaḥ uttamaḥ gokarṇam paramam tīrtham tīrtham māhiṣmatī purī kālañjaram mahī tīrtham śuklatīrtham anuttamam kṛte śauce mukti dam ca śārṅgadhārī tad antike virajam sarva dam tīrtham svarṇākṣam tīrtham uttamam kṛṣṇaveṇī bhīmarathī gaṇḍakī yā tu irāvatī tīrtham bindusaraḥ puṇyam viṣṇu pāda udakam param damaḥ tīrtham tu paramam bhavaśuddhiḥ param tathā jñāna hrade dhyāna jale rāga dveṣa mala apahe yaḥ snāti mānase tīrthe sa yāti paramām gatim idam tīrtham idam na iti ye narāḥ bheda darśinaḥ teṣām vidhīyate tīrtha gamanam tad phalam ca yat eteṣu snāna dānāni śrāddham piṇḍam atha akṣayam sarvāḥ nadyaḥ sarva śailāḥ tīrtham deva ādi sevitam śrīraṅgam ca hareḥ tīrtham tāpī śreṣṭhā mahānadī saptagodāvaram tīrtham tīrtham koṇagiriḥ param mahā lakṣmīḥ yatra devī praṇītā paramā nadī sahya adrau devadeveśaḥ eka vīraḥ sureśvarī gaṅgādvāre kuśāvarte vindhyake nīlaparvate sū uvāca etāni anyāni tīrthāni snāna ādyaiḥ sarva dāni hi śrutvā abravīt hareḥ brahmā vyāsam dakṣa ādi saṃyutam gayā ākhyam prāha sarveṣām akṣayam brahma loka dam iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe sarvatīrtha māhātmyam nāma ekāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam śrī gaṇeśāya namaḥ atha gayāmāhātmyam prārabhyate sārāt sārataram vyāsa gayābhāhātmya muttamam pravakṣyāmi samāsena bukti mukti pradam śṛṇu gaya asuraḥ abhavat pūrvam vīryavān paramaḥ sa ca tad tapaḥ tāpitāḥ devāḥ tad vadha artham harim gatāḥ śaraṇam hariḥ ūce tān bhavitavyam kadācid śiva pūjā artham kṣīrābdheḥ kamalāni ca ānīya kīkaṭe deśe śayanam ca akarot valī viṣṇu māyā vimūḍhaḥ asau gadayā viṣṇunā hataḥ atas gadādharaḥ viṣṇuḥ gayāyām mukti daḥ sthitaḥ tasya dehaḥ liṅga rūpī sthitaḥ śuddhe pitāmahaḥ janārdanaḥ ca kāla īśaḥ tathā anyaḥ prapitāmahaḥ viṣṇuḥ āha atha maryādām puṇya kṣetram bhaviṣyati yajñam śrāddham piṇḍa dānam snāna ādi kurute naraḥ gayā tīrtham param jñātvā yāgam cakre pitāmahaḥ brāhmaṇān pūjayāmāsa ṛtvij artham upāgatān mahānadīm rasa vahām sṛṣṭvā vā api ādikam tathā bhakṣya bhojya phala ādīn ca kāmadhenum tathā sṛjat pañcakrośam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dadau prabhuḥ sthitāḥ viprāḥ tadā śaptāḥ gayāyām brāhmaṇāḥ tatas mā bhūt traipuruṣī vidyā mā bhūt traipuruṣam dhanam yuṣmākam syāt vāri vahā nadī pāṣāṇa parvataḥ śaptaiḥ tu prārthitaḥ brahmā anugraham kṛtavān prabhuḥ lokāḥ puṇyāḥ gayāyām hi śrāddhinaḥ brahma loka gāḥ yuṣmān ye pūjayiṣyanti taiḥ aham pūjitaḥ sadā brahma jñānam gayā śrāddham go gṛhe maraṇam tathā vāsaḥ puṃsām kurukṣetre muktiḥ eṣā caturvidhā samudrāḥ saritaḥ sarvāḥ vāpī kūpa hradāḥ tathā snātu kāmāḥ gayā tīrtham vyāsa yānti na saṃśayaḥ brahmahatyā surā pānam steyam guru aṅganā āgamaḥ pāpam tad saṃga jam sarvam gayā śrāddhāt vinaśyati ca paśu cora hatāḥ ca ye sarpa daṣṭāḥ gayā śrāddhāt muktāḥ svargam vrajanti te gayāyām piṇḍa dānena yat phalam labhate naraḥ na tat śakyam mayā vaktum varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe gayāmāhātmyam nāma dvyaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam kīkaṭeṣu gayā puṇyā puṇyam rājagṛham vanam viṣayaḥ cāraṇaḥ puṇyaḥ nadīnām ca punar muṇḍapṛṣṭham tu pūrvasmin paścime dakṣiṇa uttare sārdha krośa dvayam mānam gayāyām parikīrtitam pañcakrośam gayā kṣetram krośam ekam gayāśiraḥ tatra piṇḍa pradānena tṛptiḥ bhavati śāśvatī nagāt janārdanāt ca eva kūpāt ca uttaramānasāt tatra piṇḍa pradānena pitṝṇām paramā gatiḥ gayā gamana mātreṇa pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet gayāyām pitṛ rūpeṇa devadevaḥ janārdanaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā puṇḍarīkākṣam mucyate vai ṛṇa trayāt ratha mārgam gaya tīrthe dṛṣṭvā rudrapada ādike kāleśvaram ca kedāram pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet dṛṣṭvā pitāmaham devam sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate lokam tu anāmayam yāti dṛṣṭvā ca prapitāmaham tathā gadādharam devam mādhavam puruṣottamam mauna ādityam mahātmānam kanaka arkam viśeṣataḥ dṛṣṭvā maunena viprarṣe pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet brahmāṇam pūjayitvā ca brahma lokam avāpnuyāt gāyattrīm pratas utthāya yaḥ tu paśyati mānavaḥ sāvitrīm ca eva madhyāhne dṛṣṭvā yajña phalam labhet sarasvatīm ca sāyāhne dṛṣṭvā dāna phalam labhet naga stham īśvaram dṛṣṭvā pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet dharmāraṇyam dharmam īśam dṛṣṭvā syāt ṛṇa nāśanam devam gṛdhreśvaram dṛṣṭvā kaḥ na mucyeta bandhanāt dhenum dṛṣṭvā dhenu vane brahma lokam nayet pitṝn prabhāseśam prabhāse ca dṛṣṭvā yāti parām gatim koṭīśvaram ca aśvamedham dṛṣṭvā syāt ṛṇa nāśanam svargadvāra īśvaram dṛṣṭvā mucyate bhava bandhanāt rāmeśvaram gadālolam dṛṣṭvā svargam avāpnuyāt brahmeśvaram tathā dṛṣṭvā mucyate brahma hatyayā muṇḍapṛṣṭhe mahācaṇḍīm dṛṣṭvā kāmān avāpnuyāt phalgvīśam phalgucaṇḍīm ca gaurīm dṛṣṭvā ca maṅgalām gomakam gopatim devam pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet aṅgāreśam ca siddheśam gayādityam gajam tathā mārkaṇḍeyeśvaram dṛṣṭvā pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet phalgutīrthe naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā devam gadādharam etena kim na paryāptam nṝṇām sukṛta kāriṇām brahma lokam prayānti iha puruṣāḥ ekaviṃśatiḥ pṛthivyām yāni tīrthānī ye samudrāḥ sarāṃsi ca pṛthivyām ca gayā puṇyā gayāyām ca gayāśiraḥ śreṣṭham tathā phalgutīrtham tat mukham ca surasya hi udīci kanakānadyaḥ nābhitīrtham tu madhyatas kūpe piṇḍa ādikam kṛtvā pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ tathā akṣayavaṭe śrāddhī brahma lokam nayet pitṝn haṃsatīrthe naraḥ snātvā sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate gayālole vaitaraṇyām ca gomake brahma lokam nayet śrāddhī puruṣān ekaviṃśatim śrāddhī rāmahrade brahma lokam pitṛ kulam nayet uttare mānase śrāddhī na bhūyas jāyate naraḥ dakṣiṇe mānase śrāddhī brahma lokam pitṝn nayet svagadvāre naraḥ śrāddhī brahma lokam nayet pitṝn bhīṣma tarpaṇa kṛttasya kūṭe tārayate pitṝn gṛdhreśvare tathā śrāddhī pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet śrāddhī ca dhenukāraṇye brihma lokam pitṝn nayet tiladhenu pradaḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā dhenum na saṃśayaḥ aindre vā naratīrthe ca vāsave vaiṣṇave tathā mahānadyām kṛta śrāddhaḥ brahma lokam nayet pitṝn snāna sa ndhyā tarpaṇa kṛt śrāddhī ca eka uttaram śatam pitṝṇām tu kulam brahma lokam nayati mānavaḥ tarpayitvā pitṝn devān na viśet yoni saṅkaṭe tarpaṇe kākajaṅghā āryā pitṝṇām tṛptiḥ akṣayā dharmāraṇye mataṅgasya vāpyām śrāddhāt divam vrajet dharmayūpe ca kūpe pitṝṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet pramāṇam devatāḥ santu lokapālāḥ ca sākṣiṇaḥ mayā āgatya mataṅge asmin pitṝṇām niṣkṛtiḥ kṛtā rāmatīrthe narāḥ snātvā śrāddham kṛtvā prabhāsake śilāyām preta bhāvāt syuḥ muktāḥ pitṛ gaṇāḥ kila sva puṣṭāyām tris saphta kuṃlam uddharet śrāddha kṛt muṇḍapṛṣṭha ādau brahma lokam nayet pitṝn gayāyām na hi tat sthānam yatra tīrtham na vidyate pañcakrośe gayā kṣetre yatra tatra tu piṇḍa daḥ janārdanasya haste tu piṇḍam dadyāt svakam naraḥ para lokam gate mokṣam akṣayyam upatiṣṭhatām gayāyām dharmapṛṣṭhe ca sarasi brahmaṇaḥ tathā gayāśīrṣe akṣayavaṭe pitṝṇām dattam akṣayam dharmāraṇyam dharmapṛṣṭham dhenukāraṇyam eva ca dṛṣṭvā etāni pitṝn ca ārya vaṃśyān viṃśatim uddharet brahmāraṇyam mahānadyāḥ paścimaḥ bhāgaḥ ucyate pūrvaḥ brahmasadaḥ bhāgaḥ nāga adriḥ bharatāśramaḥ gayāśīrṣāt dakṣiṇatas mahānadyāḥ ca paścime tat smṛtam campakavanam tatra pāṇḍu śilā asti hi śrāddhī tatra tṛtīyāyām niścirāyāḥ ca maṇḍale mahāhrade ca kauśikyām akṣayam phalam āpnuyāt vaitaraṇyāḥ ca uttaratas tṛtīya ākhyaḥ jalāśayaḥ padāni tatra krauñcasya śrāddhī svargam nayet pitṝn krauñcapādāt uttaratas niścirā ākhyaḥ jalāśayaḥ sakṛt yatra abhigamanam sakṛt piṃṇḍa prapātanam mahānadyām upaspṛśya tarpayet pitṛ devatāḥ akṣayān prāpnuyāt lokān kulam ca api samuddharet sāvitre paṭhyate sandhyā kṛtā syāt dvādaśa ābdikī śukla kṛṣṇau ubhau pakṣau gayāyām yaḥ vaset naraḥ punāti āsaptamam ca eva kulam na asti atra saṃśayaḥ gayāyām muṇāḍapṛṣṭham ca aravindam ca parvatam tṛtīyam kraiñcapādam ca dṛṣṭvā pāpaiḥ pramucyate durlabham triṣu lokeṣu gayāyām piṇḍapātanam mahāhrade ca kauśikyām mūla kṣetre viśeṣataḥ guhāyām gṛdhrakūṭasya śrāddham dattam mahā phalam yatra māheśvarī dhārā śrāddhī tatra anṛṇaḥ bhavet puṇyām viśālām āsādya nadīm trailokya viśrutām agniṣṭomam avāpnoti śrāddhī prāyāt divam naraḥ śrāddhī māsapade snātvā vājapeya phalam labhet ravi pāde piṇḍa dānāt patita uddhāraṇam bhavet kāṅkṣante pitaraḥ putrān narakāt bhaya bhīravaḥ gayām yāsyati yaḥ kaścid saḥ asmān santarayiṣyati gayā prāptam sutam dṛṣṭvā pitṝṇām utsavaḥ bhavet pabhdyām api jalam spṛṣṭvā asmabhyam kila dāsyati ātmajaḥ vā tathā anyaḥ vā gayākūpe yadā tadā yad nāmnā pātayet piṇḍam tam nayet brahma śāśvatam puṇḍarīkam viṣṇu lokam prāpnuyāt koṭitīrtha gaḥ yā sā vaitaraṇī nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā sā avatīrṇā gayā kṣetre pitṝṇām tāraṇāya hi śrāddha daḥ piṇḍa daḥ tatra go pradānam karoti yaḥ ekaviṃśati vaṃśyān sa tārayet na atra saṃśayaḥ teṣām brahmasadaḥ sthānam somapānam tathā eva ca pūjitaiḥ pūjitāḥ sarve pitṛbhiḥ saha devatāḥ sthānam deha parityāge gayāyām tu vidhīyate yaḥ karoti vṛṣotsargam gayā kṣetre hi anuttame agniṣṭoma śatam puṇyam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ ātmanaḥ api mahā buddhiḥ gayāyām tu tilaiḥ vinā piṇḍa nirvāpaṇam kuryāt anyeṣām api mānavaḥ yāvantaḥ jñātayaḥ pitryāḥ bāndhavāḥ suhṛdaḥ tathā tebhyaḥ vyāsa gayā bhūmau piṇḍaḥ deyaḥ vidhānataḥ rāmatīrthe naraḥ snātvā go śatasya āpnuyāt phalam mataṅga vāpyām snātvā ca go sahasra phalam labhet niścirā saṃgame snātvā brahma lokam nayet pitṝn vasiṣṭhasya āśrame snātvā vājapeyam ca vindati mahākauśyām samāvāsāt aśvamedha phalam labhet pitāmahasya sarasaḥ prasṛtā loka pāvanī samīpe tu agnidhārā iti viśrutā kapilā hi sā agniṣṭoma phalam śrāddhī snātvā atra kṛtakṛtya tā śrāddhī kumāradhārāyām aśvamedha phalam labhet somakuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā soma lokam ca gacchati saṃvartasya naraḥ vāpyām subhagaḥ syāt tu piṇḍa daḥ dhauta pāpaḥ naraḥ yāti pretakuṇḍe ca piṇḍa daḥ evamādiṣu tīrtheṣu piṇḍa daḥ tārayet pitṝn natvā devān vasiṣṭha īśa prabhṛtīn ṛṇa saṃkṣayam iti śrī gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrva khaṇḍe prathama aṃśa ākhye ācāra kāṇḍe gayāmāhātmyam nāma tryaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī garuḍa mahāpurāṇam udyataḥ tu gayām gantum śrāddham kṛtvā vidhānataḥ vidhāya kārpaṭī viṣam grāmasya api pradakṣiṇam tatas grāma antaram gatvā śrāddha śeṣasya bhojanam gṛhāt calita mātrasya gayāyām gamanam prati svarga ārohaṇa sopānam pitṝṇām tu pade pade muṇḍanam ca upavāsaḥ ca sarva tīrtheṣu ayam vidhiḥ varjayitvā kurukṣetram viśālām virajām gayām divā ca sarvadā rātrau gayāyām śrāddha kṛt bhavet vārāṇasyām kṛtam śrāddham tīrthe śoṇanade tathā punar śrāddhī svargam pitṝn nayet uttaram mānasam gatvā siddhim prāpnoti anuttamām kāmān sa labhate divyān mokṣa upāyam ca sarvaśas dakṣiṇam mānasam gatvā maunī piṇḍa ādi kārayet ṛṇa traya apākaraṇam labhet dakṣiṇamānase siddhānām prīti jananaiḥ pāpānām ca bhayaṅkaraiḥ nāmnā kanakhalam tīrtham triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam udīcyām muṇḍapṛṣṭhasya deva ṛṣi gaṇa sevitam tatra snātvā divam yāti śrāddham dattam atha akṣayam sūryam natvā tu idam kuryāt kṛta piṇḍa ādi satkriyaḥ kavyavāhaḥ tathā somaḥ yamaḥ ca eva aryamā tathā agniṣvāttāḥ barhiṣadaḥ somapāḥ pidṛ devatāḥ āgacchantu mahābhāgāḥ yuṣamābhiḥ rakṣitāḥ tu iha madīyāḥ pitaraḥ ye ca kule jātāḥ sanābhayaḥ teṣām piṇḍa pradāna artham āgataḥ asmi gayām imām kṛta piṇḍaḥ phalgutīrthe paśyait devam pitāmaham gadādharam tatas paśyet pitṝṇām anṛṇām anṛṇaḥ bhavet phalgutīrthe naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā devam gadādharam ātmānam tārayet sadyas daśa pūrvān daśa aparān dharmāraṇyam mataṅgasya vāpyām piṇḍa ādi kṛt bhavet dharmāraṇyam samāsādya vājapeya phalam labhet rājasūya aśvamedhābhyām phalam syāt brahmatīrthake śrāddham piṇḍa udakam kāryam madhye vai kūpa yūpayoḥ kūpa udakena tat kāryam pitṝṇām dattam akṣayam kṛtvā śrāddha ādikam piṇḍam madhye vai yūpa kūpayoḥ go pracāra samīpa sthāḥ ābrahma brahma kalpitāḥ teṣā sevana mātreṇa pitaraḥ mokṣa gāminaḥ yūpam pradakṣiṇīkṛtya vājapeya phalam labhet kṛtvā śrāddham gayāśīrṣe kuryāt rudra pada ādiṣu piṇāḍa andehi mukhe vyāse pañca agnau ca pada traye sūrya indu kārtikeyeṣu kṛtam śrāddham tathā akṣayam śrāddham tu nava devatyam kuryāt dvādaśa daivatam anvaṣṭakāsu vṛddhau ca gayāyām mṛta vāsare atra mātuḥ pṛthak śrāddham anyatra patinā saha snātvā daśāśvamedhe tu dṛṣṭvā devam pitāmaham rudrapādam naraḥ spṛṣṭvā na ca iha āvartate punar tris vitta pūrṇām pṛthivīm dattvā yat phalam āpnuyāt sa tat phalam avāpnoti kṛtvā śrāddham gayāśire śamī patra pramāṇena piṇḍam dadyāt gayāśire pitaraḥ yānti deva tvam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā muṇḍapṛṣṭe padam nyastam mahādevena dhīmatā gayāśīrṣe tu yaḥ piṇḍān nāmnā yeṣām tu nirvapet naraka sthāḥ divam yānti svarga sthāḥ mokṣam āpnuyuḥ pañcame ahni gandālole snātvā vaṭa tale tatas piṇḍān dadyāt pitṝṇām ca sakalam tārayet kulam vaṭa mūlam samāsādya śākena uṣṇa udakena vā kṛte śrāddhe akṣayavaṭe dṛṣṭvā ca prapitāmaham eṣṭavyāḥ bahavaḥ puttrāḥ yadi ekaḥ api gayām vrajet yajeta vā aśvamedhena nīlam vā vṛṣam utsṛjet pretaḥ kaścid samuddiśya vaṇijam kañcid abravīt mama nāmnā gayāśīrṣe piṇḍa nirvapaṇam kuru śrutvā vaṇij gayāśīrṣa preta rājāya piṇḍakam sarve muktāḥ viśālaḥ api sa putraḥ abhut ca piṇḍadaḥ viśālāyām viśālaḥ abhūt rāja putraḥ bravīt dvijān katham putra ādayaḥ syuḥ me viprāḥ ca uturviśālakam gayāyām piṇḍa dānena tava sarvam bhaviṣyati viśālaḥ atha gayāśīrṣa piṇḍadaḥ abhūt ca putravān dṛṣṭvā ākāśe sitam raktam kṛṣṇam puruṣam abravīt ke yūyam teṣu ca eva ekaḥ sitaḥ proce viśālakam ayam pitāmahaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ
